# Wiki Index

The catalog of all pages in this wiki. Each entry: a wikilink to the page and a one-line summary. The LLM reads this first when answering queries to identify candidate pages.

Keep summaries tight вҖ” one line each. The index is engineered to be cheap to read; a fat index defeats its purpose.

When this file exceeds ~300 lines or the wiki passes ~150 pages, shard into `wiki/indexes/<type>.md` and replace this file with a directory of shards. See the `scaling-playbook.md` reference in the `llm-wiki` skill for the migration procedure.

---

## Sources

- [[readme]] вҖ” the project's front-page `README.md`: what Seqeron is, its three entry points, and headline facts.
- [[algorithms-checklist-v2]] вҖ” the test-unit validation registry: 364 units (255 done / 109 proposed), DoD, evidence, coverage.
- [[advanced-testing-checklist]] вҖ” 2026-03-19 effectiveness/gap analysis rating the ten testing techniques by applicability, coverage, effort, and P0вҖ“P3 priority.
- [[mcp-methods-audit]] вҖ” a 2026-01-23 census of the C# API surface: 277 public static methods across 54 classes, with counting rules and the tool-count caveat.
- [[mcp-checklist]] вҖ” the SUPERSEDED (2026-07-01) MCP build tracker: a 12-server/241-tool plan never built; DoD gates, error-code catalog, two-tests-per-tool. Live status now in `docs/mcp/MCP_STATUS.md`.
- [[mcp-plan]] вҖ” the SUPERSEDED (2026-07-01) MCP design doc (sibling of the checklist): v3вҶ’v4 rationale, full 241-tool inventory across 12 servers, and the still-valid standards (naming, JSON-Schema 2020-12, error ranges, SemVer, 2-tests-per-tool, doc contract).
- [[mcp-prompt]] вҖ” the CURRENT one-tool-per-session MCP-completion subagent prompt: names the real 11 servers (serverвҶ’projectвҶ’file), the 3-part tool DoD (binding+tests+docs), and reverses the old no-business-asserts test policy. Ground truth: `docs/mcp/MCP_STATUS.md`.
- [[mcp-readme]] вҖ” the MCP front-door guide (`docs/mcp/README.md`): why MCP (real computation, structured I/O, local/auditable), the current 427-tools/11-servers table, stdio/Codex connection, and two worked tool-only workflows; supersedes the mcp-plan/mcp-checklist tool counts.
- [[skills-strategy]] вҖ” the Claude Code skills plan of record (`docs/skills/STRATEGY.md`): many independent dual-mode skills over the source of truth, point-don't-duplicate, the generated-catalog anti-drift mechanism, and the (complete) phase plan.
- [[golden-skills-regression]] вҖ” the golden skills regression set (`docs/skills/golden/README.md`): 12 hard dual-mode tasks with expected routing/pipeline/rigor/shape as a manual eval aid; the Phase-3 acceptance instrument for the skills strategy.

- [[validation-ledger]] вҖ” the live per-unit validation status board (VALIDATION_LEDGER.md): Stage A / Stage B pass-fail matrix across three phases (86 implemented + 24 new campaign units, 148 Phase-2, 12 enhanced), refreshed by reset banners after code churn; ground truth for *where things stand*, superseding the findings-register snapshot.
- [[validation-protocol]] вҖ” the validation *methodology* (VALIDATION_PROTOCOL.md): one fresh session per unit in a context separate from the implementer's, Stage A (validate the description vs external primary sources) before Stage B (validate the code), ending in exactly one of вң… CLEAN / рҹ”§ LIMITED; the per-session prompt, checklists, verdict legend, and report template the ledger operationalizes.

- [[assembly-trim-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit ASSEMBLY-TRIM-001 (quality trimming, BWA/cutadapt running-sum): cutadapt algorithm docs + BWA `bwa_trim_read`/`BWA_MIN_RDLEN` + Cock et al. 2010 sources; subtract-cutoff/argmin-partial-sum = BWA argmax, Phred+33 decode; `KI;<)(,%#$`@thr 10вҶ’first 4 bases oracle; both-end-order + minLength-filter assumptions.
- [[assembly-trim-001-report]] вҖ” validation report for ASSEMBLY-TRIM-001 (quality trimming, `SequenceAssembler.QualityTrimReads`/`TrimEnd`/`TrimStart`; distinct from the evidence artifact [[assembly-trim-001-evidence]]): Stage A вң… PASS / Stage B вқҢ FAIL вҶ’ рҹ”§ FIXED / State CLEAN, full suite 6535/0. **One real defect fully fixed** вҖ” old `TrimEnd`/`TrimStart` took the *global-minimum* partial sum with **no `s < 0` early break** and chained the 5' pass onto the 3'-surviving window; ~19.5% of random reads diverged from cutadapt (`20,0,8,40`@10 kept only the last base vs all 4). Fix adds the `s<0` early break to both passes, runs each independently over the full read `[0,n)`, and adds the `startвүҘstop вҮ’ (0,0)` drop rule; Python port vs cutadapt `quality_trim_index` = **0/900k mismatches**. Three new sourced tests (`5!)I`вҶ’`ACGT`, `##I##`вҶ’`G`, `5&&`вҶ’dropped) each fail the old code. Pre-existing M1вҖ“M5/S1вҖ“S3 were all happy-path and shared the blind spot. Corrected the concept's stale "5'-pass-on-surviving-window" wording. Concept [[quality-trimming-running-sum]].

- [[protmotif-tm-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit PROTMOTIF-TM-001 (Transmembrane helix prediction, Kyte-Doolittle hydropathy sliding window; ProteinMotif family, genuinely distinct hydrophobicity-based unit): slide a window of length **19** along the protein, score each window as the **arithmetic mean** of its per-residue Kyte-Doolittle (1982) hydropathy values, emit contiguous runs with window mean **> threshold 1.6** as membrane-spanning segments. - [[onco-sig-002-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit ONCO-SIG-002 (mutational signature fitting/refitting + de-novo NMF extraction; thirtieth Oncology unit, the downstream partner of ONCO-SIG-001): MutationalPatterns Blokzijl 2018 + deconstructSigs Rosenthal 2016 (rank 3, supervised **NNLS refit** `min_x вҖ–SВ·xвҲ’dвҖ–вӮӮВІ, xвүҘ0`, reconstruction `SВ·x`, cosine-вүҘ0.95 gate, weightsвҶ’proportions) + Lawson-Hanson 1974 (rank 4, active-set NNLS) + iMutSig Pan 2020 (rank 3, cosine) + Lee & Seung 2001 (rank 1, **NMF** multiplicative updates, Frobenius Thm 1 + KL/Poisson Thm 2, monotone non-increase, fixed point at V=WH) + Alexandrov 2013/2020 & COSMIC (rank 1вҖ“2, blind-source-separation W=signatures/H=exposures, L1-normalized 96-channel signatures) + Brunet 2004 (rank 1, consensus/**cophenetic** rank selection) + SigProfilerExtractor Islam 2022 + Rousseeuw 1987 (silhouette stability >0.80, cosine reference matching); oracles cosine (identicalвҶ’1, orthogonalвҶ’0, [1,1]/[1,0]вҶ’1/вҲҡ2, [3,4]/[6,8]вҶ’1) + NNLS (identity d=[3,5]вҶ’[3,5]; clamp-and-refit S=[[1,1],[0,1]], d=[0,1]вҶ’[0,0.5]; zeroвҶ’[0,0]; proportions [3,5]вҶ’[0.375,0.625]) + planted-truth NMF (V=WвӮҖHвӮҖ residualвүҲ0, recovered up to permutation/scaling, columns L1-sum 1) + auto-rank picks kвӮҖ=2 + cophenetic=1 at rank 1; corner cases zero catalogвҶ’zero exposures, cosine zero-normвҶ’0.0, NMF non-convexвҶ’local-minimum (planted+fixed-seed only), permutation/scale ambiguity, Оө-guarded denominators; five assumptions (Frobenius objective, seeded init, exposure proportions, zero-vector cosine 0.0, consensus-clustering/silhouette/greedy-cosine matching), no contradictions. - [[quality-phred-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit QUALITY-PHRED-001 (Phred score handling вҖ” parse/encode a FASTQ quality string + convert Phred+33 вҶ” Phred+64; QUALITY family): **Cock et al. 2010** *Nucleic Acids Research* 38(6):1767 (DOI 10.1093/nar/gkp1137, PMC2847217) вҖ” the de-facto FASTQ spec: Phred `Q=вҲ’10В·logвӮҒвӮҖ(P)`, Sanger/**Phred+33** ASCII 33вҖ“126вҶ’Q0вҖ“93 (`Q=ordвҲ’33`), Illumina 1.3+/**Phred+64** ASCII 64вҖ“126вҶ’Q0вҖ“62, Phred score **invariant** across variants so cross-variant conversion is a pure Вұ31 re-offset (Solexa odds-ratio score out of scope, lossy); representability rules **Phred+64вҶ’Phred+33 always safe** (Q0вҖ“62 вҠҶ 0вҖ“93) vs **Phred+33вҶ’Phred+64 overflows** for Q>62; oracles `!`/`5`/`?`/`I`/`~`вҶ’0/20/30/40/93, `@h~`вҶ’0/40/62, conversion `@h~`вҶ’`!I_` and `!I`вҶ’`@h`; must-test both-variant decode / round-trip identity / both-direction convert / out-of-range decode throws / Q>62 overflow throws / empty+null; two API-shape assumptions (malformed byte + overflow вҶ’ `ArgumentOutOfRangeException`, range bounds source-backed); no contradictions. **No new concept** вҖ” enriches shared [[phred-quality-encoding]] (adds the Cock et al. primary anchor + conversion representability rules) alongside sibling [[parse-fastq-001-evidence]].
- [[quality-stats-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit QUALITY-STATS-001 (FASTQ quality statistics вҖ” Q20/Q30 fractions, mean, median, min/max, population variance/std dev; QUALITY family, sibling of QUALITY-PHRED-001): Illumina *Sequencing Quality Scores* (`% вүҘ Q30` the standard NGS benchmark, **inclusive `вүҘ`** thresholds) + Newcastle Univ. ASK (population variance/Пғ `= (1/N)ОЈ(xбөўвҲ’Ој)ВІ`, **Г·N not NвҲ’1** вҖ” quality string is the complete population) + Math is Fun (median middle element; **even count averages the two central order statistics**) + Wikipedia/Ewing & Green 1998 (Phred `Q=вҲ’10logвӮҒвӮҖP` provenance) + Cock et al. 2010 (Phred+33 `ordвҲ’33` decode, **cited only** вҖ” the decode is QUALITY-PHRED-001's contract, not re-tested); statistics computed over **decoded scores** so **encoding-independent** (Phred+64 same-scores вҶ’ identical stats); mean = arithmetic mean of scores (a mean over log-scaled values, **not** an error-probability-averaged quality); `CalculateQ30Percentage` == `CalculateStatistics(...).PercentAboveQ30`; oracles `5?I`вҶ’20/30/40 mean 30.0 median 30 min/max 20/40 var 200/3вүҲ66.6667 ПғвүҲ8.16497 %вүҘQ20 100.0 %вүҘQ30вүҲ66.667, even `5II?`вҶ’median (30+40)/2=35.0 mean 32.5, single `I`(Q40)вҶ’mean=median=min=max=40 Пғ=0 %вүҘQ20/Q30 100.0; corner cases even/odd median branch, single-element Пғ=0, empty/null вҶ’ zeroed `QualityStatistics` (TotalBases=0); one API-shape assumption (emptyвҶ’zeroed not throw); no contradictions. Own concept [[fastq-quality-statistics]] (**depends on** [[phred-quality-encoding]]).
- [[rep-str-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit REP-STR-001 (Microsatellite / Short Tandem Repeat (STR) detection вҖ” perfect default `FindMicrosatellites` **plus** the opt-in approximate/imperfect/interrupted `FindApproximateTandemRepeats` + `ComputeBernoulliStatistics`, Benson **Tandem Repeats Finder** 1999 model): Benson 1999 *Nucleic Acids Research* 27(2):573 (approximate-repeat definition, seven TRF statistics, wraparound-DP alignment, majority-rule consensus) + TRF definitions/desc pages (Bernoulli adjacent-copy model, PM matching / PI indel probability, defaults PM .80/PI .10) + TRF reference impl (recommended weights `(+2,вҲ’7,вҲ’7)`, Minscore 50) + Wikipedia Microsatellite (1вҖ“6 bp unit, 5вҖ“50 copies) sources; the opt-in approximate detector **closes the exact-copies-only gap** вҖ” reports an interrupted tract as ONE repeat with percent-matches/percent-indels/score while the perfect detector fragments it; oracles `CAGCAGCAGTAGCAGCAG`вҶ’period 3 `CAG`Г—6 17match/1mismatch score 27 94.4%, single-base-deletion 29-bpвҶ’score 51 clears default gate, Bernoulli adjacent PM 13/15 distinct from consensus 17/18, `CACACATACACA`вҶ’PM 0.80 on-threshold; three assumptions (deterministic exhaustive (start,period) scan vs TRF probabilistic k-tuple seeding вҖ” the genome-scale residual; percentage denominator = total alignment columns; adjacent-copy segmentation for Bernoulli PM/PI, exact for substitution-only); no contradictions. **No new concept** вҖ” enriches the repeats family anchor [[repetitive-element-detection]] (Approximate STR detection section).
- [[restr-filter-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit RESTR-FILTER-001 (Restriction Enzyme Filtering вҖ” the first RESTR-* / MolTools reagent-selection unit): filter the enzyme library by end type (`GetBluntCutters()` / `GetStickyCutters()`) and by recognition-site length (`GetEnzymesByCutLength(min, max)` + single-length overload). Sources: Wikipedia *Sticky and blunt ends* (blunt = both strands terminate in a base pair, sticky = 5'/3' overhang, **blunt & sticky are the only two categories вҶ’ total, disjoint partition**, blunt-blunt always compatible) + Wikipedia *Restriction enzyme* (Type II undivided palindromes **4вҖ“8 nt**; center cutвҶ’blunt / staggeredвҶ’sticky; EcoRI `G^AATTC` / SmaI `CCC^GGG` / KpnI `GGTAC^C` / PstI `CTGCA^G` examples) + Wikipedia *List of restriction enzyme cutting sites* (4/6/8-bp categories) + NEB/REBASE (KpnI 3' overhang, EcoRI 5' overhang) + PMC/REBASE (SfiI interrupted palindrome `GGCCNNNN^NGGCC`, 13 nt, outside 4вҖ“8). Dataset oracle: SmaI/EcoRV/AluI/HaeIII blunt vs EcoRI(5')/KpnI(3')/PstI(3')/NotI/TaqI sticky + SfiI 13-nt interrupted. Contract: blunt вҲӘ sticky = full library & disjoint; `[min,max]` **inclusive** (`6вҶ’6` all 6-cutters, `9вҶ’10` none, `[4,8]` whole undivided library **except** 13-nt SfiI); single-length overload agrees at `min==max`; `min>max`/negative/zero вҶ’ empty. One API-shape assumption (inclusive range bounds; recognition-length values source-backed). No contradictions. New concept [[restriction-enzyme-filtering]].
- [[rna-dotbracket-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit RNA-DOTBRACKET-001 (Dot-Bracket / extended WUSS notation вҖ” **parse & validate** a structure string; the notation/representation layer of the RNA secondary-structure family): `RnaSecondaryStructure.ParseDotBracket` (structure string вҶ’ base pairs) + `ValidateDotBracket` (well-formedness). Sources: ViennaRNA *RNA Structure Notations* / *Dot-Bracket Notation* (rank 3 вҖ” base pairs = matching `()`, unpaired = `.`; extended notation adds `<>`/`{}`/`[]` + uppercase/lowercase letter pairs; **families are not required to nest вҶ’ pseudoknots**; uppercase = 5' opener / lowercase = 3' closer) + ViennaRNA WUSS / `vrna_db_from_WUSS()` + Infernal Nawrocki & Eddy 2013 (rank 3 вҖ” **any matched pair = a base pair, symbol has no meaning if partners match**; flatten treats letter-pair pseudoknots as unpaired вҶ’ each family an **independent pairing system**) + Rfam glossary (rank 5 вҖ” `<>`/`()`/`[]`/`{}` all pair; non-bracket `-`/`,`/`:`/`.` all single-stranded). Algorithm: **one balanced-bracket stack per family** (shared stack would mis-pair `([)]`); a closer must match a same-family opener. Oracles вҖ” parse `((((....))))`вҶ’(0,11),(1,10),(2,9),(3,8), `([)]`вҶ’`(`:(0,2)+`[`:(1,3), `<<<<[[[[....>>>>]]]]` / `((((AAAA....))))aaaa`вҶ’two 4-bp crossing helices; validate `(((...)))`/`(([[]]))`/`([)]`вҶ’**true**, `(((...)` / `...)` / `)(` / `(]`вҶ’**false**. Two API-contract assumptions (malformed input вҶ’ best-effort parse dropping unmatched closers, gate with `ValidateDotBracket`; empty/null вҶ’ valid pair-free). No contradictions. New concept [[rna-dot-bracket-notation]].
- [[rna-energy-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit RNA-ENERGY-001 (**Free Energy Calculation**; the thermodynamic/energy layer of the RNA secondary-structure family): `RnaSecondaryStructure.CalculateStackingEnergy`/`CalculateStemEnergy`/`CalculateHairpinLoopEnergy`/`CalculateMinimumFreeEnergy`, the **Turner 2004 nearest-neighbor** free-energy terms summed into a fold's О”GВ° at 37 В°C. Sources: **NNDB (Nearest Neighbor Database) Turner04** (definitive parameter tables вҖ” WC/GU stacking, hairpin `loop.txt`, terminal-mismatch, tri/tetra/hexaloop totals, hairpin bonuses/penalties) + Turner 2004 + Mathews 2004 (PNAS 101:7287) + Xia 1998 + SantaLucia 1998 + Heus & Pardi 1991; reference impls ViennaRNA / MFOLD / RNAstructure. Model `О”GВ°total = init + ОЈstacking + ОЈloops`. Key parameters вҖ” WC stacking **all negative** (GC-rich most stable, `GC/CG` вҲ’3.42, `GG/CC` вҲ’3.26; `AA/UU` вҲ’0.93); **G-U wobble variable, two positive** (`UG/GU` +0.30, `GU/UG` +1.29), note-a `GG/UU`=вҲ’0.5, note-b `5'GGUC/3'CUGG` special 3-stack total вҲ’4.12 (vs вҲ’1.77); **hairpin-loop init positive & non-monotonic** (3вҶ’5.4, 4вҶ’5.6, 6вҶ’5.4, 9вҶ’6.4, Jacobson-Stockmayer beyond 9); special UNCG/GNRA tri/tetra/hexaloop total energies; all-C loop penalty (3-nt +1.5 / >3-nt 0.3n+1.6); terminal mismatch (96); +0.45 per AU/GU end. Oracles GC 3-bp stem вҲ’5.78, NNDB hairpin example-1 `GGGAUAAAUCCC` вҲ’3.42, GGUC/CUGG вҲ’4.12; single base pair / empty / poly-A вҶ’ **О”GВ°=0** (stacking needs вүҘ2 adjacent pairs). No assumptions remain (all params = exact NNDB match); three **defined conditions** (37 В°C, 2-dp precision, unknown stacksвҶ’0.0). No contradictions. New concept [[rna-free-energy-turner-model]].
- [[rna-hairpin-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit RNA-HAIRPIN-001 (**Hairpin Loop and Stem Free-Energy Calculation**, Turner 2004 NN model): a focused deep-dive on `RnaSecondaryStructure.CalculateHairpinLoopEnergy` + `CalculateStemEnergy`, **not** a stem-loop enumerator and **not** miRNA-specific вҖ” it enriches the energy-layer concept [[rna-free-energy-turner-model]] (sibling of [[rna-energy-001-evidence]]) rather than defining a new one; distinct from the miRNA hairpin *finder* [[pre-mirna-hairpin-detection]]. Source: **NNDB Turner 2004** hairpin pages (via Wayback) + **Mathews et al. 2004** PNAS 101:7287. Hairpin О”GВ° = init(n) + terminal mismatch + first-mismatch bonuses (UU/GA вҲ’0.9, GG вҲ’0.8) + special-GU-closure вҲ’2.2 (**G-U only, not U-G** вҖ” documented asymmetry) + all-C penalty (3-nt +1.5, >3-nt 0.3n+1.6); **3-nt loops get no first-mismatch term**; loops < 3 nt prohibited; special tri/tetra/hexaloop totals override the model (`CAACG` 6.8, `CCUCGG` 2.5). Stem = per-stack stacking + **+0.45/AU-end**, P pairs вҶ’ **PвҲ’1 stacks** (P вүӨ 1 вҮ’ 0). Oracles NNDB Example 1 (A-U closing, 6-nt loop AвҖҰA) loop +4.6 + helix вҲ’6.01 = **вҲ’1.4**; Example 2 (5-nt loop GвҖҰG, GG bonus) loop +4.1 + helix вҲ’6.01 = **вҲ’1.9**; all-C 3-nt loop 6.9, 4-nt 7.7. One display-precision item (2-dp intermediate rounding, tests assert `.Within(1e-9)`); no contradictions. **No new concept** вҖ” enriches [[rna-free-energy-turner-model]].
- [[rna-invert-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit RNA-INVERT-001 (RNA inverted repeats / potential stem regions вҖ” antiparallel **reverse-complement arms** that form a stem-loop; RNA secondary-structure family, `RnaSecondaryStructure`): IUPACpal (Alamro 2021, PMC7866733) `W G WМ„бҙҝ` gapped model + *k*-Hamming mismatch (perfect = k=0) + Watson-Crick RNA complement (Aвҹ·U, Cвҹ·G) + Wikipedia/Ussery 2008 (`5'---TTACGnnnnnnCGTAA---3'`, zero-gap вҮ’ palindrome) + EMBOSS `einverted` (inverted repeat = stem-loop = local alignment of a sequence vs its reverse complement) sources; oracles `UUACGAAAAAACGUAA` (arm `UUACG` 0вҖ“4 / loop 5вҖ“10 / arm `CGUAA` 11вҖ“15) and palindromic `GGCCAAAGGCC` (left 0вҖ“3 / right 7вҖ“10 / len 4); MUST antiparallel-not-parallel + no-IRвҶ’empty; scope restriction = **perfect ungapped `k=0`** arms only (einverted scored mismatch/gap DP Not Implemented), loop bounds via minSpacing/maxSpacing, maximal-arm non-overlapping greedy reporting; no contradictions. **No new concept** вҖ” reuses [[repetitive-element-detection]] (same IUPACpal IR model) + [[rna-base-pairing]] (antiparallel RNA complement) + [[pre-mirna-hairpin-detection]]/[[rna-dot-bracket-notation]] (stem-loop framing).
- [[rna-mfe-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit RNA-MFE-001 (**Minimum Free Energy (MFE) RNA secondary-structure prediction** вҖ” the ZukerвҖ“Stiegler dynamic-programming folder; the folding/search layer of the RNA secondary-structure family, `RnaSecondaryStructure.CalculateMinimumFreeEnergy` / `PredictStructure`). Sources: **Zuker & Stiegler 1981** *NAR* 9(1):133 (rank 1 вҖ” original MFE DP, loop decomposition hairpin/stacking/bulge-interior/multibranch, polynomial) + **Lorenz 2011** ViennaRNA 2.0 (rank 3 вҖ” MFE fold "derived from the ZukerвҖ“Stiegler decomposition", **O(nВі)**) + **Ward 2017** *NAR* 45(14):8541 (rank 1 вҖ” C(i,j)=min(hairpin, interior/bulge, multiloop) + multiloop M/M1 + exterior F matrices, **standard affine multiloop вҶ’ O(nВі) time / O(nВІ) space**, "simplest model is best") + **NNDB Turner 2004** worked examples + **Mathews 2004** PNAS 101:7287. The unit that **consumes** the [[rna-free-energy-turner-model]] Turner terms and **produces** a [[rna-dot-bracket-notation]] structure. Oracles `CalculateMinimumFreeEnergy("CACAAAAAAAUGUG")`=вҲ’1.41 (NNDB Example 1, structure `((((......))))`), `CACAGAAAGUGUG`=вҲ’1.91 (Example 2, GG first mismatch). Invariants INV-01 MFE вүӨ 0, INV-02 suffix-monotone `MFE(s) вүӨ MFE(prefix)`, INV-03 optimized DP == classic O(nВі) baseline; empty/null / homopolymer `AAAAAAAA` / sequence `< minLoopSize+2` (`GCGC`) вҶ’ 0 (min hairpin loop 3 nt); intramolecular вҮ’ no helix-init constant. Two documented simplifications (multiloop per-unpaired `c=0` with `a=9.25`/helix `c=вҲ’0.63`; 2-dp rounding, tests `.Within(1e-9)` + `Round(mfe,1)`==NNDB), no source contradictions. **New concept** [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding]]; the folder the [[pre-mirna-hairpin-detection]] `AssessHairpinByMfe` path (prior pages' generic *RNA-STRUCT-001*) uses.
- [[rna-pair-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit RNA-PAIR-001 (**RNA Base Pairing** вҖ” the RNA-secondary-structure family's own base-pairing primitive): `RnaSecondaryStructure.CanPair` / `GetBasePairType` (typed `WatsonCrick`/`Wobble`/`null` classifier) / `GetComplement`. Sources: **Crick 1966** *J Mol Biol* 19:548 (wobble hypothesis вҖ” G pairs C(WC)+U(wobble), U pairs A(WC)+G(wobble); G-U the only standard wobble, distinct from WC) + Wikipedia *Base pair* (canonical AвҖўU 2 H-bonds / GвҖўC 3 H-bonds, pairing reciprocal) + Wikipedia *Wobble base pair* + IUPAC-IUB 1970 *Biochemistry* 9(20):4022 (complement table) + Biopython `complement_rna("CGAUT")`вҶ’`"GCUAA"`. Rule {A-U, U-A, G-C, C-G}=WatsonCrick, {G-U, U-G}=Wobble, all else false/null; complement AвҶ’U/UвҶ’A/GвҶ’C/CвҶ’G/**TвҶ’A**(DNA T=U)/NвҶ’N/RвҶ’Y; symmetry `f(x,y)==f(y,x)`; non-alphabetвҶ’false/null no exception. One non-correctness normalization (case-insensitive upper-casing). No contradictions. **No new concept** вҖ” enriches the shared [[rna-base-pairing]] primitive (the MIRNA-PAIR-001 sibling), adding the typed `GetBasePairType` classifier surface.
- [[rna-partition-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit RNA-PARTITION-001 (**RNA partition function (McCaskill) and Boltzmann structure probability** вҖ” the probabilistic/ensemble layer of the RNA secondary-structure family): the Boltzmann-weighted counterpart of MFE folding that computes the equilibrium partition function `Z`, per-base-pair binding probabilities, and the Boltzmann probability of a given structure. Sources: **McCaskill 1990** *Biopolymers* 29(6-7):1105 (rank 1, PMID 1695107 вҖ” full equilibrium partition function + substructure probabilities, **O(nВі) recursion**) + **S. Will MIT 18.417 (2011)** slides (rank 1 вҖ” inside `Q_ij = Q_{i,j-1} + ОЈ_k Q_{i,k-1}В·Q^b_{kj}`, `Z = Q_{1n}`, base case `Q_ij=1` for iвүҘjвҲ’m; outside base-pair-probability recursion; `Pr[P|S]=ZвҒ»В№exp(вҲ’ОІE(P))`) + **Freiburg McCaskill tool** (rank 3 вҖ” simplified fixed-per-pair `E_bp` model, WC+GU pairing) + **ViennaRNA pf_fold** (rank 3 вҖ” `p(s)=e^(вҲ’ОІE(s))/Z`, default 37 В°C = 310.15 K, RT = 0.61626805). **Correction (2026-06-16):** base-pair probability requires the **outside** recursion `p_kl = Q^b_klВ·O_kl/Z`; the external-only term is **wrong for nestable pairs** (`GGGAAACCC` P(2,6)=6/20 not external 1/20; verified to 3.3e-16 vs Boltzmann brute force). Oracles (E_bp=0 вҮ’ Z counts structures): `AAAA`вҶ’1, `GC`вҶ’1, `GGGGCCCC`вҶ’16, `GGGAAACCC`вҶ’20 (two independent derivations). Invariants Z вүҘ 1 (empty structure weight 1), P(i,j) вҲҲ [0,1] + symmetric, per-base pairing sum вүӨ 1 (300 random seqs, max 0.983), monotone in E_bp; min-loop m forbids jвҲ’k вүӨ m pairs, WC+GU only. One simplification (fixed-per-pair `E_bp` energy model vs full Turner NN вҖ” energy model only; recurrence + probabilities + invariants conformant with McCaskill 1990), no source contradictions. **New concept** [[rna-partition-function-mccaskill]] вҖ” the ensemble/`alternative_to` counterpart of [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding]].
- [[rna-pkpredict-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit RNA-PKPREDICT-001 (**Pseudoknot structure prediction вҖ” canonical H-type, pknotsRG class**; the **crossing-helix layer** of the RNA secondary-structure family, `RnaSecondaryStructure`): predict the optimal fold that may contain a single simple recursive pseudoknot (two **crossing** helices, `i<k<j<l` Antczak 2018) вҖ” the one feature the nested [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding|MFE]] / [[rna-partition-function-mccaskill|McCaskill]] predictors cannot represent. Sources: **Reeder & Giegerich 2004** *BMC Bioinformatics* 5:104 (rank 1, PMC514697 вҖ” pknotsRG "two crossing helices with three intervening loops", grammar `a~~~u~~~b~~~v~~~a'~~~w~~~b'`, **O(nвҒҙ)/O(nВІ)**, canonization rules, penalties) + **pknotsRG `Energy.lhs`** source (rank 3 вҖ” verbatim penalties + same-NN-model helices, no extra per-pair penalty) + **Wikipedia/Rivas & Eddy 1999** (H-type 5'вҶ’3' stem1-5'вҶ’loop1вҶ’stem2-5'вҶ’loop2вҶ’stem1-3'вҶ’loop3вҶ’stem2-3', two-layer `()`/`[]`) + **PDB 437D / Su 1999** (BWYV real H-type, tertiary-stabilized) + **Antczak 2018** (crossing `i<k<j<l`). Energy = Turner NN stacking both helices + penalties **pseudoknot initiation 9.0** (anti-spurious-knot gate) / **unpaired loop nt 0.3** / **base pair inside knot 0.0** (kcal/mol). Canonization: equal-length bulge-free helices / maximal extent / fixed overlap boundary. Oracles designed H-type `GGGGAACCCCAACCCCAAGGGG`вҶ’`HasPseudoknot==true`, stems (0,15)вҖҰ(3,12)+(6,21)вҖҰ(9,18), two-layer `((((..[[[[..))))..]]]]`, О”G<MFE; plain hairpin `GGGGAAAACCCC`вҶ’`HasPseudoknot==false` = MFE `((((....))))`; BWYV `GGCGCGGCACCGUCCGCGGAACAAACGG`вҶ’NN optimum is the stem-1 hairpin **not** the knot (documented NN-only limit). Invariants `FreeEnergy вүӨ CalculateMfeStructure().FreeEnergy` (MFE fallback), no spurious knot, each position paired вүӨ1Г— + вүҘ1 genuine crossing; empty/null/too-shortвҶ’empty pair-free О”G 0. One documented scope note (PARTIAL pknotsRG coverage вҖ” single canonical H-type only; recursively-nested / over-arching / multiple knots **not** implemented; loops fold with the existing MFE). No contradictions. **New concept** [[rna-pseudoknot-prediction]] вҖ” the crossing-structure complement of the nested MFE folder + McCaskill ensemble.
- [[rna-pkrecursive-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit RNA-PKRECURSIVE-001 (**Recursive pknotsRG pseudoknot prediction вҖ” nested / multiple / over-arching H-type knots**; the **recursive-grammar extension** of the single-knot RNA-PKPREDICT-001, `RnaSecondaryStructure`): predict the optimal fold that may contain **several** pseudoknots and knots **nested inside loops / over-arched by an enclosing helix**, filling exactly the PARTIAL-coverage gap the single-knot unit recorded. **Same pknotsRG class** (Reeder & Giegerich 2004/2007) вҖ” same Turner-NN energy on both helices, same penalties **initiation 9.0 / unpaired loop nt 0.3 / pair inside knot 0.0** kcal/mol, same canonization rules вҖ” but the three loops *u*/*v*/*w* now fold by the **same recursive folder** (a loop may contain a further knot), the top level **chains multiple knots**, and an enclosing helix may **over-arch** a knot. Sources: **Reeder & Giegerich 2004** *BMC Bioinformatics* 5:104 (loops "fold internally вҖҰ **including simple recursive pseudoknots**", **O(nвҒҙ)/O(nВІ)**, canonization 8вҶ’4 boundaries vs Rivas & Eddy O(nвҒ¶)/O(nвҒҙ)) + **Reeder, Steffen & Giegerich 2007** *NAR* 35:W320 (per-interval **competition** with unknotted foldings вҖ” the whole-sequence mechanism enabling multiple/nested knots) + **pknotsRG `Energy.lhs`** (verbatim 9.0/0.3/0.0) + **Antczak 2018** (crossing `i<k<j<l`). Constructed fully-derivable oracles: over-arching `AAAAAAAAGGGGAACCCCAACCCCAAGGGGUUUUUUUU` (38 nt)вҶ’`((((((((((((..[[[[..))))..]]]]))))))))` **О”G вҲ’14.37** (single-knot/MFE both вҲ’13.05, no combined structure); two-knot 80-ntвҶ’**two** crossing knots (crossing-count 32) **О”G вҲ’28.74** (single/MFE вҲ’27.14, none); plain `GGGGAAAACCCC`вҶ’ no knot = MFE; single-knot parity `GGGGAACCCCAACCCCAAGGGG`вҶ’identical вҲ’8.76. Invariants recursive О”G вүӨ MFE (0 violations, 150-seq random sweep), no spurious knots, each position paired вүӨ1Г— + вүҘ1 crossing; empty/null/too-shortвҶ’empty pair-free. **Excluded** (verbatim): triple-crossing helices, kissing hairpins, bulged/unequal-length helices. Two scope notes: PARTIAL recursion (realizes the recursive *class* via maximal-extent helix scan, not bit-identical to the reference 4-boundary ADP parser) + two-simultaneous-knot cases are **engineered** (isolated AВ·U clamps вҖ” two strong GВ·C knots are the genuine MFE only when the cross-region nested alternative is suppressed). No contradictions. **Enriches** [[rna-pseudoknot-prediction]] (В§6, the recursive extension of the single-knot concept вҖ” no new concept).
- [[rna-pseudoknot-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit RNA-PSEUDOKNOT-001 (**Pseudoknot detection** вҖ” identify **crossing** base pairs in a **given** structure; the detection/analysis facet of the RNA crossing-helix family, `RnaSecondaryStructure.DetectPseudoknots`): given a base-pair **set** (not a sequence), a pure **O(nВІ) combinatorial scan** reports every crossing pair-of-pairs `i<k<j<l`. Sources: **Antczak et al. 2018** *Bioinformatics* 34(8):1304 (rank 1 вҖ” crossing/conflict `i<j<i'<j'`, pseudoknot **order** = min base-pair-set decompositions to nested, DBL notation order 0 `()`/1 `[]`/2 `{}`/3 `<>`/4вҖ“8 letters, H-type `([)]`) + **Smit, Rother, Heringa & Knight 2008** *RNA* 14(3):410 (rank 1 вҖ” pseudoknot presence *requires* crossing pairs; order-assignment / pseudoknot-removal family) + **biotite.structure.pseudoknots** (rank 3 вҖ” crossing = not purely nestable; nested order 0 / knotted order 1+) + **Wikipedia Pseudoknot** (rank 4, cites Rivas & Eddy 1999). Crossing `i<k<j<l` = pseudoknot; two exhaustive negatives **nested** `i<k<l<j` + **disjoint** `j<k`. Oracles `([)]`=(0,2)+(1,3)вҶ’`0<1<2<3`вҶ’one pseudoknot, nested (0,5)+(1,4)вҶ’none, disjoint (0,2)+(3,5)вҶ’none. Invariants вүҘ2 pairs required / endpoints normalized min-max to open<close / deterministic / every reported knot satisfies `i<k<j<l`. **Distinct** from the energy-driven [[rna-pseudoknot-prediction]] predictor (pair set vs sequence, O(nВІ) scan vs O(nвҒҙ) energy DP) вҖ” it *is* the crossing primitive that predictor's validity invariant leans on. One scope note: pseudoknot-**order** grouping (DBL layering) Not Implemented (reports the binary crossing relations); no contradictions. **New concept** [[rna-pseudoknot-detection]] вҖ” the analysis-side sibling of the crossing-helix predictor.
- [[rna-stemloop-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit RNA-STEMLOOP-001 (**Stem-Loop (Hairpin) Detection**, area `RnaStructure`): the **enumeration layer** of the RNA secondary-structure family вҖ” `FindStemLoops(sequence, minStem, minLoop, maxLoop, allowWobble)` / `FindHairpins` **scan a sequence for every stem-loop** it can form (stem of antiparallel WC/wobble pairs + apical loop), an **O(nВІВ·L)** scan distinct from the single-optimal [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding|MFE folder]], the hairpin *energy* unit [[rna-hairpin-001-evidence]], and the miRNA-specific [[pre-mirna-hairpin-detection]]. Sources: Wikipedia (Stem-loop / Tetraloop / Pseudoknot вҖ” loop **вүҘ3 nt** steric floor, optimal **4-8 nt**; UUCG+GNRA **~70%** of 16S-rRNA tetraloops) + Woese 1990 (PNAS 87:8467) + Antao 1991 (NAR 19:5901, **UUCG most stable**) + Heus & Pardi 1991 (Science 253:191) + Rivas & Eddy 1999 (pseudoknot alg) + NNDB Turner 2004 (tetraloop energetics). Tetraloop families **GNRA** (GAAA/GCAA/GGAA/GUAA) / **UNCG** (UACG/UCCG/UGCG/UUCG) / **CUUG**, ~3.0 kcal/mol bonus; `FindPseudoknots` flags crossing pairs `i<k<j<l` (same primitive as [[rna-pseudoknot-detection]]). Oracles `GGGAAAACCC`вҶ’`(((....)))` (3-bp stem + AAAA loop), `GGGCGAAAGCCC`вҶ’GNRA tetraloop, `AAAAвҖҰ`/`GC`/`GCAUC`вҶ’none. Invariants non-overlap / вүӨ1 pair per base / contiguous loop / antiparallel stem; defaults wobble-on, minLoop 3, minStem 3. Limitations: no PK prediction from sequence, simplified energy, no internal loops/bulges, single structure. No contradictions. **New concept** [[rna-stem-loop-enumeration]].
- [[rna-struct-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit RNA-STRUCT-001 (**Secondary Structure Prediction**, area `RnaStructure`): the **top-level structure-prediction umbrella** on `RnaSecondaryStructure` вҖ” `Predict(sequence)` (a **Nussinov & Jacobson 1980** O(nВі)/O(nВІ) base-pair-**maximizing** DP), `PredictWithConstraints` (forced base pairs, Mathews 2004), `ToDotBracket`/`FromDotBracket` (notation round-trip). Headline objective = maximize the **(weighted) base-pair count** (WC вҲ’2.0 / wobble вҲ’1.0), "**relative stability, not physical energy units**" вҖ” a **distinct sibling** of the physical-kcal/mol [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding|RNA-MFE-001]], **not an alias**: both live on `RnaSecondaryStructure` and share its Zuker MFE machinery (this unit's **deviation D5** added `CalculateMfeStructure`/`PredictStructureMfe`, the ZukerвҖ“Stiegler traceback partner of RNA-MFE-001's `PredictStructure`). Stem-loop energy model uses Turner 2004 / NNDB terms ([[rna-free-energy-turner-model]]). Sources: Nussinov & Jacobson 1980 (*PNAS* 77:6309) + Zuker & Stiegler 1981 (*NAR* 9:133) + MIT 6.047 Lec 08 (Washietl 2012, explicit F/C/M/MВ№ recurrences) + Turner 2004/NNDB + Mathews 2004 (*PNAS* 101:7287) + Wikipedia. Oracles simple hairpin `GGGGAAAACCCC`вҶ’`((((....))))`, GNRA `GCGCGAAACGCGC`вҶ’GA first-mismatch вҲ’0.9, tRNA-like 72-nt cloverleaf, poly-A `AAAAAAAAAAAA`вҶ’no pairs/MFE 0. Invariants dot-bracket balance / MFE sign вүӨ 0 / WC stacking negative / loop init positive / non-overlap / вүӨ1 pair per base; empty/nullвҶ’MFE 0, min hairpin 3-bp stem + 3-nt loop, case-insensitive. **Pseudoknots detected (not predicted)** via the `i<k<j<l` crossing test ([[rna-pseudoknot-detection]]); D1/D2/D5 resolved, D3 int21 (2,304) / D4 int22 (36,864) internal-loop lookup tables BLOCKED (too large for inline static data). No source contradictions; one wiki reconciliation (RNA-STRUCT-001 вү  RNA-MFE-001, superseding the earlier alias assumption). **New concept** [[rna-secondary-structure-prediction]].
- [[phylo-boot-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit PHYLO-BOOT-001 (Phylogenetic Bootstrap Analysis вҖ” Felsenstein's bootstrap proportions; first phylogenetics PHYLO-* unit): Felsenstein 1985 *Evolution* 39(4):783 (origin вҖ” resample characters with replacement, same sample size, keep species; *P* = fraction of bootstrap samples a group appears in; 95%вҶ’significant) + Lemoine 2018 *Nature* 556:452 PMC6030568 (same-length pseudo-alignments; support = proportion of pseudo-trees containing that branch; branch = bipartition; binary per-replicate) + Biopython `Bio.Phylo.Consensus` (`bootstrap`/`bootstrap_trees`/`get_support` вҖ” column resample `randint(0,length-1)`, clades matched **by terminal leaf-name set**, only `find_clades(terminal=False)` scored, `(t+1)*100/size`) sources; oracles two-group `AAAAAAAAAA`/`AAAAAAAAAA`/`GGGGGGGGGG`/`GGGGGGGGGG` UPGMA+JukesCantor 100 reps seed 42 вҶ’ support{A,B}=support{C,D}=1.0 (saturated JC distances вҶ’ identical topology every replicate), all-identical `ACGTACGT`вҶ’every clade 1.0; MUST-test supportвҲҲ[0,1] / determinism / keys=non-trivial reference clades / support=k/replicates, input validation null/<2-seq/replicates<1 throw; two source-consistent assumptions (rooted-clade scoring vs unrooted bipartitions matching Biopython, proportion [0,1] vs percentage Г—100); no contradictions. Own concept [[phylogenetic-bootstrap-support]].
- [[phylo-comp-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit PHYLO-COMP-001 (Tree Comparison вҖ” RobinsonвҖ“Foulds distance, MRCA, patristic distance; second phylogenetics PHYLO-* unit): Wikipedia RobinsonвҖ“Foulds metric / MRCA / Phylogenetic tree + Robinson & Foulds 1981 (doi:10.1016/0025-5564(81)90043-2, RF proper metric via splits) + Smith 2020 (generalized RF) + Day 1985 (linear-time) sources; RF = symmetric difference `A+B` of canonical split sets (raw count, even, rooted-clade = dummy-leaf), **max RF = 2(nвҲ’2) rooted vs 2(nвҲ’3) unrooted** reconciled by dummy-leaf equivalence; MRCA O(n) recursive leaf-name traversal (not-in-treeвҶ’null), patristic = `dist(x,MRCA)+dist(y,MRCA)` (not-in-treeвҶ’NaN, zero-branchesвҶ’0); invariants RF identity/symmetric/вүҘ0/even, MRCA symmetric/always-ancestor/unique, patristic PD(x,x)=0/symmetric/вүҘ0; two source-backed scope decisions (binary-only via `PhyloNode` Left/Right, rooted-only via UPGMA/NJ); no deviations, no contradictions. Own concept [[tree-comparison-metrics]].
- [[phylo-dist-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit PHYLO-DIST-001 (Phylogenetic Distance Matrix Calculation; third phylogenetics PHYLO-* unit): Wikipedia Models-of-DNA-evolution / Substitution-model / Distance-matrices-in-phylogeny + Jukes & Cantor 1969 + Kimura 1980 + Felsenstein 2004 sources; `CalculatePairwiseDistance`/`CalculateDistanceMatrix` over four methods **Hamming** (raw count) / **p-distance** (`differences/comparableSites`) / **JC69** (`-3/4В·ln(1вҲ’4p/3)`) / **K2P** (`-1/2В·ln((1вҲ’2SвҲ’V)В·вҲҡ(1вҲ’2V))`, S=transition/V=transversion); matrix symmetric / zero-diagonal / non-negative / *nГ—n*, correction ordering JC69вүҘp & K2PвүҘp, triangle-inequality expected-not-guaranteed; pairwise deletion (gaps + IUPAC N/R/Y skipped), case-insensitive; **JC69 saturates pвүҘ3/4вҶ’+вҲһ / K2P VвүҘ1/2вҶ’+вҲһ**, all-gap/emptyвҶ’0, unequal-lengthвҶ’ArgumentException; oracles `ACGTACGT`/`TCGTACGT`вҶ’Hamming 1/p 0.125/JC69вүҲ0.137, transition `GCGT` K2PвүҲ0.34657 vs transversion `CCGT`вүҲ0.31713, mixedвүҲ0.30679, gapвҶ’7 sites; two API-contract assumptions (empty/all-gapвҶ’0, pairwise deletion); no contradictions. Own concept [[evolutionary-distance-matrix]].

Serializer, not a new algorithm вҖ” no own concept; cross-links [[tree-comparison-metrics]] / [[evolutionary-distance-matrix]] / [[phylogenetic-bootstrap-support]].

- [[phylo-tree-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit PHYLO-TREE-001 (Phylogenetic Tree Construction вҖ” UPGMA & Neighbor-Joining; the phylogenetics PHYLO-* tree-building core): Wikipedia UPGMA / Neighbor-joining / Phylogenetic-tree + Saitou & Nei 1987 (MBE 4(4):406вҖ“425, NJ) + Sokal & Michener 1958 (UPGMA) + Felsenstein 2004 sources; `BuildTree`/`BuildTreeFromMatrix` consume the distance matrix and emit a `PhyloNode` tree via two agglomerative methods вҖ” **UPGMA** (rooted ultrametric, molecular clock, **height=d/2**, arithmetic-mean update, O(nВі)/O(nВІ)) and **NJ** (unrooted/midpoint-rooted, clock-free, **Q(i,j)=(nвҲ’2)В·d(i,j)вҲ’ОЈd(i,k)вҲ’ОЈd(j,k)** join minimum-Q, Оҙ(f,u)=d(f,g)/2+(ОЈd(f,k)вҲ’ОЈd(g,k))/(2(nвҲ’2)), additive-matrix topology guarantee, **negative branches preserved, not clamped**, O(nВі)); invariants all-taxa-leaves / binary / n leaves+nвҲ’1 internal / UPGMA branchesвүҘ0 / UPGMA ultrametric+rooted / NJ additive-correct+may-be-negative+no-clock; oracles UPGMA 5S-rRNA matrixвҶ’(a,b)@17вҶ’((a,b),e)@22вҶ’(c,d)@28вҶ’final@33, Оҙ(a,u)=8.5/Оҙ(e,v)=11/Оҙ(c,w)=14/root 16.5 (tips all 16.5, tol 1e-10), NJ 5-taxonвҶ’first join (a,b) **QвӮҒ(a,b)=вҲ’50**, Оҙ(a,u)=2/Оҙ(b,u)=3/Оҙ(u,v)=3/Оҙ(c,v)=4/Оҙ(v,w)=2/Оҙ(d,w)=2/Оҙ(e,w)=1 (patristic recovers input); edge cases <2/unequalвҶ’throw, identicalвҶ’arbitrary join, all-equalвҶ’star, saturated p>0.75вҶ’JC +вҲһ; 32 runs (M01вҖ“M13/S01вҖ“S05/C01вҖ“C05), S06 removed (dup of S02); deviations None (В§8). Own concept [[distance-based-tree-construction]].
- [[pop-ancestry-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit POP-ANCESTRY-001 (Ancestry Estimation вҖ” supervised/projection ADMIXTURE, estimate ancestry proportions Q by EM with **fixed** reference allele frequencies F; **first population-genetics POP-\* unit**): Alexander, Novembre & Lange 2009 *Genome Research* 19(9):1655 (rank 1 вҖ” genotype gвҲҲ{0,1,2}=allele-1 count, Q IГ—K / F KГ—J, **log-likelihood Eq. 2** `L=ОЈбөўОЈвұј{gВ·ln(ОЈqВ·f)+(2вҲ’g)В·ln(ОЈqВ·(1вҲ’f))}` under `ОЈ_k q_ik=1`, **FRAPPE EM Eq. 4** `q^{n+1}=(1/2J)ОЈвұј[gВ·a+(2вҲ’g)В·b]`, convergence Eq. 5 О”L<Оө default 10вҒ»вҒҙ, cost O(IJKВІ), K! label-permutation maxima) + Alexander & Lange 2011 *BMC Bioinformatics* 12:246 (supervised mode вҖ” labelled reference individuals as training samples, less allele-freq uncertainty; full text Springer-gated) + ADMIXTURE 1.4 Manual В§2.10 supervised / В§2.14 projection (reference rows of Q pinned, refs 100% single-ancestry; learned F as fixed input `admixture -P`) sources; oracles symmetric K=2 J=2 panel f_A=[0.8,0.2]/f_B=[0.2,0.8] g=[2,0] from (0.5,0.5) вҶ’ **one EM iter (0.8,0.2) exactly** вҶ’ (0.9412,0.0588) вҶ’ converges (1.0,0.0), single-SNP f=[0.9,0.1] g=2вҶ’(0.9,0.1)/g=1вҶ’(0.5,0.5) uninformative-het/g=0вҶ’(0.1,0.9), identical panels uniform fixed point; MUST ОЈ_k q=1 / EM-ascent L non-decreasing / diagnosticвҶ’source; two assumptions (maxIterations budget augments Оө=10вҒ»вҒҙ convergence вҖ” same fixed point; missing genotype вҲү{0,1,2} skipped); label non-identifiability pinned by fixed labelled panels; no contradictions. - [[pop-div-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit POP-DIV-001 (Diversity statistics вҖ” nucleotide diversity ПҖ, Watterson's Оё, Tajima's D, heterozygosity; **second population-genetics POP-\* unit**, sibling of POP-ANCESTRY-001): Nei & Li 1979 *PNAS* (ПҖ = ОЈ_{i<j} d_ij / (C(n,2)В·L), mean per-site pairwise differences) + Watterson 1975 *TPB* (ОёМӮ_W = S/a_n, a_n = ОЈ_{i=1}^{nвҲ’1} 1/i harmonic number; per-site Оё_W = S/(a_nВ·L)) + Tajima 1989 *Genetics* (D = (kМӮ вҲ’ S/a_1)/вҲҡ(e_1В·S + e_2В·S(SвҲ’1)), **kМӮ = average pairwise-difference COUNT not per-site ПҖ**, variance terms a_1/a_2/b_1/b_2/c_1/c_2/e_1/e_2; DвүҲ0 neutral / D<0 excess rare alleles=sweep-or-expansion / D>0 deficit=balancing-or-contraction) + Nei 1978 *Genetics* (unbiased gene diversity H_obs = n/(nвҲ’1)В·H_exp, H_exp = (1/L)ОЈ(1вҲ’ОЈpВІ); haploid H_obs вүЎ ПҖ) sources; all "exact match" no deviations; Wikipedia oracle n=5/L=20/S=4/a_1=25/12 вҶ’ kМӮ=2.0/ПҖ=0.1/S/a_1вүҲ1.92/d=0.08/Оё_WвүҲ0.096 вҶ’ **DвүҲ0.273** (TD-C01/TD-C02); edge cases n=0вҶ’0, n=1вҶ’ПҖ0/Оё undef, n=2вҶ’ПҖ defined but **D undefinedвҶ’0** (needs nвүҘ3), S=0/monomorphicвҶ’all 0, VarвүӨ0вҶ’D=0; API note `CalculateTajimasD(kМӮ, S, n)` takes kМӮ NOT per-site ПҖ; no contradictions. Own concept [[genetic-diversity-statistics]].
- [[pop-freq-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit POP-FREQ-001 (Allele & genotype frequencies вҖ” major/minor frequencies, MAF, MAF filtering; foundational population-genetics POP-\* primitive): Wikipedia *Allele frequency* / *Genotype frequency* (biallelic `p = f(AA) + ВҪf(AB)`, `q = f(BB) + ВҪf(AB)`, **`p + q = 1`**; allele-counting `total = 2В·(n_AA+n_AB+n_BB)`, `major = 2В·n_AA+n_AB`, `minor = 2В·n_BB+n_AB`; four-o'clock oracle 49/42/9 вҶ’ freq(a)=0.30/freq(A)=0.70) + Wikipedia *Minor allele frequency* (`MAF = min(alt_freq, 1вҲ’alt_freq)`, **`0 вүӨ MAF вүӨ 0.5`**; HapMap MAF вүҘ 0.05, common>0.05 vs rare<0.05) + VCF/PLINK dosage encoding (0=hom-ref/1=het/2=hom-alt, `alt_freq = ОЈg/(2n)`) + Gillespie 2004 / NDSU PopGen sources; oracles AF-1вҖҰAF-6, MAF-1вҖҰMAF-6 (alt_freq 0.7 вҶ’ MAF 0.3 symmetry; monomorphic вҶ’ 0; 50/50 вҶ’ 0.5), FLT-1вҖҰFLT-6 (MAF<0.01 / <0.05 / >0.4, empty/all/none); invariants p+q=1, major+minor=total, MAF symmetric 0вҖҰ0.5; edge cases zero samplesвҶ’(0,0), empty vectorвҶ’MAF 0, **negative count вҶ’ `ArgumentOutOfRangeException`**; scope = biallelic counting/normalization only (no HWE test, no multiallelic, no phasing/imputation); all exact-match, no deviations/contradictions. Own concept [[allele-genotype-frequencies]].
- [[pop-fst-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit POP-FST-001 (Fst fixation index + F-statistics Fis/Fit/Fst + pairwise Fst; population-genetics POP-\* differentiation unit, **consumes** per-population allele frequencies from POP-FREQ-001): Wikipedia *Fixation index* (**Wright 1965 variance-based** `Fst = Пғ_SВІ/(pBar(1вҲ’pBar))`; two-pop `pBar=(n1В·p1+n2В·p2)/(n1+n2)`, `Пғ_SВІ=(n1(p1вҲ’pBar)ВІ+n2(p2вҲ’pBar)ВІ)/(n1+n2)`; multi-locus **ratio-of-sums** `ОЈПғ_SВІ/ОЈhet`; FstвҲҲ[0,1], 0=panmixia/1=fixed differences; **not a metric** вҖ” fails triangle inequality) + Wikipedia *F-statistics* (heterozygosity partition `Fis=1вҲ’Hi/Hs`, `Fit=1вҲ’Hi/Ht`, `Fst=1вҲ’Hs/Ht`; **exact identity** `(1вҲ’Fit)=(1вҲ’Fis)(1вҲ’Fst)`) + Wright 1950/1965, Weir & Cockerham 1984 (Оё estimator вҖ” cited as what is **deliberately NOT** implemented: no ANOVA/finite-sample bias correction), Holsinger & Weir 2009, Cavalli-Sforza 1994 sources; oracles identicalвҶ’0, fixed p1=1/p2=0вҶ’**1.0 exactly** (pBar=.5,var=.25,het=.25), pop1=(.9,.8)/pop2=(.1,.2)вҶ’1/2, unequal sizes 0.006274вҖҰ, components Fis=1/19/Fit=1/13/Fst=1/39, scale 1/2499 & 61/198, pairwise cells 1/99,4/21,3/25, excess-het **negative** Fis=вҲ’2/3/Fit=вҲ’2/5/Fst=4/25; ref values Cavalli-Sforza (MbutiвҖ“PNG 0.4573, mean 0.1338) + Elhaik 2012 HapMap; edge cases denominator 0 (pBar=0/1, both-fixed-same, empty)вҶ’**return 0**, monomorphicвҶ’0; pairwise matrix symmetric, zero diagonal; 25 tests (вҲ’1 dup +4 new); no deviations/contradictions. Own concept [[population-differentiation-fst]].
- [[pop-hw-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit POP-HW-001 (Hardy-Weinberg equilibrium chi-square test; population-genetics POP-\* unit, **consumes** genotype counts from POP-FREQ-001): Wikipedia *Hardy-Weinberg principle* (Hardy 1908 / Weinberg 1908 вҖ” expected genotype freqs `f(AA)=pВІ`/`f(Aa)=2pq`/`f(aa)=qВІ`, Ford moth example, deviation causes, genotyping-error note) + Wikipedia *Chi-squared test* (Pearson goodness-of-fit `ПҮВІ=ОЈ(OвҲ’E)ВІ/E`) + Emigh 1980 (chi-square comparison) + Wigginton et al. 2005 AJHG (**exact test** вҖ” cited as the out-of-scope alternative) sources; allele freq `p=(2В·n_AA+n_Aa)/(2n)`/`q=1вҲ’p`, expected counts `E={pВІn,2pqn,qВІn}`, **df=1** (`#genotypesвҲ’#alleles=3вҲ’2`), p-value via chi-square CDF (lower-incomplete-gamma approx), default **Оұ=0.05** critical 3.841; `TestHardyWeinberg` returns InEquilibrium/ChiSquare/PValue; oracles Ford moth (1469,138,5)вҶ’`pвүҲ0.954`/`ПҮВІвүҲ0.83`вҶ’in-eq (HW-E01), perfect (25,50,25)вҶ’`ПҮВІ=0` (HW-E02), excess-het (10,80,10)вҶ’`ПҮВІ=36 вү« 3.84`вҶ’out-of-eq (HW-E03), zero samplesвҶ’InEquilibrium true/PValue 1 (HW-E04), fixed (100,0,0)вҶ’in-eq (HW-E05), all-het (0,100,0)вҶ’out-of-eq (HW-E06); edge cases **zero nвҶ’PValue 1** (no evidence against HвӮҖ), **expected-0 term skipped** (div-by-zero guard); scope = biallelic chi-square goodness-of-fit only (no exact test, no multiallelic); no deviations/contradictions. Own concept [[hardy-weinberg-equilibrium-test]].
- [[pop-ld-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit POP-LD-001 (Linkage disequilibrium вҖ” `CalculateLD` (D, D', rВІ) + `FindHaplotypeBlocks`; population-genetics POP-\* unit, **consumes** allele/haplotype frequencies from POP-FREQ-001): Wikipedia *Linkage disequilibrium* (`D = p_AB вҲ’ p_AВ·p_B`; Lewontin 1964 `D' = |D|/D_max` with sign-branched `D_max` clamped [0,1]; Hill & Robertson 1968 `rВІ = DВІ/(p_AВ·q_AВ·p_BВ·q_B)`; **diploid-frequency result** `R_AB = r_AB` (Wright 1933) вҮ’ rВІ computable **without phase**) + Wikipedia *Haplotype block* (Gabriel 2002 / Patil 2001 threshold blocks) sources; implementation `rВІ` = squared Pearson correlation of 0/1/2 genotype dosage vectors `CovВІ/(VarВ·Var)`, `D` from diploid covariance `Cov=2D вҮ’ D=Cov/2`; `FindHaplotypeBlocks` = simplified adjacent-pair Gabriel (consecutive `rВІ вүҘ threshold`, default **0.7**, вүҘ2 variants); oracles perfect LD (identical vectors)вҶ’`rВІвүҲ1`, no LD (balanced)вҶ’`rВІвүҲ0`, anti-correlationвҶ’`rВІ=1`/`D'=1` (sign-blind), block oracles singleвҶ’none / two-highвҶ’one / two-lowвҶ’none / all-strongвҶ’one span / non-contiguousвҶ’multiple; INV `0вүӨrВІвүӨ1`, `0вүӨ|D'|вүӨ1`, block StartвүӨEnd/вүҘ2/non-overlapping/ordered, distance+IDs preserved; edge cases emptyвҶ’`rВІ=0,D'=0`, monomorphic (zero variance/denominator)вҶ’`rВІ=0` (guarded), all-identicalвҶ’`rВІ=0`; scope = two-biallelic-loci rВІ/D' + adjacent-pair blocks only (no full LD matrix, no phasing/EM, no decay-curve fit, no exact Gabriel CI); no deviations/contradictions. Own concept [[linkage-disequilibrium]].
- [[pop-select-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit POP-SELECT-001 (Selection-signature detection вҖ” `CalculateEhh`, `CalculateIHS`, `StandardizeIHS`, `ScanForSelection` = integrated Haplotype Score iHS; population-genetics POP-\* unit, **consumes** derived/ancestral allele freqs + MAF filter from POP-FREQ-001): Voight et al. 2006 PLoS Biol (**iHS = ln(iHH_A/iHH_D)** ancestral numerator, standardized to std-normal in derived-freq bins, integration truncated at **EHH<0.05**, scan = proportion `|iHS|>2` in ~50-SNP windows, **MAF>5%**) + Sabeti 2002 (EHH = homozygosity prob of two core-allele chromosomes) + selscan Szpiech & Hernandez 2014 (`EHH_c=ОЈC(n_h,2)/C(n_c,2)`, trapezoidal iHH, **opposite sign convention** `ln(iHH_1/iHH_0)`) + rehh (worked SNP F1205400 `iHH_A=284429.9`/`iHH_D=2057107.4`вҶ’ln=**вҲ’1.978569274**, `limehh`/`freqbin`=0.05) sources; oracles constructed panel iHH_A=10/iHH_D=40вҶ’ln(0.25)=**вҲ’1.386294361** (long derived haplotypeвҶ’negative iHS), EHH unit values 0.5/0.3333/1.0/0.0, balanced decayвҶ’iHSвүҲ0; INV EHHвҲҲ[0,1], single-element binвҶ’std iHS 0, window value = count(|iHS|>2)/size; throws on monomorphic core / null / empty / inconsistent-length / invalid core allele / OOR coreIndex; assumptions (NвҲ’1 SD, 20 default bins) affect magnitude only; scope = single-core iHS/EHH scan (no XP-EHH, no Fst-outlier/Tajima's-D scan, no genetic-map interpolation); no deviations/contradictions. Own concept [[selection-scan-ihs-ehh]].

- [[probe-design-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit PROBE-DESIGN-001 (**TaqMan 5'-nuclease hydrolysis-probe design rules**, opt-in extension over the unchanged generic hybridization-probe designer; **first PROBE-\* unit**): Applied Biosystems / Thermo Fisher (rank 2, chemistry manufacturer) + PREMIER Biosoft (rank 3) + ScienceDirect "TaqMan" (5'-G quenching rationale) + IDT (corroborating) sources; the TaqMan-specific hard rules вҖ” **no G at the 5' end** (a 5'-G quenches the reporter *even after cleavage* вҶ’ hard rule, not a soft penalty; `SelectTaqManStrand` moves to the antisense strand when unavoidable), **more Cs than Gs**, **no run of вүҘ4 consecutive Gs** (separate from the generic homopolymer cap), **GC 30вҖ“80%**, **length 18вҖ“22 nt** (default, `minLength`/`maxLength` parameterised), **probe Tm вүҘ primer Tm + 10 В°C** (caller-supplied primer Tm; probe Tm via the PRIMER-TM-001-validated salt-adjusted `81.5+16.6В·logвӮҒвӮҖ[NaвҒә]+41В·GCвҲ’600/N` formula, not a TaqMan-specific NN calc); oracles CCATCACCCTACATCACC passes-all (primerTm вүӨ 39.35), GCATCACCCTACATCACC fails 5'-G, ACCCCGGGGACCCTACAT fails GGGG-run, C=1/G=9 fails more-G-than-C, 16-nt fails len<18, GC 100% fails, sense GTTAGGGTTAGGGTTAGG вҶ’ RC CCTAACCCTAACCCTAAC strand-selection; two parameterisation assumptions (18вҖ“22 default window, repository salt-adjusted Tm engine), no source contradictions. - [[probe-design-001-lna-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for the **LNA (locked nucleic acid) Tm-adjustment** variant of PROBE-DESIGN-001: an **LNA-adjusted nearest-neighbour Tm** that raises a probe's Tm/specificity (enabling shorter MGB-style 13вҖ“20 nt probes) by locking internal bases. Sources: **McTigue, Peterson & Kahn 2004** (*Biochemistry*, rank 1 вҖ” О”О”HВ°/О”О”SВ° increments for all **32** LNA+DNA:DNA nearest neighbours; internal LNA **raises Tm**), **MELTING 5** reference impl (`McTigue2004lockedmn.xml` verbatim table in **cal/mol** + `McTigue04LockedAcid.java` вҖ” **additive-increment** application and **terminal-LNA rejection**), rmelting worked example. Model: compute plain DNA NN О”HВ°/О”SВ° then **add** the McTigue increment per LNA-containing step, onto the library's SantaLucia-1998-unified DNA NN engine (same as PRIMER-TM-001 [[primer-dimer-thermodynamics-tm]]); terminal/non-ACGT/out-of-range вҶ’ not-computable. Oracle CCATTGCTACC (LNA@4) вҶ’ О”HВ° вҲ’80.014 / О”SВ° вҲ’216.6 вҶ’ LNA Tm **63.528 В°C** vs all-DNA 59.692 (**О”Tm +3.84 В°C**), agreeing with MELTING `mct04` 63.614 to 0.086 В°C (documented base-NN-set residual; increments applied exactly). Enriches [[taqman-probe-design-rules]] (LNA section).
- [[probe-valid-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit PROBE-VALID-001 (**hybridization-probe validation / off-target specificity scan** вҖ” a **gapped SmithвҖ“Waterman local alignment** of the candidate probe against a pooled reference, replacing an earlier ungapped Hamming scan; the **specificity-checking sibling** of PROBE-DESIGN-001, a genuinely distinct algorithm): Smith & Waterman 1981 (local-alignment recurrence with the **zero floor** вҶ’ local, indel-aware; traceback stops at 0 so a mismatched tail is trimmed), Altschul et al. 1990/1997 BLAST (the **gapped-vs-ungapped** improvement вҖ” a single gapped alignment finds indel off-targets the ungapped HSPs miss; the unit realizes the *gapped local alignment* property, an **exact** full SW scan, not seed-and-extend or a genome-scale index), Karlin & Altschul 1990 / Altschul 1990 statistics (opt-in `ComputeLambdaNucleotide`/`ComputeKarlinAltschul`: `E=KВ·mВ·nВ·e^(вҲ’О»S)`, О» = root of `ОЈ p_i p_j e^(О» s_ij)=1`, bit score `S'=(О»SвҲ’ln K)/ln 2`, `E=mВ·nВ·2^(вҲ’S')`; preconditions expected-score<0 **and** a positive score; K caller-supplied), Kane et al. 2000 (empirical **>75% identity** cross-hybridization threshold, `minIdentity` default 0.75, caller-configurable; <14вҖ“15 contiguous-complement caveat); oracles вҖ” probe `ACGTACGTACGT` vs an indel copy `ACGTACTGTACGT` aligns `ACGTAC-GTACGT` 12/12 identity 1.0 `HasGaps=true` (**found by gapped, missed by ungapped Hamming maxMismatches=3**); indel+mismatch `ACGTACTGTACTT` вҶ’ SW trims `TT` tail вҶ’ 10/12 = 0.8333 (admitted @0.75, rejected @0.90); О» for +1/вҲ’3 uniform-0.25 = **1.3740631** (вүҲ blastn 1.37, expected score вҲ’2.0<0), K=0.711/S=30/m=20/n=1000 вҶ’ bit **59.9627**, **E=1.7802eвҲ’14**, EвҶ“ in S and linear in mВ·n; BLAST DNA scoring +2/вҲ’3 gap вҲ’2. ASSUMPTION: on-target = first perfect ungapped full-coverage exact match (API/labelling, not a sourced constant); no source contradictions. Own concept [[probe-offtarget-specificity-scan]].
- [[seq-atskew-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-ATSKEW-001 (**AT skew**, `(A вҲ’ T)/(A + T)` вҖ” the A/T strand-asymmetry sibling of GC skew): Lobry 1996 *Mol Biol Evol* 13(5):660 (PMID 8676740, primary вҖ” founding intra-strand base-asymmetry observation over *E. coli*/*B. subtilis*/*H. influenzae*) + Charneski et al. 2011 *PLoS Genet* 7(9):e1002283 (verbatim formula; Firmicute AT skew from **selection not mutation**) + Wikipedia "GC skew" (both formulas + range **вҲ’1вҖҰ+1**, AT skew `вҲ’1вҮ”A=0` / `+1вҮ”T=0`) + Biopython `Bio.SeqUtils.GC_skew` (symbol conventions вҖ” **case-insensitive** counting, **zero-denominator вҮ’ 0.0**, ambiguous/non-canonical bases ignored); hand-derived oracles `AAAAвҶ’1.0`, `TTTTвҶ’вҲ’1.0`, `ATATвҶ’0.0`, `AAATвҶ’0.5`, `GGCCвҶ’0.0` (no A/T), `AAATGGGCCCвҶ’0.5` (G/C ignored), `aaatвҶ’0.5` (case-insensitive); corner cases empty/no-A-or-T вҮ’ 0.0, non-A/T symbols ignored, bounds [вҲ’1,+1]; one documented ASSUMPTION (lowercase + non-ACGT handling inferred by analogy from the shipped `GC_skew` вҖ” formula itself fully sourced), no source contradictions. New concept [[dust-low-complexity-score]].
- [[seq-complex-kmer-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-COMPLEX-KMER-001 (**k-mer entropy** вҖ” Shannon entropy `H = вҲ’ОЈ pбөў logвӮӮ pбөў` of the overlapping k-mer frequency distribution, `pбөў = nбөў/(LвҲ’k+1)`, bits; the **entropy member of the `SEQ-COMPLEX-*` family**, `SequenceComplexity.CalculateKmerEntropy`): Li 2025 longdust arXiv:2509.07357 (overlapping `LвҲ’k+1` k-mers, `H=вҲ’ОЈpбөўlogвӮӮpбөў`, skewedвҮ’low / uniformвҮ’high) + ГҮakДұr 2025 EntropyвҖ“Rank Ratio arXiv:2511.05300 (same formula, base-2вҮ’bits, single-nt max logвӮӮ4=2) + Shannon 1948 (bounds `0вүӨHвүӨlog(k)`, deterministicвҮ’0 / uniformвҮ’log_b n); hand-derived oracles `ACGT` k=1вҶ’2.0 / `ACGT` k=2вҶ’logвӮӮ3вүҲ1.5849625 / `ATATAT` k=2вҶ’0.9709505945 / `AAAA` k=2вҶ’0.0 / `AAACGT` k=2вҶ’1.9219280949 (=logвӮӮ5вҲ’0.4) / `AC` k=5вҶ’0.0 (L<k); homopolymerвҮ’H0, all-distinctвҮ’H logвӮӮN; two API-shape ASSUMPTIONs (L<kвҶ’0; k<1вҶ’ArgumentOutOfRangeException, null DnaSequenceвҶ’ArgumentNullException, null/empty stringвҶ’0), no source contradictions. **Same formula as [[k-mer-statistics]]'s `Entropy` field** (a second entry point, not a new measure) вҖ” enriches that concept rather than adding a new one.
- [[seq-complex-window-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-COMPLEX-WINDOW-001 (**windowed sequence complexity** вҖ” a **sliding-window** scan emitting a per-position `ComplexityPoint` *profile*, each window carrying a **Shannon entropy** of base composition and a **linguistic complexity** value; the **profiling / scanning** member of the `SEQ-COMPLEX-*` family, distinct from the whole-sequence scalars LZ / DUST / k-entropy): Troyanskaya et al. 2002 *Bioinformatics* 18(5):679 (PMID 12050064, primary вҖ” **complexity profiles** as a function of position; linguistic complexity = distinct-subword counts, suffix-tree linear-time) + Wikipedia "Linguistic sequence complexity" (Gabrielian & Bolshoy 1999 / Trifonov 1990 вҖ” `Uбөў = Vбөў / min(4^i, NвҲ’i+1)`, summation `LC = ОЈ Vбөў / ОЈ Vmax,i`, range 0<C<1) + Wikipedia "Shannon entropy" (Shannon 1948 вҖ” `H = вҲ’ОЈ p logвӮӮ p` bits, uniform DNA max logвӮӮ4 = 2, deterministic вҮ’ 0); hand-derived oracles `ACGTACGT` window вҶ’ Shannon **2.0** / LC **23/29 = 0.7931вҖҰ**, `AAAAAAAA` poly-A window вҶ’ Shannon **0.0** / LC **6/29 = 0.2069вҖҰ**, geometry L=24/w=8/s=8 вҶ’ **3** windows ([0,7]c4 / [8,15]c12 / [16,23]c20); window count `floor((LвҲ’w)/s)+1` for LвүҘw else 0, only fully-contained windows emitted (no trailing partial), Position = `WindowStart + w/2`, bounds 0вүӨHвүӨ2 / 0вүӨLCвүӨ1; three ASSUMPTIONs (center-position label, default w=64/s=10, maxWordLength = min(6,w)), nullвҶ’ArgumentNullException / w<1В·s<1вҶ’ArgumentOutOfRangeException, no source contradictions. New concept [[windowed-sequence-complexity-profile]].
- [[seq-composition-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-COMPOSITION-001 (**sequence composition** вҖ” exact nucleotide counts/fractions A/T/G/C/U/N/Other partitioning Length, **GC content** `(G+C)/(A+T+G+C+U)`, and amino-acid residue counts; a **duplicate/consolidated Registry entry** over the two composition methods already delivered under SEQ-STATS-001, TestSpec В§7): Biopython `Bio.SeqUtils.gc_fraction` (`gc/length` in **[0,1]**, empty вҮ’ 0, case-insensitive `"CGScgs"`) + Wikipedia "GC skew" (GC/AT skew formulas, cumulative-skew origin/terminus) + IUPAC codes (canonical A/C/G/T/U + degenerate/N; the 20 amino-acid letters); worked oracles `ATGC`вҶ’GC 0.5, `GGGC`вҶ’GC 1.0/skew 0.5, `AAUUGGCC`вҶ’GC 0.5/AT skew 1.0, `MKVLWA`вҶ’6 residues each 1; corner cases empty/null вҮ’ all-zero, no-G-or-C вҮ’ skew 0.0, mixed case вҮ’ case-insensitive, non-canonical letters routed to `CountN`/`CountOther`; one ASSUMPTION (degenerate IUPAC codes excluded from GC/AT totals вҖ” Biopython counts S toward GC / W toward denominator, agrees exactly over {A,T,G,C,U}), no source contradictions. New concept [[base-composition]]; skew members on the sibling [[nucleotide-composition-skew]].
- [[seq-dinuc-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-DINUC-001 (**Dinucleotide analysis** вҖ” dinucleotide frequency `f_XY = count/(NвҲ’1)`, the **Karlin genomic-signature odds ratio** `ПҒ_XY = f_XY/(f_XВ·f_Y)`, and codon frequencies; method `CalculateDinucleotideRatios`): Karlin PMC126251 (odds-ratio definition, `r=1.0` no-bias independence baseline, normalized frequencies) + Karlin & Burge 1995 via MBE 19(6):964 (interpretation thresholds `ПҒвүӨ0.78` under-/`ПҒвүҘ1.23` over-represented вҖ” documentation-only, method returns raw ratio) + Gardiner-Garden & Frommer 1987 (CpG O/E = same odds-ratio shape normalized by `N` not `NвҲ’1` вҶ’ `N/(NвҲ’1)` modeling-choice difference) + Kazusa CUTG (codon frequency = count/total non-overlapping in-frame triplets, non-ACGT excluded); exact-rational oracles for `ATGCGCGT` (GC/CG ПҒ = 64/21 вүҲ 3.0476, AT ПҒ = 32/7 вүҲ 4.5714, TG/GT ПҒ = 32/21 вүҲ 1.5238; f_XY GC=CG=2/7, AT=TG=GT=1/7) + codon `ATGATGAAA` f0вҶ’ATG 2/3/AAA 1/3, f1вҶ’TGA 1.0; div-by-zero guard (absent constituent base вҮ’ expected 0 вҮ’ ratio **0**), case-insensitive, null/empty/len<2вҶ’empty ratios, len<3вҶ’empty codons; two documented modeling choices (Karlin `(NвҲ’1)` vs Gardiner-Garden `(N)` normalization; `U` counted as a fifth base for RNA), no source contradictions. New concept [[dinucleotide-relative-abundance]]; CpG special case [[cpg-island-detection]]; codon-frequency metric shared with [[seq-codon-freq-001-evidence]].

- [[seq-entropy-profile-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-ENTROPY-PROFILE-001 (**sliding-window Shannon entropy profile** вҖ” per fixed-width window, `H = вҲ’ОЈ pбөў logвӮӮ pбөў` bits over the window's **single-base (k=1) composition**; emitted as a standalone entropy profile). The **same per-window Shannon measure and window geometry** as the Shannon component of [[windowed-sequence-complexity-profile]] (SEQ-COMPLEX-WINDOW-001), just without the paired linguistic complexity вҶ’ a **second entry point**, enriches that concept rather than adding a new one. Sources: Shannon 1948 *Bell Syst Tech J* 27(3):379 (primary, `H=вҲ’ОЈp log p`, `0В·log0=0`) + Wikipedia "Entropy (information theory)" (base-2 вҮ’ bits, uniform max `log_b n`) + IntechOpen ch. 75997 (DNA 4-letter alphabet, max 2 bits = logвӮӮ4, sliding counter of width W). Hand-derived per-window oracles `AAAA`вҶ’0.0 / `AATT`вҶ’1.0 / `ATGC`вҶ’2.0 / `AAAT`вҶ’0.8112781244591328 / `AATG`В·`GCAA`вҶ’1.5 / `AAATTC`вҶ’1.4591479170272448; sliding profiles `AAATGC` w4 s1вҶ’[0.8112781244591328,1.5,2.0] / `AAATGCAA` w4 s2вҶ’[0.8112781244591328,2.0,1.5]; `windowSize>length`вҶ’empty profile, `==length`вҶ’single value, case-insensitive, bounds `0вүӨHвүӨlogвӮӮkвүӨ2`. One ASSUMPTION (mono-symbol k=1 alphabet is the modelling choice вҖ” sources define H over any distribution; the k-mer/block generalization is the separate SEQ-COMPLEX-KMER-001 k-entropy on [[k-mer-statistics]]); no source contradictions. Enriches [[windowed-sequence-complexity-profile]].
- [[seq-gc-analysis-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-GC-ANALYSIS-001 (**Comprehensive GC analysis** вҖ” the composite `GcAnalysisResult` bundling whole-sequence scalars OverallGcContent `(G+C)/(A+T+G+C)Г—100` + OverallGcSkew `(GвҲ’C)/(G+C)` + OverallAtSkew `(AвҲ’T)/(A+T)` with a **sliding-window** GC%/GC-skew profile and the **population variance** `ПғВІ=ОЈ(xбөўвҲ’Ој)ВІ/N` of each windowed series). The overall scalars are already covered вҖ” GC content on [[base-composition]], GC/AT skew on [[nucleotide-composition-skew]]; the genuinely-distinct windowed profile + compositional variance вҶ’ NEW concept [[windowed-gc-profile-and-variance]]. Sources: Wikipedia GC-content (Madigan & Martinko 2003 *Brock* `GC%=(G+C)/(A+T+G+C)Г—100%`) + Wikipedia GC skew (Lobry 1996 + Grigoriev 1998 cumulative-skew, spectrum вҲ’1вҖҰ+1, sign switch = replication origin/terminus) + Biopython `Bio.SeqUtils` (`GC_skew` "multiple windows", zero-division вҮ’ 0, ambiguous bases ignored; `gc_fraction` `[0,1]` = percentage Г·100) + Cuemath population variance (`ПғВІ=ОЈ(xбөўвҲ’Ој)ВІ/n`, worked `{12,13,12,14,19}`вҶ’6.8). Oracles `GGGCCAT`вҶ’GC% 71.428вҖҰ/GC-skew 0.2/AT-skew 0.0; windowed `GGCC` w2s2вҶ’windows GG(+1,100)/CC(вҲ’1,100)вҶ’`GcSkewVariance` 1.0 / `GcContentVariance` 0.0; shorter-than-window вҮ’ empty lists + variances 0, scalars still computed; no-G/C вҮ’ skew 0/GC% 0. Two labelling/estimator ASSUMPTIONs (GC% Г—100 vs Biopython `[0,1]` fraction; window "variability" = population variance Г·N, not sample Г·NвҲ’1), no source contradictions.
- [[seq-gc-profile-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-GC-PROFILE-001 (**sliding-window GC-content profile** вҖ” per fully-contained window, `GC% = (G+C)/(A+T+G+C)Г—100`, GC% only, no skew profile and no variance). The **same windowed GC-content measure and window geometry** as the composite `GcAnalysisResult`'s GC-content channel (SEQ-GC-ANALYSIS-001) вҶ’ a **standalone entry point**, enriches [[windowed-gc-profile-and-variance]] rather than adding a new concept. Sources: Wikipedia "GC-content" (`GC%=(G+C)/(A+T+G+C)Г—100%`, four-base denominator, undefined at A+T+G+C=0) + Biopython `Bio.SeqUtils.gc_fraction` (`[0,1]` Г—100 = percentage, default `ambiguous="remove"` drops N from the length, doctests `ACTGN` removeвҶ’0.50 / ignoreвҶ’0.40, RNA `GGAUCUUCGGAUCU`вҶ’0.50). Hand-derived window oracles (Г—100) `GGGG`вҶ’100.0 / `AAAA`вҶ’0.0 / `ATGC`вҶ’50.0 / `GGGA`вҶ’75.0 / `GCAT`вҶ’50.0 / `GGAN` (N excluded)вҶ’66.66666666666666; window count `вҢҠ(nвҲ’w)/stepвҢӢ+1`, offsets 0/step/2В·step, RNA U = non-GC, every window bounded `[0,100]`, `windowSize>length`/null/emptyвҶ’empty profile, case-insensitive. One open ASSUMPTION (all-N window вҮ’ A+T+G+C=0 division by zero вҶ’ GC% **0**, mirroring sibling `GcSkewCalculator`; not dictated by the external sources) вҖ” the N-exclusion denominator is source-backed (`remove` mode), not assumed; no source contradictions. Enriches [[windowed-gc-profile-and-variance]].
- [[seq-hydro-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-HYDRO-001 (**hydrophobicity analysis** вҖ” the whole-sequence **Kyte-Doolittle GRAVY index** `ОЈ(kd value)/length` and the **sliding-window hydropathy profile**, exactly `NвҲ’W+1` unweighted window means). Genuinely distinct SEQ-\* protein-property unit вҶ’ NEW concept [[hydrophobicity-gravy-and-profile]] (the whole-sequence-scalar + raw-profile sibling that the segment-calling [[transmembrane-helix-prediction]] thresholds). Sources: Biopython `ProtParamData.py` kd scale (20 residues I 4.5вҖҰR вҲ’4.5, Kyte & Doolittle 1982) + `ProtParam.py` (`gravy()` = total/length, `protein_scale` loop `range(NвҲ’W+1)`, default `edge=1.0` = unweighted mean) + Expasy ProtParam (GRAVY = ОЈ hydropathy Г· residues; positive вҮ’ hydrophobic) + GCAT/Davidson (window 9 surface, window 19 transmembrane peaks > 1.6) + alakazam (CRAN) `gravy`. Hand-derived oracles `A`вҶ’1.8 / `AG`вҶ’0.7 / `FLIV`вҶ’3.825 / `RKDE`вҶ’вҲ’3.85; window-3 `FLIV`вҶ’[3.7, 4.1666666667], `AG` (W>N)вҶ’empty; case-insensitive, empty/null вҶ’ 0/empty. One documented deviation (unknown residues **skipped** вҖ” GRAVY Г· recognized count, profile treats as 0 вҖ” vs Biopython `gravy()` `KeyError`; neither mandated by the kd sources, in-alphabet values stay exactly source-conformant, algorithm doc В§5.4); no source contradictions.

- [[seq-mw-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-MW-001 (**molecular weight calculation** вҖ” the average-isotopic **molecular mass in Daltons** of a **protein, DNA or RNA** sequence via one shared polymerization formula). Genuinely distinct SEQ-\* whole-sequence-scalar unit (mass, spanning all three molecule types) вҶ’ NEW concept [[molecular-weight]], the mass-weighted sibling of the [[base-composition]] tally and of the [[hydrophobicity-gravy-and-profile]] GRAVY scalar. Formula fully sourced: Biopython `Bio.SeqUtils.molecular_weight` (`weight = ОЈ weight_table[x] вҲ’ (lenвҲ’1)В·water`, one water removed per bond вҖ” peptide for protein, phosphodiester for nucleic acid; `water = 18.0153` avg / `18.010565` monoisotopic; single monomer вҮ’ free-monomer mass, circular вҮ’ вҲ’one more water, double-strand adds the complement strand, **error for protein**; "only unambiguous letters", nucleotides assumed 5'-phosphate) + Biopython `IUPACData` average tables ("from PubChem": protein *free-amino-acid* A 89.0932вҖҰG 75.0666вҖҰW 204.2252; DNA *monophosphate* A 331.2218/C 307.1971/G 347.2212/T 322.2085; RNA A 347.2212/C 323.1965/G 363.2206/U 324.1813) + Expasy Compute pI/Mw (protein Mw = "addition of average isotopic masses of amino acids ... and ... one water molecule", Da вҖ” algebraically = `ОЈ free-amino-acid вҲ’ (lenвҲ’1)В·water`) + Expasy ProtParam (delegates to Compute pI/Mw) + Expasy FindMod (residue-mass table + HвӮӮO 18.01524). Re-derived oracles (avg tables, water 18.0153) `AGC`вҶ’protein **249.29** / DNA **949.61** / RNA **997.61** (Biopython docstring), single monomer (zero bonds вҮ’ free-monomer mass) `G`вҶ’**75.0666** / `A` DNAвҶ’**331.2218** / `A` RNAвҶ’**347.2212**; empty/nullвҶ’0. One documented deviation (unknown/ambiguous symbols **skipped** вҖ” contribute no mass and no bond, reflecting only recognized monomers, no invented average вҖ” whereas Biopython *rejects* them; the SEQ-\* skip-unknown convention, an API-shape choice, in-alphabet values stay exactly source-conformant) + two API-shape assumptions (ToUpperInvariant case-fold; the skip resolution); no source contradictions (Expasy/Biopython agree on formula and average-mass tables to rounding). Note MW pairs with pI in the Expasy source but **pI/charge is a separate calculation not in this unit**.
- [[seq-pi-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-PI-001 (**isoelectric point (pI)** вҖ” the **pH at which a protein's net charge is zero**, found by bisecting the HendersonвҖ“Hasselbalch net-charge function over [0,14]). Genuinely distinct SEQ-\* protein-property scalar (a charge/pH calculation, not mass or hydropathy) вҶ’ NEW concept [[isoelectric-point]], the ExPASy Compute pI/Mw partner of [[molecular-weight]]. Charge model fully sourced: Osorio et al. 2015 Peptides `charge_pI.cpp` (net charge `ОЈ_basic +1/(1+10^(pHвҲ’pKa)) + ОЈ_acidic вҲ’1/(1+10^(pKaвҲ’pH))`, Moore 1985; basic {R,K,H,N-term} / acidic {D,E,C,Y,C-term}, both termini once) + EMBOSS `iep` (pI = net-charge-zero pH, `Epk.dat` scale N-term 8.6/C-term 3.6/C 8.5/D 3.9/E 4.1/H 6.5/K 10.8/R 12.5/Y 10.1, [0,14] bracket, "no electrostatic interactions" вҮ’ composition-only/order-independent) + Peptides `charge()` (nine pKa scales; EMBOSS worked example `FLPVLAGLTPSIVPKLVCLLTKKC` net charge 3.037398/2.914112/0.7184524 @ pH 5/7/9) + seqinr `computePI` + ExPASy Compute pI/Mw (Bjellqvist 1993 scale; small/highly-basic-protein accuracy caveat; pairs pI with Mw). Derived-pI oracles (EMBOSS, bisection Вұ0.01): `A`/`AG`вҶ’6.10 (termini-only midpoint), `D`вҶ’3.75, `K`вҶ’9.70, `DDDD`вҶ’3.23, `KKKK`вҶ’11.27, `FLPVLAGLTPSIVPKLVCLLTKKC`вҶ’9.67 (basic), `ACDEFGHIKLMNPQRSTVWY`вҶ’7.36 (EMBOSS вү  seqinr Bjellqvist 6.78454 вҖ” scale-dependent). Two assumptions (empty/nullвҶ’7.0 input-guard; pKa scale = EMBOSS, a parameter choice not a deviation), pIвҲҲ[0,14] invariant, no source contradictions.
- [[seq-secstruct-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-SECSTRUCT-001 (**protein secondary structure prediction** вҖ” the **Chou-Fasman (1974/1978) PОұ/PОІ/Pt conformational propensities** evaluated as a generic **sliding-window mean-propensity profile**: for a window `W`, the arithmetic mean of each of the Оұ-helix/ОІ-sheet/ОІ-turn propensities over each window). Genuinely distinct SEQ-\* protein-property unit вҶ’ NEW concept [[protein-secondary-structure-chou-fasman]] (the conformational-propensity analogue of the [[hydrophobicity-gravy-and-profile]] hydropathy profile, sharing the exact `NвҲ’W+1` unweighted window-mean mechanism). Sources: Wikipedia ChouвҖ“Fasman (rank 4; nucleation rules 4-of-6-helix threshold 1.03 / 3-of-5-sheet 1.00 / turn вҲҸp_t cutoff 7.5e-3; ~50вҖ“60% Q3 / 29-protein caveat) + Kelley bioinfo lecture (rank 4; helix STEP 1вҖ“4 state machine, worked A 142/83 E 151/37) + CSB|SJU Jakubowski (rank 4; **Lys PОұ 1.16**) + Przytycka NCBI lecture (rank 4; **Lys 1.14 0.74 1.01**) + ravihansa3000/ChouFasman reference impl (rank 3; full 20-residue Pa/Pb/Pt integer table, **Lys 114**) + BMC Bioinformatics PMC1780123 (rank 1, peer-reviewed; restates rules, helix вҹЁPОұвҹ©>1.03 & >вҹЁPОІвҹ©). Hand-derived oracles: single-residue window = that residue's tuple (A 1.42/0.83/0.66, E 1.51/0.37/0.74, V 1.06/1.70/0.50, N 0.67/0.89/1.56, K 1.14/0.74/1.01); `AE` W2 вҶ’ helix 1.465 / sheet 0.60 / turn 0.70; `AEV` W3 вҶ’ helix 1.330 / sheet 0.9666вҖҰ / turn 0.6333вҖҰ; `AXE` W3 averages only A+E; NвҲ’W+1 windows in N-terminus order, case-insensitive, W>N/non-positive/null/empty вҶ’ empty. Three assumptions (the method under test is the generic **profile not** the nucleation/extension state machine, so default `W=7` is an API convenience not a CF constant; unknown residues **skip-and-excluded**; the **only contested value Lys PОұ resolved to 1.14** вҖ” two independent sources incl. the reference impl vs a single 1.16), no contradictions on the 19 uncontested residues.
- [[seq-stats-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-STATS-001 (**the ORIGINAL sequence-composition umbrella** вҖ” nucleotide composition A/T/G/C/U/N/Other + Length, **GC content** `(G+C)/(A+T+G+C+U)`, **GC skew** `(GвҲ’C)/(G+C)` and **AT skew** `(AвҲ’T)/(A+T)`; also `SummarizeNucleotideSequence` aggregator + `CalculateAminoAcidComposition`). Connective tissue for the piecemeal-ingested composition family: [[seq-composition-001-evidence]] is a later duplicate/consolidated registry entry over the two composition methods first delivered here, [[seq-atskew-001-evidence]] split out the AT-skew member, and [[windowed-gc-profile-and-variance|SEQ-GC-ANALYSIS-001]] re-bundled both skews windowed. Sources: Biopython `gc_fraction`/`GC_skew` (rank 3; `gc/length`вҲҲ[0,1], emptyвҮ’0, case-insensitive, `ZeroDivisionError`вҮ’skew 0.0) + Wikipedia "GC skew" (rank 4; both formulas, sign convention) + Lobry 1996 *MBE* 13(5):660 (rank 1, primary вҖ” intra-strand base asymmetry). Worked oracles `ATGC`вҶ’GC 0.5/skews 0, `GGGC`вҶ’GC 1.0/GC skew 0.5/AT skew 0, `AAAT`вҶ’GC 0.0/GC skew 0/AT skew 0.5, `GCCC`вҶ’GC skew вҲ’0.5, `AAUUGGCC`вҶ’GC 0.5/AT skew 1.0; emptyвҮ’all-zero, zero-denominator skewsвҮ’0.0, case-insensitive; one ASSUMPTION (degenerate IUPAC codes excluded from GC/AT totals вҖ” agrees with Biopython over {A,T,G,C,U}), no contradictions. **No new concept** вҖ” synthesized on existing [[base-composition]] (composition + GC content) and [[nucleotide-composition-skew]] (both skews).
- [[seq-summary-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-SUMMARY-001 (**`SummarizeNucleotideSequence` вҖ” the per-sequence summary record**: bundles Length, nucleotide Composition (A/T/G/C/U/N), **GcContent** `(G+C)/(A+T+G+C+U)`, **Shannon Entropy** `вҲ’ОЈpбөўlogвӮӮpбөў` bits, **linguistic Complexity**, and **MeltingTemperature** (Wallace len<14 / GC-Marmur-Doty lenвүҘ14) into one object). A **pure aggregation** вҖ” each field MUST equal its canonical per-metric method on the identical input, so **no new concept**: composition/GC вҶ’ [[base-composition]], entropy вҶ’ [[seq-entropy-profile-001-evidence]]/[[windowed-sequence-complexity-profile]], linguistic complexity вҶ’ [[windowed-sequence-complexity-profile]], Tm вҶ’ [[primer-dimer-thermodynamics-tm]] (legacy Wallace/Marmur default, SEQ-TM-001). Sources: Biopython `gc_fraction` + `MeltingTemp` (Wallace `4(G+C)+2(A+T)` / Marmur-Doty `69.3+0.41В·%GCвҲ’650/N`) + Wikipedia Shannon (base-2вҮ’bits, max logвӮӮn) + Wikipedia linguistic complexity (Trifonov 1990, `C=вҲҸUбөў`, 0<C<1). Oracles `ATGCATGC`вҶ’GcContent 0.5/Entropy 2.0/Tm 24.0/Complexity 0.83968вҖҰ, 16-mer `ATGCATGCATGCATGC`вҶ’Tm 43.375 (GC branch, lenвүҘ14); empty/nullвҮ’zero summary, case-insensitive. One ASSUMPTION (Tm threshold len<14 = SEQ-TM-001 `WallaceMaxLength`, non-correctness-affecting for the summary's equality contract), no contradictions. **Corrects** the earlier "thin GC wrapper" description of `SummarizeNucleotideSequence` on [[base-composition]]/[[seq-stats-001-evidence]] вҖ” it is a full per-sequence statistics record.
- [[seq-thermo-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-THERMO-001 (**DNA duplex thermodynamics** вҖ” the full nearest-neighbor **О”HВ°/О”SВ°/О”GВ°/Tm** 4-tuple of a Watson-Crick DNA duplex, a port of Biopython `Tm_NN` over the **DNA_NN3 / Allawi & SantaLucia 1997** table). Genuinely distinct SEQ-\* full-tuple thermodynamics engine вҶ’ NEW concept [[dna-duplex-nearest-neighbor-thermodynamics]] (neither the legacy Wallace/Marmur scalar Tm nor the 2004-unified PCR-primer engine [[primer-dimer-thermodynamics-tm]]). Sources: Biopython `MeltingTemp.Tm_NN` (rank 3; DNA_NN3 table verbatim, two-terminus init counted off `seq[0]+seq[-1]`, `Tm=(1000В·О”H)/(О”S+RВ·ln k)вҲ’273.15` with `k=(dnac1вҲ’dnac2/2)В·1eвҲ’9`, default 25 nM each вҮ’ k=C_T/4, salt method 5 `0.368В·(lenвҲ’1)В·ln[Na]`, docstring `CGTTCCAAAGATGTGGGCATGAGCTTAC`вҶ’60.32 В°C) + MELTING 5 User Guide (rank 3; Tm eq В§4.2, F-factor 1/4 В§4.3, default model "all97") + Wikipedia Nucleic acid thermodynamics (rank 4, cites SantaLucia 1998; per-terminus init corroboration). Oracles `GCGC`вҶ’О”H вҲ’30.0/О”S вҲ’84.91/О”G вҲ’3.67/Tm вҲ’18.6, `ATCG`вҶ’О”H вҲ’23.6/О”S вҲ’71.81, length<2 вҮ’ `(0,0,0,0)`, case-insensitive; zero correctness-affecting assumptions (only the length<2 API convention), no source contradictions.
- [[seq-tm-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-TM-001 (**`CalculateMeltingTemperature` вҖ” the standalone scalar melting temperature**, length-dispatched at `ThermoConstants.WallaceMaxLength = 14` between the **Wallace rule** `4(G+C)+2(A+T)` for short oligos and the **Marmur-Doty GC formula** `64.9+41В·(GCвҲ’16.4)/N` for lenвүҘ14). A **%GC rule of thumb carrying no О”HВ°/О”SВ°/О”GВ°** вҶ’ NEW concept [[melting-temperature]] (the **third distinct Tm surface** and the canonical home of the Wallace/Marmur formulas, previously only sketched as the legacy default on [[primer-dimer-thermodynamics-tm]]). Sources: Biopython `MeltingTemp` `Tm_Wallace` (`4(G+C)+2(A+T)`, "rule of thumb 14вҖ“20 nt", `ACGTTGCAATGCCGTA`вҶ’48.0) + `Tm_GC` (general form `A+BВ·%GCвҲ’C/N+saltвҲ’DВ·%mismatch`; valueset-1 `69.3+0.41В·%GCвҲ’650/N` Marmur-Doty, valueset-2 QuikChange `81.5+вҖҰвҲ’675/N`); the same evidence file's NN/`Tm_NN`/SantaLucia-1998 datasets belong to SEQ-THERMO-001. Oracles Wallace `ACGTTGCAATGCCGTA`вҶ’48.0 / `ATGCATGC`вҶ’24.0, Marmur-Doty `GCGCGCGCGCATATATATAT`вҶ’51.78 / 16-mer `ATGCATGCATGCATGC`вҶ’43.375; empty/nullвҶ’0, case-insensitive. **Consolidation note:** SEQ-TM-001 is a duplicate/consolidated Registry entry over the two methods already delivered under SEQ-THERMO-001 (`CalculateMeltingTemperature` here + `CalculateThermodynamics` вҶ’ [[dna-duplex-nearest-neighbor-thermodynamics]]) вҖ” consolidated not re-implemented (TestSpec В§7). One ASSUMPTION (14-nt dispatch boundary, non-correctness-affecting under explicit flag) + NN-facet default C_T assumption + repo-vs-Biopython Marmur-Doty constant variant (64.9/вҲ’672.4 vs 69.3/вҲ’650); no source contradictions. Resolves the "SEQ-TM-001 remains un-ingested / natural home for Wallace/Marmur" follow-up flagged by the SEQ-SUMMARY-001 and SEQ-THERMO-001 ingests.
