- [[seq-replication-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-REPLICATION-001 (**replication origin prediction via the cumulative GC-skew minimum** вҖ” the classic ori-finder: integrate an *integer* running skew (G:+1, C:вҲ’1, A/T:0, `Skew_0=0`, prefix indices `[0,n]`) and read origin off the global **minimum**, terminus off the **maximum**): Rosalind BA1F Minimum Skew Problem (rank 3, canonical worked example вҖ” 100-nt sample min вҲ’4 @ positions **53, 97**, re-derived in-session exactly) + Grigoriev 1998 *Nucleic Acids Res* 26(10):2286 (rank 1 вҖ” cumulative diagram min=origin/max=terminus, extrema вүҲ half chromosome apart, leading strand G-rich) + Lobry 1996 (PMID 8676740 вҖ” skew sign flips at origin/terminus) + Wikipedia "GC skew" (max=terminal/min=origin); diagram oracles `CCGGGG`вҶ’`0,вҲ’1,вҲ’2,вҲ’1,0,+1,+2` (min вҲ’2 @2/max +2 @6), `GGGCCC`вҶ’`0,+1,+2,+3,+2,+1,0`, `AATT`вҶ’flat; `PredictedOrigin=53` first-minimizer tie-break; one documented ASSUMPTION вҖ” `IsSignificant` redefined threshold-free as `max>min` (invented `amplitude>countГ—0.01` constant **removed**), flat diagram вҮ’ origin=terminus=0/false; no source contradictions. New concept [[replication-origin-cumulative-skew]] (the distinct cumulative-integration + argmin/argmax *locator*, vs the scalar/windowed skew).
- [[seq-rnacomp-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-RNACOMP-001 (**RNA-specific per-base complement** вҖ” `GetRnaComplementBase`, the IUPAC-complete RNA complement map; **RNACOMP вү  composition**, this is complement chemistry, not the [[base-composition]] tally). **No new concept** вҖ” enriched [[rna-base-pairing]] (which already owns the RNA base complement `GetComplement`, RNA-PAIR-001): added a *SEQ-family full-IUPAC RNA complement* subsection. Same chemistry as `RnaSecondaryStructure.GetComplement` but IUPAC-complete (AвҶ’U/UвҶ’A/GвҶ’C/CвҶ’G, **TвҶ’A** treating DNA T as U; reciprocal RвҶ”Y/MвҶ”K/DвҶ”H/BвҶ”V; self-complementary W/S/X/N; non-IUPAC pass-through). RNA sibling of DNA `GetComplementBase` (SEQ-COMP-001, not yet ingested); distinct from DNA path (`GetRnaComplementBase('A')='U'` vs `GetComplementBase('A')='T'`). Sources: Biopython `IUPACData.py`/`Seq.py`/API docs (`ambiguous_rna_complement` = `ambiguous_dna_complement` with TвҶ’U; "any T is treated as a U") + bioinformatics.org SMS + NC-IUB 1984 (Cornish-Bowden 1985). One deviation: recognized bases returned **uppercase** (repo convention vs Biopython case-preserving) вҖ” casing only, complement identity unchanged; no source contradictions.
- [[splice-acceptor-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit SPLICE-ACCEPTOR-001 (**acceptor / 3' splice site detection** вҖ” score candidate `AG` dinucleotides for the three cis-elements of a real 3'ss under the canonical **GU-AG rule**). First ingested member of the **splicing** family вҶ’ NEW concept [[splice-acceptor-site-prediction]]. Three scoring surfaces: default `FindAcceptorSites` (**AcceptorPwm** PWM + PPT-quality, `(score/(count+1)+2)/4` [0,1] heuristic; weights from Shapiro & Senapathy 1987), opt-in `FindAcceptorBranchPoint` (18вҖ“40 nt window for the human **`yUnAy`** consensus, Gao 2008 conservation y@вҲ’3 0.790/U@вҲ’2 0.746/A@0 0.923/y@+1 0.751, found вүҘ 0.8В·3.210; Mercer 2015 corroboration), opt-in **MaxEntScan score3ss** `ScoreAcceptorMaxEnt` (Yeo & Burge 2004 23-nt max-entropy model; MIT-licensed maxentpy 82,560-record tables `Data/maxent_score3.txt`; canonical `ttccaaacgaacttttgtAGgga`вҶ’**2.89** cross-check, +8.19/вҲ’0.08); U12 **YCCAC** non-canonical scoring (Hall & Padgett 1994). Corner cases: < 20 nt вҶ’ empty guard, no-AG вҶ’ empty, cryptic intronic AG decoys, weak PPT skipped. All prior assumptions RESOLVED (PWM weights verified, normalization = design choice, branch-point constants source-traceable). Licence flag: bundled MaxEntScan table is the MIT port, not the academic-terms Burge-lab Perl. No source contradictions.
- [[splice-donor-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit SPLICE-DONOR-001 (**donor / 5' splice site detection** вҖ” score candidate `GT/GU` dinucleotides for the almost-invariant `GU` intron start under the canonical **GU-AG rule**). Donor member of the **splicing** family вҶ’ NEW concept [[splice-donor-site-prediction]] (5' partner of [[splice-acceptor-site-prediction]]). Single contiguous **`MAG|GURAGU`** consensus (вҲ’3..+6; 0-G/+1-U ~100%, вҲ’1-G ~80% for U1 snRNP; **no branch point / PPT** вҖ” asymmetric with the acceptor). Two surfaces only: default **IUPAC consensus match-fraction** `FindDonorSites`/`ScoreDonorSite` (plainer than the acceptor PWM+PPT; GC donors self-penalize via the +1-U mismatch 8/9<9/9, old 0.7 penalty removed), opt-in **MaxEntScan score5ss** `ScoreDonorMaxEnt` (Yeo & Burge 2004 9-nt window, **single 16,384-entry table, no overlapping sub-windows** vs score3's 82,560 records; canonical `cagGTAAGT`вҶ’**10.86**, +11.08/вҲ’0.12). GC-AG (~0.5вҖ“1%) + U12 **AT-AC**/`ATATCC` non-canonical donors. Corner cases: < 9 nt вҶ’ empty, no GT/GU вҶ’ empty, cryptic donors. All prior assumptions RESOLVED (PWMвҶ’IUPAC binary weights, normalizationвҶ’match fraction, GC penalty removed). Licence flag: bundled MaxEntScan table is the MIT port, not the academic-terms Burge-lab Perl. No source contradictions.
- [[sv-breakpoint-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit SV-BREAKPOINT-001 (**breakpoint detection from split / soft-clipped reads**). First ingested member of the **germline structural-variant (SV)** family вҶ’ NEW concept [[breakpoint-detection-split-reads]]. Localize an SV breakpoint to a single base at the aligned/clipped **junction** of a split read: the SAM/BAM CIGAR **soft clip `S` consumes the read (SEQ) but not the reference** and sits only at a read end вҶ’ **leading `S` = left / trailing `S` = right breakpoint** (ClipCrop "marginal point between clipped and matched sequence"; L/R-breakpoints; a no-`S` read = no signal). **Cluster** per-read junctions under three source-backed constraints вҖ” positional **tolerance** (ClipCrop "clustered within 5-base differences", 5 b), **minimum support** (SoftSearch вүҘ x soft-clipped reads at a position, default 5 / configurable 2; support = # clipped reads in cluster), and **same clip-side + same chromosome** вҖ” with a **min clip length** filter (вүӨ 5 clipped bases dropped) and `RefineBreakpoint`. Repository `SplitRead` record: `PrimaryPosition` = anchored SAM POS / `SupplementaryPosition` = junction coordinate / `ClipLength`. Oracles: 3 reads @ 5000 Вұ вүӨ 5 b, same chr, support вүҘ 2 вҶ’ one breakpoint ~5000; 1 isolated read вҶ’ none; 5000 vs 5100 (gap > tolerance) вҶ’ two below-support groups вҶ’ none. Sources: SAM/BAM spec (samtools/hts-specs, rank 2 вҖ” CIGAR consume table / POS / S-at-ends) + Tattini-Magi 2015 review (rank 1 вҖ” anchored+imprecise split read, single-base resolution, clustering) + ClipCrop Suzuki 2011 (rank 1 вҖ” junction=breakpoint, 5-b clustering, L/R) + SoftSearch Hart 2013 (rank 1 вҖ” вүҘ x clipped reads, orientation combining, min clip > 5). One ASSUMPTION (cluster reported coordinate = rounded **mean** of member junctions, sub-tolerance only, mirroring sibling `ClusterSplitReads`); operates on already-extracted `SplitRead` records, not raw BAM. Orthogonal to the oncology read-evidence [[gene-fusion-detection-read-evidence]] / [[chromothripsis-inference]]. No source contradictions.
- [[sv-cnv-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit SV-CNV-001 (**read-depth copy-number variation detection**). The **read-depth-segmentation member of the germline structural-variant (SV) family** вҶ’ NEW concept [[read-depth-cnv-segmentation]] (a distinct method from the split-read anchor [[breakpoint-detection-split-reads]] вҖ” aggregate **read depth of coverage**, not per-read junctions). Pipeline: **read depth вҲқ copy number** (Yoon 2009) вҶ’ **windowed counting** (non-overlapping fixed-size windows, one read per start position, per-window mean RD) вҶ’ optional **GC correction** `r_i' = r_iВ·m/m_GC` вҶ’ **log2 ratio** `log2(observed depth / reference depth)` (reference = overall median of window means when no baseline given) вҶ’ **integer CN = round(2В·2^log2)** (CNVkit "round" method, diploid ploidy 2) вҶ’ **del/dup call** + segment merge (`DetectCNV`/`SegmentCopyNumber`). Diploid anchors (verbatim CNVkit): 0.5Г—вҶ’log2 вҲ’1.0вҶ’CN 1 (Deletion), 1.0Г—вҶ’0вҶ’CN 2 (Neutral), 1.5Г—вҶ’+0.585вҶ’CN 3 (Duplication/gain), 2.0Г—вҶ’+1.0вҶ’CN 4 (amp). Corner cases: **zero-depth window вҶ’ no-call** (log2(0)=вҲ’вҲһ undefined, homozygous-deletion candidate, not вҲ’вҲһ); **NaN log2 вҶ’ Neutral (CN 2)**; CN clamped **вүҘ 0**. Sources: Yoon 2009 (Genome Res, rank 1 вҖ” RDвҲқCN, windowed counting, GC formula) + CNVkit `call.py` + calling docs (rank 3 вҖ” `n=ref_copiesВ·2^log2`, anchors log2(1/2)=вҲ’1 / log2(3/2)=0.585, `max(0,ncopies)` clamp, `nan`вҶ’neutral). Two ASSUMPTIONs (reference baseline = overall median of non-zero window means; diploid ploidy 2), both source-supported. The oncology [[copy-number-alteration-classification]] (ONCO-CNA-001) is the classification layer *on top of* this same log2 ratio (swaps `round` for hard-threshold binning into 5 CNA states). Research-grade, not for clinical use. No source contradictions.
- [[sv-detect-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit SV-DETECT-001 (**structural-variant detection from paired-end mapping (PEM) signatures** вҖ” discordant read pairs). The **discordant-read-pair member of the germline structural-variant (SV) family** вҶ’ NEW concept [[discordant-pair-sv-detection]] (a third read-evidence channel, orthogonal to the split-read anchor [[breakpoint-detection-split-reads]] and the depth-based [[read-depth-cnv-segmentation]]). Read how a mate pair's mapped **span + orientation** deviate from the concordant **FR** proper pair (SAM FLAG 0x02; **RF is everted/discordant**, not proper) and classify the SV type: span `> Ој+cВ·Пғ` (FR, same chr) вҶ’ **Deletion**, span `< ОјвҲ’cВ·Пғ` вҶ’ **Insertion**, **FF/RR** вҶ’ **Inversion**, everted **RF** вҶ’ **tandem Duplication**, mates on **different chromosomes** вҶ’ **Translocation**. Span cutoff = `c` s.d. of the empirical insert-size distribution (BreakDancer `-c`, default 3 вҮ’ mean=400/sd=50 вҮ’ bounds [250,550]); **signature-then-cluster** with **min support** вүҘ `-r` pairs (default 2). Corner cases: an insertion larger than the insert size is invisible to PEM span and its sequence is not recovered (split-read channel's job); below-support clusters dropped; cutoff bounds exact. One ASSUMPTION вҖ” inter-chromosomal (translocation) precedence evaluated **before** orientation (inversion defined only for intra-chromosomal flipped pairs). Sources: Medvedev/Stanciu/Brudno 2009 (Nat Methods, rank 1 вҖ” signature catalogue) + BreakDancer README + protocol (Chen 2009 / Fan 2014 вҖ” s.d. cutoff, min support, DEL/INS/INV/ITX/CTX codes) + SAM/BWA proper-pair FR convention (cureffi/FLAG 0x02) + DELLY 2012 / SVXplorer 2020 (orientationвҶ’type: RF=dup, FF/RR=inv). Consumes already-mapped read-pair records, not raw BAM; research-grade, not for clinical use. No source contradictions.
- [[trans-diff-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit TRANS-DIFF-001 (**two-group RNA-seq differential expression** вҖ” log2 fold change + Welch's t-test + Benjamini-Hochberg FDR). **First ingested unit of the Transcriptome / RNA-seq family** вҶ’ NEW concept [[differential-expression]]. `TranscriptomeAnalyzer.CalculateFoldChange` / `FindDifferentiallyExpressed`: **log2FC** `log2((mean(treatment)+c)/(mean(control)+c))` (pseudocount c=1, positive = up in treatment, DESeq2 Love 2014 + Science Park lesson) + a **Welch unequal-variance t-test** raw p `t=(XМ„вӮӮвҲ’XМ„вӮҒ)/вҲҡ(sвӮҒВІ/NвӮҒ+sвӮӮВІ/NвӮӮ)`, unbiased (NвҲ’1) variances, Welch-Satterthwaite df, exact Student-t tail `p=I_{ОҪ/(ОҪ+tВІ)}(ОҪ/2,ВҪ)` via regularized incomplete beta (Welch 1947) + **Benjamini-Hochberg FDR** reproducing R `p.adjust(method="BH")` `pmin(1,cummin(n/iВ·p[o]))[ro]` (BH 1995). DE вҮ” **two-criterion gate** `|log2FC| вүҘ threshold (default 1.0) AND adjusted p < alpha (default 0.05)`. Oracles: UP `log2(41/11)=+1.8981204вҖҰ` / DOWN вҲ’1.8981204вҖҰ / FLAT 0; Welch {1,2,3} vs {7,8,9} вҶ’ t=7.348469, ОҪ=4, p=0.0018262607 (SciPy cross-check); BH raw (0.001,0.4,0.5,0.9) вҶ’ adj (0.004,0.6667,0.6667,0.9). Corner cases: <2 replicates вҶ’ p=1; se=0 вҶ’ p=1 (equal means)/p=0 (unequal); zero mean вҶ’ pseudocount. Three source-backed ASSUMPTIONs (pseudocount 1, <2-replicate p=1, se=0 conventions). A **simple two-group** estimator, **not** the full DESeq2 negative-binomial GLM. `alternative_to` the rank-sum [[significant-taxa-detection]] (no built-in FDR); DE gene lists feed [[pathway-enrichment-ora]]. Research-grade, not for clinical use. No source contradictions.
- [[trans-expr-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit TRANS-EXPR-001 (**RNA-seq expression quantification** вҖ” TPM / FPKM / RPKM + quantile normalization). **Transcriptome / RNA-seq family** sibling of the anchor [[differential-expression]] вҶ’ NEW concept [[expression-quantification]] (a distinct quantification/normalization method, upstream of the DE test). `TranscriptomeAnalyzer.CalculateTPM` / `CalculateFPKM` / `QuantileNormalize`: **TPM** `(X_i/l_i)/ОЈ(X_j/l_j)В·10вҒ¶` (length-normalize into RPK **then** rescale so each sample **sums to exactly 10вҒ¶** вҖ” the invariant RPKM lacks; Wagner 2012, Zhao/Ye/Stanton 2020); **FPKM/RPKM** `X_iВ·10вҒ№/(l_iВ·N)` (per-kb + per-million-reads; RPKMвүЎFPKM formula; `TPM=FPKM/ОЈ FPKMВ·10вҒ¶`); **quantile normalization** (Bolstad 2003 вҖ” sort each column, set each rank to the cross-column rank mean, re-place; **tied values get the mean of the rank means they'd span**). Oracles: TPM A(10,2000)/B(20,4000)/C(30,1000) вҶ’ **(125000,125000,750000)** sum 10вҒ¶; FPKM X=1000,l=2000,N=10вҒ¶ вҶ’ **500**; quantile C1=(5,2,3,4)/C2=(4,1,4,2)/C3=(3,4,6,8) вҶ’ C2's two tied `4`s вҶ’ **5.166вҖҰ** (mean of top-two rank means 4.666вҖҰ/5.666вҖҰ). Corner cases: all-zero counts вҶ’ TPM 0/0 undefined вҶ’ emit 0; non-positive length/N вҶ’ FPKM 0; empty вҶ’ empty. Two source-backed ASSUMPTIONs (all-zero TPM вҶ’ 0; effective length = annotated length). Classic count-normalization, **not** an effective-length fragment model (kallisto/salmon) or TMM/median-of-ratios size factors (edgeR/DESeq2). TPM/RPKM are within-sample relative measures вҖ” misused across samples (Zhao 2020). Research-grade, not for clinical use. No source contradictions.
- [[trans-splice-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit TRANS-SPLICE-001 (**RNA-seq alternative / differential splicing** вҖ” event classification + Percent-Spliced-In / PSI). **Transcriptome / RNA-seq family** sibling of the anchor [[differential-expression]] вҶ’ NEW concept [[alternative-splicing-psi]] (read-quantification of splicing usage вҖ” **distinct from** the genomic splice-site motif predictors [[splice-donor-site-prediction]] / [[splice-acceptor-site-prediction]] / [[gene-structure-prediction-intron-exon]]). `TranscriptomeAnalyzer.CalculatePSI` / `DetectAlternativeSplicing`: **PSI** `ОЁ = I/(I+S)` (inclusion / (inclusion+exclusion) reads; Wang 2008, PMC3330053, SUPPA2) with opt-in **rMATS length-normalized** `ПҲМӮ = (I/lбөў)/(I/lбөў + S/lвӮӣ)` (Shen 2014, effective isoform lengths) вҶ’ default unnormalized, switches to rMATS when both lengths > 0; **О”PSI** = splicing-level differential readout. **Five canonical AS classes** (Wang 2008 = rMATS codes): SkippedExon (SE), RetainedIntron (RI), AlternativeFivePrimeSS (A5SS, alternative **donor** = moving 3вҖІ/END boundary of upstream exon), AlternativeThreePrimeSS (A3SS, alternative **acceptor** = moving 5вҖІ/START boundary of downstream exon), MutuallyExclusiveExons (MXE); an event needs **вүҘ2 isoforms** of one gene. Oracles: (I=80,S=20) вҶ’ **0.80**; (80,20,lбөў=200,lвӮӣ=100) вҶ’ **0.6666вҖҰ**. Corner cases: **0/0 вҶ’ NaN**, S=0 вҶ’ PSI 1, I=0 вҶ’ PSI 0, `0 вүӨ PSI вүӨ 1`, <2 isoforms вҶ’ no event. Two source-backed ASSUMPTIONs (length normalization opt-in; forward strand / ascending coords). The splicing-level counterpart to the gene-level [[differential-expression]] вҖ” a gene can be differentially spliced without changing total expression. Read-count ratio + coordinate comparison, **not** the full rMATS/SUPPA2 replicate statistics. Research-grade, not for clinical use. No source contradictions.
- [[splice-predict-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit SPLICE-PREDICT-001 (**gene structure prediction вҖ” intron/exon**), the **composite / umbrella** of the **splicing** family вҶ’ NEW concept [[gene-structure-prediction-intron-exon]]. Assembles the two boundary detectors into a whole split-gene model: find donors (`GT/GU`) + acceptors (`AG`) вҶ’ **pair** into introns under the **GT-AG rule** (Breathnach & Chambon 1981 `MAG|GURAGU` / `(Y)nNCAG|G`; Burge 1999 "each donor pairs with exactly one acceptor") bounded by `minIntronLength` (default 60) / `maxIntronLength` вҶ’ **greedy non-overlapping** selection вҶ’ exons = the gaps вҶ’ **type** each exon (Initial/Internal/Terminal/Single, Gilbert 1978) + **phase** = `(ОЈ preceding exon lengths) mod 3` (Alberts 2002) вҶ’ emit **spliced sequence** + **overall score** = mean of per-intron `(donor+acceptor)/2`, [0,1]. Datasets: D1 two-exon 153 nt вҶ’ 1 intron/2 exons/70-nt spliced, D2 single-exon 50 nt вҶ’ Single, D3 empty вҶ’ 0/0. Corner cases: 30-bp introns excluded by default min=60, no sites вҶ’ single-exon, DNA TвүЎU. All 4 assumptions RESOLVED (greedy=design decision, phase=trivial, overall-score=definition, **default branch-point 0.3 constant removed**). No source contradictions.
- [[variant-annot-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit VARIANT-ANNOT-001 (**variant annotation** вҖ” VEP-style functional consequence + Sequence-Ontology IMPACT). The **interpretation / annotation** member of the variant-analysis family вҶ’ NEW concept [[variant-effect-annotation-vep]] (downstream of variant calling [[somatic-variant-calling-tumor-normal]], orthogonal to pathogenicity/tier classification). Ensembl **OverlapConsequence predicate system**: `Constants.pm` consequenceвҶ’IMPACTвҶ’rank table (**IMPACT stored on the term, not computed**; frameshift HIGH / missense MODERATE / synonymous LOW / intron MODIFIER) + `VariationEffect.pm` peptide predicates; **most-severe = lowest rank** (McLaren 2016 "most specific term under any parent"). The coding engine **translates ref/alt codons** through [[genetic-code-translation]] (NCBI Standard code table 1) and compares peptides: `synonymous` (ref_pep==alt_pep, no `X`, not stop_retained) / `missense` (differ, same length; false if start_lost/stop_lost/stop_gained/partial_codon) / `stop_gained` (alt gains `*`) / `stop_lost` (ref loses `*`) / **`frameshift` purely length-based `|altвҲ’ref| mod 3 вү  0`** / inframe ins-del (Г—3). Precedence stop_gained>missense, start_lost(rank 7)>coding-substitution. Oracles GAAвҶ’GTA missense/MODERATE В· TTAвҶ’TTG synonymous/LOW В· CAAвҶ’TAA stop_gained/HIGH В· TAAвҶ’CAA stop_lost/HIGH В· ATGвҶ’ATC start_lost/HIGH В· ACвҶ’A frameshift В· AвҶ’ATTT inframe_insertion. Sources McLaren 2016 (PMC4893825) + Ensembl Constants.pm/VariationEffect.pm (release/110) + NCBI gc.prt + Sequence Ontology (Eilbeck 2005). Two assumptions (Standard code table 1 only; single-codon SNV peptide comparison). Research-grade, not for clinical use. No source contradictions.
- [[variant-call-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit VARIANT-CALL-001 (**variant calling** вҖ” SNP/insertion/deletion detection from a referenceвҶ”query alignment + transition/transversion + Ti/Tv). The **calling / detection** member of the variant-analysis family вҶ’ NEW concept [[germline-variant-calling-snp-indel]] (**upstream of** annotation [[variant-effect-annotation-vep]]; the germline referenceвҶ”query counterpart of the oncology tumor-vs-normal caller [[somatic-variant-calling-tumor-normal]]). `CallVariantsFromAlignment` runs `SequenceAligner.GlobalAlign(reference,query)` and walks aligned columns: **SNP** (both bases differ), **Insertion** (`-`/base), **Deletion** (base/`-`), 0-based `Position` + `"-"` gap sentinel (in-memory model; VCF padding + 1-based POS only in serialized `ToVcfLines`). SNPs classified case-insensitively **Transition** (AвҶ”G, CвҶ”T) vs **Transversion** (AвҶ”C/AвҶ”T/GвҶ”C/GвҶ”T); **Ti/Tv = #Ti/#Tv**, undefined `#Tv=0` вҶ’ **0** by convention; non-SNP вҶ’ `Other`. Sources VCFv4.3 (samtools/hts-specs вҖ” REF/ALT/POS + padding-base grammar, В§1.1 `GвҶ’A` SNP / `GTCвҶ’G` 2-base del / `GTCвҶ’GTCT` 1-base ins) + Danecek 2011 (VCF classes) + Tan 2015 (normalized вҹә left-aligned+parsimonious) + Collins & Jukes 1994 (transitional bias, Ti rate > Tv rate). Three assumptions (gap-sentinel internal rep; indels **not** normalized вҶ’ position-only implementation-dependence in repeats; Ti/Tv zero вҶ’ 0). Alignment-based (single query vs reference), **not** a read-pileup genotype caller. Research-grade, not for clinical use. No source contradictions.
- [[variant-indel-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit VARIANT-INDEL-001 (**indel detection** вҖ” `FindInsertions` / `FindDeletions`, the insertion/deletion facet of the aligned-column caller). **Enriches** (does not fork) the concept [[germline-variant-calling-snp-indel]] вҖ” the indel facet of the same VARIANT-CALL-001 caller, not a separate algorithm. `FindInsertions`/`FindDeletions` are **filters over `CallVariants`** returning only their class (insertion column `-`/base, deletion column base/`-`); a multi-base indel = **consecutive per-base indel columns**. Load-bearing claim = the **directional length invariant**: **insertion вҮ’ ALT longer than REF** (VCF `CвҶ’CA`), **deletion вҮ’ REF longer than ALT** (VCF `TCвҶ’T`); VCFv4.3 В§1.1 `GTCвҶ’G,GTCT` shows both anchored at `G`. Normalization theory (Tan 2015 **normalized вҹә left-aligned + parsimonious**; Algorithm 1 = suffix-then-prefix trimming) documents the ASM: the caller reports the indel at the `GlobalAlign` column with **no** normalization pass, so **position** is implementation-dependent in repeats/low-complexity only (PharmCAT `AATGAвҶ’A`@97740414 вҮ’ `GATGAвҶ’G`@97740410, same count/type), **not** counts or types. Reference oracles: `ATGCAT`вҶ’`ATGTCAT` = 1-base insertion `T`; `ATGTCAT`вҶ’`ATGCAT` = 1-base deletion `T`; minimal_representation CFTR p.F508del `(7,117199646,CTT,-)вҶ’(...,ATCT,A)` + BRCA2 `(13,32914438,T,-)вҶ’(...,GT,G)` confirm deletion вҮ’ len(REF)>len(ALT) + left-anchor padding. Three assumptions (gap-sentinel internal rep; indels not normalized вҶ’ position-only in repeats; 0-based in-memory Position). Sources VCFv4.3 + Tan 2015 (PMID 25701572) + minimal_representation (Minikel) + PharmCAT. Research-grade, not for clinical use. No source contradictions.
- [[variant-snp-001-evidence]] вҖ” evidence artifact for test unit VARIANT-SNP-001 (**SNP detection** вҖ” `FindSnps` / `FindSnpsDirect`, the single-nucleotide-substitution facet of the aligned-column caller). **Enriches** (does not fork) the concept [[germline-variant-calling-snp-indel]] вҖ” the SNP facet of the same VARIANT-CALL-001 caller, not a separate algorithm (mirrors how [[variant-indel-001-evidence]] folded in the indel facet). Two entry points, **substitution columns only** (no indels): **`FindSnps`** = alignment-based filter over the caller (keeps columns where both bases differ, `Type=SNP`); **`FindSnpsDirect`** = positional / **Hamming-style** вҖ” over two **equal-length** sequences it enumerates exactly the **Hamming-mismatch positions** (Acharya 2017, PMC5410656) and the SNP count equals the **Hamming distance**. Each SNP: `Position=i` (0-based mismatched index), `ReferenceAllele=ref[i]`, `AlternateAllele=query[i]`, `ref[i]вү query[i]` (**REF==ALT is not a variant**). Load-bearing scope claim = the **equal-length precondition**: `FindSnpsDirect` on unequal-length inputs compares only the **common prefix** `min(ref.Length,query.Length)` вҖ” the trailing region is indel territory (VARIANT-INDEL-001), never a SNP. Identical sequences вҶ’ 0 SNPs (Hamming distance 0); comparison + Ti/Tv classification **case-insensitive** (VCFv4.3 REF alphabet A,C,G,T,N). Oracles: `ATGC`вҶ’`ATTC`={2} (GвҶ’T) В· `AAAA`вҶ’`TGTA`={0,1,2} В· VCFv4.3 В§1.1 simple SNP `GвҶ’A`@14370. Two assumptions (unequal-length вҶ’ common prefix; 0-based in-memory Position). Sources VCFv4.3 + Wikipedia/Futuyma Transversion + Acharya 2017 (PMC5410656, Hamming) + Collins & Jukes 1994 (transitional bias). Research-grade, not for clinical use. No source contradictions.
- [[genomic-repeat-001-report]] вҖ” validation report for GENOMIC-REPEAT-001 (LRS + all-repeats suffix-tree enumerator): Stage A PASS, Stage B FAILвҶ’FIXED, End-state CLEAN; fixed a real completeness defect where FindRepeats emitted only the maximal adjacent-pair LCP (ACGTACGTTTTTACGT@3 returned 5 of 8 true repeats), locked with a brute-force regression guard, suite 6571/0.
- [[meta-resist-001-report]] вҖ” validation report for META-RESIST-001 (ResFinder-style AMR gene detection): Stage A PASS-WITH-NOTES, Stage B PASS after in-session fix, State вң… CLEAN; fixed a BestUngappedMatch tie-break defect that padded windows with mismatches and caused a real false negative at 0.90/0.60 defaults (M3 strengthened, M3b edge-HSP guard added), suite 6556/0.
- [[mirna-pair-001-report]] вҖ” validation report for MIRNA-PAIR-001 (miRNA-target base pairing + antiparallel duplex): Stage A PASS, Stage B PASS-WITH-NOTES, End-state CLEAN; fixed CanPair/IsWobblePair not honouring the DNA-TвҶ’U contract plus a green-washed test, added NormalizeBase so the predicates (and delegating MCP tools) treat T as U, suite 6543/0.
- [[mirna-target-001-report]] вҖ” validation report for MIRNA-TARGET-001 (miRNA target-site prediction + TA_3UTR abundance): Stage A/B both PASS, State вң… CLEAN; the one non-overlapping-counting divergence (periodic seed cores over-counted) fixed in-session with a greedy scan + lock test CTX-TA-009, full suite 18861/0.
- [[pangen-core-001-report]] вҖ” validation report for PANGEN-CORE-001 (pan-genome core/accessory/unique partition + fluidity + open/closed): Stage A/B PASS-WITH-NOTES, State CLEAN; the floor core-threshold defect fixed to Roary's fractional 99% rule (occupancy/N вүҘ coreFraction) across code/tests/docs, fluidity & Heaps openness already correct, full suite 6509/0.
- [[parse-genbank-001-report]] вҖ” validation report for PARSE-GENBANK-001 (GenBank flat-file parser): Stage A PASS (INSDC 1-based-inclusive / complement / join-vs-order grammar faithful), Stage B PASS-WITH-NOTES, State CLEAN; multi-line qualifier reconstruction defect (spurious /translation space + unstripped opening quote) fixed to Biopython behaviour with 2 REDвҶ’GREEN tests, full suite 18213/0.
- [[protmotif-tm-001-report]] вҖ” validation report for PROTMOTIF-TM-001 (transmembrane helix prediction, Kyte-Doolittle hydropathy sliding window): Stage A PASS-WITH-NOTES / Stage B PASS, вң… CLEAN вҖ” fixed an off-by-one segment-End (residue outside every passing window), corrected across code/doc/Evidence/TestSpec, suite 6579/0.
- [[rna-partition-001-report]] вҖ” validation report for RNA-PARTITION-001 (RNA partition function, McCaskill 1990 + Boltzmann structure probability): Stage A PASS-WITH-NOTES / Stage B FAIL вҶ’ FIXED, вң… CLEAN вҖ” external-only base-pair probabilities corrected to the McCaskill outside recursion (matches brute force to 3.3e-16), docs fixed and nested-pair tests added; Z and structure probability already correct; suite 6596/0.
- [[seq-complex-compress-001-report]] вҖ” validation report for SEQ-COMPLEX-COMPRESS-001 (LempelвҖ“Ziv 1976 compression-based sequence complexity): Stage A PASS-WITH-NOTES / Stage B FAIL вҶ’ FIXED, вң… CLEAN вҖ” b<2 single-symbol normalization returned the raw count vs the cited reference's clamp-to-2 ("0"Г—16 вҶ’ 1.25, not 5.0); code fixed, test locked to the sourced value, coverage gaps closed; suite 6603/0.
- [[sv-cnv-001-report]] вҖ” validation report for SV-CNV-001 (read-depth CNV: windowed depth вҶ’ log2 ratio вҶ’ integer copy number): Stage A PASS / Stage B PASS-WITH-NOTES, вң… CLEAN вҖ” a round-half-away-from-zero rounding defect corrected to NumPy round-half-to-even (CNVkit parity), suite 6493/0.
- [[sv-detect-001-report]] вҖ” validation report for SV-DETECT-001 (paired-end-mapping SV detection: span + orientation вҶ’ SV type): Stage A / Stage B both PASS-WITH-NOTES, вң… CLEAN вҖ” the RF-everted signature corrected from "concordant" to a discordant tandem-Duplication (DELLY/SVXplorer), suite 6485/0.
- [[trans-splice-001-report]] вҖ” validation report for TRANS-SPLICE-001 (alternative-splicing event classification + Percent-Spliced-In): Stage A PASS-WITH-NOTES / Stage B FAILвҶ’fixed, вң… CLEAN вҖ” swapped A5SS/A3SS labels in ClassifyIsoformPair corrected against the rMATS convention, suite 6501/0.
- [[validation-verdicts]] вҖ” CLEAN validation-verdict registry: one row per per-unit report that found **no defect** (reports that found one get their own `[[<unit>-report]]` page instead), each linking the unit to its concept + Stage A/B state; see [[validation-ledger]] / [[validation-protocol]].

## Concepts

- [[three-front-doors]] вҖ” one algorithm engine exposed through skills, the C# API, and MCP, with identical results.
- [[skill-layer]] вҖ” the Agent-Skill routing + discipline layer that keeps 427 tool schemas out of the model's context.
- [[mcp-tool-catalog]] вҖ” reference map of all 427 MCP tools across 11 servers to the [[concept]] each thin wrapper delegates to (209 mapped / 218 unmapped, 120 concepts); replaces per-tool ingestion.
- [[layered-architecture]] вҖ” the strict up-only dependency layering (Levels 0вҖ“4) enforced by architecture tests.
- [[scientific-rigor]] вҖ” runtime honesty: `LimitationPolicy`, tool-only computation, provenance on every result.
- [[validation-and-testing]] вҖ” 22k+ tests across ten methodologies plus the per-unit validation campaign.
- [[validation-findings-disposition]] вҖ” the A/B/C/D triage governance process for validation findings, with green-washing detection and the spec-not-impl remedy.
- [[operating-envelope-and-limitation-policy]] вҖ” the validated operating envelope + the `LimitationPolicy` runtime guard (Strict/Moderate/Permissive, minimum-access-mode table) and the irreducible/data-blocked/scope limitation taxonomy.
- [[property-based-testing]] вҖ” P0 methodology (FsCheck): hundreds of generated inputs checked against expressible invariants (R/S/I/M/P/RT/D); 258/258.
- [[metamorphic-testing]] вҖ” P0 methodology: metamorphic relations across runs (SUB/MON/INV/SYM/COMP/SHIFT) that solve the oracle problem; 258/258, ~200+ relations.
- [[fuzzing]] вҖ” P2 methodology: random/malformed/boundary input for clean-failure; parsers the hot target; zeroвҶ’258/258.
- [[snapshot-testing]] вҖ” P1 methodology (Verify): golden-master `.verified.txt` regression capture; the least-complete methodology at 37/255.
- [[algebraic-testing]] вҖ” P1 methodology: explicit algebraic laws (identity/associativity/involution/round-tripвҖҰ); 89 applicable + 169 not-applicable.
- [[architecture-testing]] вҖ” P2 methodology (ArchUnitNET): 22 IL-level module rules enforcing the [[layered-architecture]] Dependency Rule; scales by module not algorithm.
- [[differential-testing]] вҖ” P2 methodology: two independent implementations cross-checked (ALT/BRUTE/REF/DUAL); 107/255.
- [[combinatorial-testing]] вҖ” P3 methodology: minimal pairwise parameter-interaction coverage; 193/255 + 65 not-applicable.
- [[characterization-testing]] вҖ” P3 methodology: golden-master pinning of behaviour before refactors (invariance, not correctness); on-demand.
- [[build-quality-gate]] вҖ” the build-time static-analysis gate: SonarAnalyzer ratcheted to blocking under `TreatWarningsAsErrors`, fix-or-silence, review-not-blind-fix.
- [[test-unit-registry]] вҖ” the area-prefixed Test Unit ID scheme and per-unit record behind the validation effort.
- [[definition-of-done]] вҖ” the six-criterion acceptance bar (TestSpec, tests, вүҘ80% coverage, edge cases, CI, evidence) each unit must clear.
- [[algorithm-validation-evidence]] вҖ” the templated per-unit `docs/Evidence/` artifact pattern (sources, worked-example dataset, deviations) behind the "Evidence documented" DoD criterion.
- [[global-alignment-needleman-wunsch]] вҖ” the canonical DP global-alignment algorithm (`GlobalAlign`): linear-gap recurrence, O(nm), traceback, affine-as-extension.
- [[multiple-sequence-alignment]] вҖ” aligning 3+ sequences (NP-complete): Seqeron's star (`MultipleAlign`), iterative-refinement (MUSCLE), and consistency (T-Coffee) aligners; sum-of-pairs + consensus.
- [[local-alignment-smith-waterman]] вҖ” the canonical DP local-alignment algorithm (`LocalAlign`): zero-floor linear-gap recurrence, 0/0 border, optimum from the max cell, traceback-to-zero вҶ’ best local subsequences; linear-gap only (affine/WвӮ– not implemented).
- [[semi-global-alignment-fitting]] вҖ” ends-free "glocal" alignment: fitting/query-in-reference variant (Rosalind SIMS); NW recurrence with free reference end gaps, traceback from max of last row.
- [[alignment-statistics]] вҖ” post-alignment metrics: percent identity/similarity/gaps (EMBOSS/BLAST convention, denominator includes gaps, positive-score вҮ’ similar) and srspair three-line markup.
- [[coding-potential-hexamer-score]] вҖ” CPAT hexamer usage-bias coding-potential score: mean of ln(coding/noncoding) over in-frame hexamers (wordSize 6/step 3), sign convention, Вұ1 pseudo-scores; Fickett TESTCODE as not-implemented alternative.
- [[prokaryotic-gene-prediction-rbs]] вҖ” annotation-layer prokaryotic ORF-based gene prediction + Shine-Dalgarno RBS detection (ANNOT-GENE-001, `GenomeAnnotator.PredictGenes` / `FindRibosomeBindingSitesBothStrands` / `ScanStrandForShineDalgarno`): both-strand startвҶ’stop CDS finding with `protein_length` excluding the stop, and SD consensus `AGGAGG` (+ substrings) matched upstream of a start at an aligned spacing вҲҲ [minDistance,maxDistance] (score = motifLen/6). Core correctness = the reverse-strand SD mapping `forwardPosition = len вҲ’ hit.position вҲ’ motifLen` (scan the reverse complement, since the SD is an mRNA feature); anti-SD 3' 16S tail `YACCUCCUUA`, ~8 nt location, 5 nt literature optimum (Chen 1994). `alternative_to` the Analysis-layer six-frame [[open-reading-frame-detection]] (not contract-equivalent); the strand/spacing-aware counterpart to the bare `AGGAGG` row in [[regulatory-element-detection]]. Validation report [[annot-gene-001-report]].
- [[relative-synonymous-codon-usage]] вҖ” RSCU (Sharp & Li 1986) codon-usage-bias measure: n_iВ·x/ОЈx normalization, 1.0=no bias, bounded [0,n_i], ОЈ-over-family=n_i invariant; pooled counts, sense codons only; base anchor of the codon-usage family (vs CAI's max-normalization).
- [[codon-adaptation-index]] вҖ” CAI (Sharp & Li 1987) whole-gene codon-bias / expression-proxy score in [0,1]: geometric mean of relative adaptiveness w=f/max_synonym_f, low-value-sensitive, stop excluded; dual include/exclude-Met/Trp mode (exclude can give L=0вҶ’0); E. coli oracles; Seqeron deviation = 1e-6 zero-freq clamp (vs Sharp & Li's 0.5 reference-table pseudocount); one level above RSCU.
- [[rare-codon-analysis]] вҖ” codon-usage family's *localization/diagnostic* unit (`FindRareCodons` + cluster addendum): a codon is rare when its per-family frequency < threshold (default 0.15), reports position/AA/frequency (E. coli AGA 0.04/AGG 0.02/CGA 0.06/CUA 0.04); addendum adds two published cluster methods вҖ” Clarke & Clark 2008 %MinMax (18-codon window, signed %Min/%Max вҲҲ[вҲ’100,+100], rare clusters = negative peaks) and Chartier 2012 Sherlocc (7-codon window, вүҘ4 of 7 freqвүӨthreshold "slow" positions = a rare-codon cluster); single-codon-AA contributes 0 to %MinMax (no NaN), overlapping windows merged; feeds [[codon-optimization]]'s AvoidRareCodons; oracles вҲ’86.36/+100/+36.47% and 7Г—AGAвҶ’1 cluster; deviations None.
- [[codon-usage-comparison]] вҖ” codon-usage family's *raw* end (`CalculateCodonUsage` + `CompareCodonUsage`): unnormalized codon-count table (non-overlapping triplets, TвҶ’U, drop partial codon, Dictionary<codon,int>, ОЈcounts=total invariant) + Total Variation Distance similarity `1вҲ’ОЈ|fвӮҒвҲ’fвӮӮ|/2 вҲҲ [0,1]` between two codon-frequency distributions; proven identity 1.0 / symmetry / range [0,1] / disjointвҶ’0 / partial-overlap-exact properties; emptyвҶ’0, TVD-not-cosine deliberate metric choice; Kazusa-verified organism tables; shares RSCU's counting primitive, the distribution-comparison op none of the bias measures provide.
- [[codon-optimization]] вҖ” codon-usage family's CDS-*rewriting* operation (`OptimizeSequence`): synonymous substitution to improve host expression; five strategies (MaximizeCAI / BalancedOptimization 40-60% GC / HarmonizeExpression=Mignon 2018 / AvoidRareCodons / MinimizeSecondaryвҶ’ReduceSecondaryStructure); invariants protein-preservation + Met/AUG & Trp/UGG fixed + stop preserved + CAIвҲҲ(0,1]; RNA notation, TвҶ’U, trim-to-codon, 1e-6 CAI clamp; E. coli/yeast/human preferred-codon fixtures; actuator to RSCU/CAI/ENC's measurement.
- [[effective-number-of-codons]] вҖ” ENC/Nc (Wright 1990) reference-free whole-gene codon-bias measure in [20,61]: reciprocal of codon homozygosity FМӮ=(nВ·ОЈpВІвҲ’1)/(nвҲ’1) aggregated by degeneracy class (Nc=2+9/FМӮвӮӮ+1/FМӮвӮғ+5/FМӮвӮ„+3/FМӮвӮҶ); 20=max bias / 61=uniform, unbiasedвҶ’61, no-bias-simвҶ’40.5; Ile absentвҶ’(FМӮвӮӮ+FМӮвӮ„)/2 fallback, overshoot re-adjusts to 61; reference-free counterpart of CAI; one assumption = non-source-prescribed lower clamp at 20.
- [[genetic-code-translation]] вҖ” the codon-family's foundational table: `GeneticCode` codonвҶ’amino-acid map (64 codons вҶ’ 20 AA + 3 stops), 4 of NCBI's 33 tables (Standard/1, Vertebrate-Mito/2, Yeast-Mito/3, Bacterial-Plastid/11) as static singletons; `Translate`/`IsStartCodon`/`IsStopCodon`/`GetCodonsForAminoAcid`; DNAвҶ”RNA TвҶ’U + case-insensitive + stopвҶ’`*` + lenвү 3вҶ’ArgumentException; Met/AUG & Trp/UGG single-codon fixed points (the wвүЎ1 fact behind CAI/optimization); IUPAC ambiguity codonвҶ’`'X'` (a flagged divergence from the Evidence doc's promised exception). The table [[open-reading-frame-detection|ORF detection]] and [[codon-optimization]] read. Also covers the **whole-sequence `Translator` layer** (TRANS-PROT-001 + TRANS-SIXFRAME-001): framed / six-frame translation + genetic-code-parameterized STARTвҶ’STOP ORF finding, verified against the UniProt-P01308 insulin B-chain oracle; six-frame reverse-frame numbering follows the **Biopython independent-offset** convention (вҲ’k = RC offset kвҲ’1), the documented alternative to EMBOSS phase-locked.
- [[repetitive-element-detection]] вҖ” repeats/tandem family anchor: tandem (head-to-tail, вүҘ2 copies, primitive unit), inverted (WВ·GВ·WМ„бҙҝ / zero-gap palindrome, IUPACpal), and RepeatMasker-class assignment; ClassifyRepeat = exact-substring containment, not Smith-Waterman homology.
- [[consensus-sequence]] вҖ” assembly CONSENSUS family anchor: column-wise majority/threshold consensus (Biopython dumb_consensus rule) вҖ” gaps skipped, emit iff unique max and freq вүҘ threshold else ambiguous, tieвҶ’ambiguous, all-gapвҶ’N no div-by-zero; N/0.5 parameterized defaults; shared with MSA consensus step.
- [[consensus-from-alignment]] вҖ” Motif-Analysis consensus-from-a-multiple-alignment (MOTIF-CONS-001, `MotifFinder.CreateConsensusFromAlignment`): pure most-frequent (plurality) column consensus over equal-length aligned strings, deterministic alphabetical tie-break (A<C<G<T), no threshold (always emits); Rosalind CONS `ATGCAACT` oracle; `alternative_to` the threshold/tieвҶ’ambiguous assembly [[consensus-sequence]], motif-family sibling of the exact [[known-motif-search]].
- [[iupac-degenerate-consensus]] вҖ” MotifFinder degenerate-consensus unit (MOTIF-GENERATE-001, `MotifFinder.GenerateConsensus`): collapses equal-length aligned columns into an IUPAC-ambiguity-coded string вҖ” per column keep every base with `count > 0.25В·n` (strict `>`), emit the NC-IUB 1984 symbol for that base set (R/Y/S/W/K/M, B/D/H/V, N), no-pass fallback вҶ’ most-frequent (alphabetical tie); DECIPHER threshold-consensus family + NC-IUB/UCSC/Wikipedia bijective setвҶ’symbol table; `A,A,G,G,C`вҶ’R / strict-`>` boundary / four-wayвҶ’A-fallback oracles; `alternative_to` the plurality [[consensus-from-alignment]], degenerate sibling of the exact [[known-motif-search]] and de-novo [[overrepresented-kmer-discovery]].
- [[regulatory-element-detection]] вҖ” Motif-Discovery regulatory-element unit (MOTIF-REGULATORY-001, `KnownMotifs` catalog scan): matches a **fixed, cited catalog of 12 canonical regulatory consensus elements** (TATA/вҲ’10/вҲ’35/CAAT/GC promoter boxes, Kozak + Shine-Dalgarno translation signals, poly(A), and E-box/AP-1/NF-ОәB/CREB TF sites) against a DNA sequence, reporting each occurrence's Name/Pattern/Sequence at its 0-based start; mixes exact and one IUPAC-degenerate (E-box `CANNTG`) match; anchors the AP-1 corrected-consensus regression (`TGAGTCA`вҶ’`TGACTCA`, `AATGAGTCAGG`вҶ’0 hits); two source-backed representative-site assumptions (NF-ОәB `GGGACTTTCC`, Kozak `GCCGCCACCATGG`); the curated-biological-catalog specialization of the generic exact [[known-motif-search]], distinct from the generation-direction [[iupac-degenerate-consensus]] and de-novo [[overrepresented-kmer-discovery]]; the scored вҲ’10/вҲ’35 alternative is [[promoter-detection]].
- [[promoter-detection]] вҖ” Annotation-layer scored вҲ’10/вҲ’35 promoter motif detector (ANNOT-PROM-001, `GenomeAnnotator.FindPromoterMotifs`): scans DNA for the prokaryotic вҲ’35 box `TTGACA` and вҲ’10/Pribnow box `TATAAT` plus derived prefix-5/suffix-5/prefix-4 variants, scoring each hit `ОЈ matched-position p / ОЈ all-6 consensus p вҲҲ [0,1]` from the E. coli position-specific frequencies (вҲ’35 sum 373, вҲ’10 sum 412); a full box scores 1.0, partial variants 0.665вҖ“0.855; `position` is a **0-based string index** (not the TSS-relative negative coordinate), `type` вҲҲ {`-35 box`,`-10 box`}, вҲ’35/вҲ’10 scanned independently (no pairing). Declared scope limits: **17 bp spacing not enforced**, **exact-substring not PWM/HMM/mismatch-tolerant** вҖ” motif annotation, not full promoter prediction; no null guard. The `alternative_to` the exact-hexamer catalog scan [[regulatory-element-detection]] (same two boxes, no scoring). Validation report [[annot-prom-001-report]].
- [[overrepresented-kmer-discovery]] вҖ” Motif-Discovery de-novo unit (MOTIF-DISCOVER-001, `MotifFinder.DiscoverMotifs`): finds **unknown** over-represented motifs by enumerating every length-`k` k-mer, counting overlapping occurrences, and ranking by observed/expected enrichment `Count/((NвҲ’k+1)/4^k)` under a zero-order i.i.d. uniform background (Compeau & Pevzner); deterministic exact single-pass, 0-based positions; `ATGC` in `ATGCATGCATGC` k=4 вҶ’ 768/9вүҲ85.333, `AAA` in `AAAAAAAAAA` k=3 вҶ’ 64.0 oracles; `k>N`вҶ’empty, minCount presentation-only, zero-order-only + no-p-value simplifications; the de-novo inverse of the exact [[known-motif-search]] and distinct from the [[consensus-from-alignment]] plurality consensus.
- [[shared-motifs]] вҖ” Motif-Discovery cross-sequence unit (MOTIF-SHARED-001, `FindSharedMotifs`): the van Helden / RSAT oligo-analysis **"matching sequences"** quorum вҖ” enumerate every fixed-`k` exact word across a *set* of sequences and report each word present in вүҘ `minSequences` of them (each carrying its `SequenceIndices` set + `Prevalence`=matching/total); a within-sequence repeat counts **1** (presence/absence, not multiplicity); exact-word only (no degenerate/substitution); the cross-sequence sibling of the single-sequence O/E [[overrepresented-kmer-discovery]] and `alternative_to` the fixed-k-quorum-vs-single-longest LCSM framing of [[longest-common-substring]] (returns all qualifying words, not one longest present in all).
- [[approximate-pattern-matching-mismatches]] вҖ” pattern-matching PAT-APPROX family anchor (PAT-APPROX-003): Hamming-distance **approximate matching** вҖ” a `k`-mer appears with вүӨ`d` mismatches when `HammingDistance(P,P')вүӨd` (BA1H); `Count_d`/`FindApproximateOccurrences` scan windows, `FindFrequentKmersWithMismatches` (BA1I) ranks `k`-mers by their **d-neighborhood** (Hamming-ball) tally so the winner need not occur exactly, `Neighbors` (BA1N) enumerates the ball (includes identity), `FindBestMatch` returns the leftmost min-Hamming window; oracles {GATG,ATGC,ATGT} count 5, {6,7,26,27,78}, Count_1=4, ACG/1вҶ’10; d=0 degenerates to exact so it is the mismatch-tolerant `alternative_to` [[k-mer-positions]] and the fuzzy sibling of the exact [[known-motif-search]] / de-novo [[overrepresented-kmer-discovery]]; substitution-only (no indels вҖ” that is the alignment family), deviations none.
- [[coverage-depth-calculation]] вҖ” assembly COVER family anchor: per-base sequencing depth over a reference (count of placed reads spanning each position, exact); average depth = ОЈdepth/G = Lander-Waterman C=LN/G, breadth = covered/G = 1вҲ’e^вҲ’c; boundary-clip + empty-input rules; ACGTTGCAATвҶ’1.5/1.0 oracle; Poisson (e^вҲ’c gap) as a property check only; read placement (minOverlap best-match) out of scope.
- [[de-bruijn-graph-assembly]] вҖ” assembly DBG family anchor: k-mer graph (distinct (k-1)-mers = nodes, each k-mer = one prefixвҶ’suffix edge, directed multigraph) + Eulerian-walk reconstruction (balanced/semi-balanced, Euler theorems 8.1/8.2, O(|E|) Hierholzer); spelling = path[0]+last char of each node; unique-walk oracles only (AAABBBA, a_longвҖҰ, to_everyвҖҰ k=4, ATGGCGTGCA); repeat/gap/error вҶ’ non-Eulerian; walk-selection unspecified so exact asserts on unique-walk inputs; OLC is the alternative formulation.
- [[overlap-layout-consensus-assembly]] вҖ” assembly OLC family anchor: the three-stage Overlap-Layout-Consensus paradigm (`FindAllOverlaps` + `AssembleOLC`) вҖ” overlap graph (read=node, edge on longest suffix-of-A/prefix-of-B вүҘ threshold), Layout = Hamiltonian path (NP-complete) + transitive reduction + non-branching contigs, Consensus = majority vote; GTACGTACGAT 12-edge / 5-overlap-tiling oracles; suffix-tree O(N+a) vs all-pairs O(NВІ); NP-complete/repeat-split/greedy-suboptimal failure modes; identity-1.0 + empty-input assumptions; Hamiltonian/overlap-graph alternative to DBG's Eulerian/k-mer formulation.
- [[contig-merge-overlap-collapse]] вҖ” assembly MERGE family anchor: suffixвҖ“prefix overlap collapse primitive (`MergeContigs`) behind greedy SCS and OLC layout; overlap = length-l suffix of X = prefix of Y, longest match reported, collapse keeps one copy so |merge|=|c1|+|c2|вҲ’l; overlap 0 / out-of-range вҶ’ plain concatenation; BAA+AABвҶ’BAAB, chainвҶ’AAABBBA oracles; caller-trusts-length + out-of-rangeвҶ’concat API-contract assumptions; overlap-based sibling of DBG's k-mer/Eulerian formulation.
- [[scaffolding]] вҖ” assembly SCAFFOLD family anchor: joining ordered contigs into a scaffold, adjacent contigs separated by `N`-runs of length = the (upstream) inter-contig distance estimate (ABySS 2.0 rule); positive gap `g` вҶ’ `g`Г—`N`, scaffold length = ОЈ|contig|+ОЈgap; non-positive (zero/negative) estimate вҶ’ AGP unknown-size default 100 N (negative = overlap, unresolved here); each contig in вүӨ1 scaffold, unlinked вҶ’ singleton; parameterized fill char; ACGTNNNTTGGNNCCAA / AAAA+100N+TTTT oracles; downstream of DBG/OLC/merge, hands off to contig-merge on the negative-gap overlap case; 100-constant source-backed (INSDC), only the fall-back-not-resolve decision is assumed.
- [[assembly-statistics]] вҖ” assembly STATS family anchor: contiguity/QC summary metrics over contig lengths (read-only, downstream of DBG/OLC/merge/scaffold) вҖ” Nx = shortest length covering вүҘx% (largest-first, inclusive вүҘ; N50/N90), Lx = the matching contig count, N90 вүӨ N50 / L90 вүҘ L50, auN = ОЈLбөўВІ/ОЈLвұј (area under Nx curve, more stable than N50); + totals/largest/smallest/GC and 0-based inclusive N-run gaps; Miller 2010 + Wikipedia + QUAST + Heng Li 2020; Assembly A N50 70/L50 2, auN 73.333 oracles; emptyвҶ’zeros (not None) + upper-median-not-source-derived assumptions.
- [[quality-trimming-running-sum]] вҖ” assembly TRIM family anchor: BWA/cutadapt running-sum quality trimming вҖ” subtract cutoff from each Phred quality, take partial sums to the 3' end, cut at the minimum (= BWA argmax of accumulated thresholdвҲ’q, with `s<0` early break + `BWA_MIN_RDLEN=35` floor); Phred+33 decode (Cock 2010); `KI;<)(,%#$`@thr 10вҶ’first 4 bases oracle; threshold<1 disables / all-high unchanged / all-low dropped / good-base-among-bad refinement; both-end pass + downstream minLength filter as assumptions; read-QC preprocessing upstream of correction/DBG/OLC.
- [[kmer-spectrum-error-correction]] вҖ” assembly CORRECT family anchor: two-sided k-mer-spectrum read error correction (Musket/Quake) вҖ” trusted (multiplicity > cut-off) vs untrusted k-mers, base trusted if covered by any trusted k-mer, unique alternative making all covering k-mers trusted, ambiguity/no-setвҶ’unchanged; substitution-only (count+length preserved); kmerSize=15/minKmerFrequency=2 non-behavioral defaults.
- [[centromere-analysis]] вҖ” chromosome centromere/alpha-satellite family anchor (second Chromosome-analysis unit): `AnalyzeCentromere` + 4 additive detectors вҖ” Levan 1964 q/p arm-ratio classes (Metacentric вүӨ1.7 / Submetacentric вүӨ3.0 / Subtelocentric <7.0 / Acrocentric вүҘ7.0 / Telocentric p=0); alpha-satellite-specific `DetectAlphaSatellite`/`FindCenpBBoxes` (171-bp tandem period Вұ5, AT>0.5, 17-bp CENP-B box `YTTCGTTGGAARCGGGA`, no embedded monomer); `DetectHigherOrderRepeat` (HOR period = smallest k with monomers k apart вүҘ95% identical across вүҘ90%, intra-HOR 50вҖ“70% vs inter-HOR 97вҖ“100%); `AssignSuprachromosomalFamily` (bundled CC0 Dfam ALR/ALRa=A/ALRb=B, SF3 pentameric/SF4 monomeric/{SF1,SF2} dimeric/SF5 irregular); base AlphaSatelliteContent is density-heuristic-not-specific + SF1/SF2-unresolved (non-redistributable consensus library) limitations.
- [[base-composition]] вҖ” foundational sequence-composition tally (SEQ-COMPOSITION-001): exact **nucleotide** partition of Length into A/T/G/C/U/`CountN`/`CountOther` (seven counts sum to Length), **GC content** `(G+C)/(A+T+G+C+U)` вҲҲ [0,1] (Biopython `gc_fraction`, empty вҮ’ 0), and **amino-acid** residue counts over the 20 IUPAC letters; case-insensitive, non-canonical/degenerate codes tracked separately (not folded into A/T/G/C/U) вҖ” the documented assumption vs Biopython (which counts S toward GC / W toward denominator), agreeing exactly over {A,T,G,C,U}; the magnitude/fraction view whose *asymmetry* counterpart is the sibling [[nucleotide-composition-skew]], base layer under [[cpg-island-detection]] dinucleotide O/E, [[windowed-sequence-complexity-profile]] window entropy, and the GC constraints in [[taqman-probe-design-rules]]/[[codon-optimization]]. Records [[seq-composition-001-evidence]].
- [[nucleotide-composition-skew]] вҖ” strand compositional-skew family (Lobry 1996): **AT skew** `(AвҲ’T)/(A+T)` + **GC skew** `(GвҲ’C)/(G+C)`, both bounded [вҲ’1,+1] (AT skew `вҲ’1вҮ”A=0`/`+1вҮ”T=0`); zero-denominator вҮ’ **0.0** (Biopython `GC_skew` convention), case-insensitive counting, ambiguous/non-canonical bases ignored; biological meaning = replication-strand asymmetry, cumulative-skew sign flip locates the origin/terminus (Charneski 2011: Firmicute AT skew from selection, not mutation); AT-skew member validated by [[seq-atskew-001-evidence]] (SEQ-ATSKEW-001), GC-skew member (`gc-skew`) not yet ingested; single-base cousin of the dinucleotide CpG O/E in [[cpg-island-detection]] and the GC-skew unit flagged in [[centromere-analysis]].
- [[dinucleotide-relative-abundance]] вҖ” dinucleotide composition & the **Karlin genomic signature** (SEQ-DINUC-001): the 2-mer generalization of [[base-composition]] and the general case of the CpG O/E in [[cpg-island-detection]]. Two outputs over the `NвҲ’1` adjacent base-steps вҖ” **dinucleotide frequency** `f_XY = count/(NвҲ’1)` and the **relative-abundance odds ratio** `ПҒ_XY = f_XY/(f_XВ·f_Y)` (`CalculateDinucleotideRatios`; `ПҒ=1` no-bias independence baseline, Karlin & Burge over/under thresholds `ПҒвүҘ1.23`/`ПҒвүӨ0.78` documentation-only); CpG O/E is the `CG`-specialized case, differing only by the `N` vs `NвҲ’1` normalization (`N/(NвҲ’1)вҶ’1` long sequences, a documented modeling choice). Exact-rational oracles for `ATGCGCGT` (GC/CG ПҒ=64/21, AT ПҒ=32/7, TG/GT ПҒ=32/21); div-by-zero guard вҶ’ ratio 0 when a constituent base is absent, `U` counted as a fifth base for RNA, case-insensitive. Also validates the codon-frequency metric owned by [[codon-usage-comparison]]/[[seq-codon-freq-001-evidence]]. Records [[seq-dinuc-001-evidence]].
- [[windowed-gc-profile-and-variance]] вҖ” composite **GC-analysis** unit's distinct layer (SEQ-GC-ANALYSIS-001, `GcAnalysisResult`): bundles the whole-sequence scalars OverallGcContent `(G+C)/(A+T+G+C)Г—100` (percentage Г—100, [[base-composition]] carries the `[0,1]` fraction), OverallGcSkew `(GвҲ’C)/(G+C)`, OverallAtSkew `(AвҲ’T)/(A+T)` ([[nucleotide-composition-skew]]) with a **sliding-window** GC%/GC-skew profile (only fully-contained windows; shorter-than-window вҮ’ empty lists) and the **population variance** `ПғВІ=ОЈ(xбөўвҲ’Ој)ВІ/N` (Г·N, not Г·NвҲ’1) of each windowed series вҖ” a compositional-heterogeneity/isochore-style variability signal, cumulative GC-skew locating the replication origin/terminus (Grigoriev 1998), same window-GC signal the [[centromere-analysis]] heuristic uses, composition sibling of the entropy/complexity [[windowed-sequence-complexity-profile]]. Sources GC-content Brock/Wikipedia + GC skew Lobry 1996/Biopython `GC_skew` + Cuemath population variance (6.8 anchor); `GGGCCAT`вҶ’71.428вҖҰ/0.2/0.0, `GGCC` w2s2вҶ’`GcSkewVariance` 1.0/`GcContentVariance` 0.0; two labelling/estimator assumptions (Г—100 vs fraction; Г·N population variance), no contradictions. Records [[seq-gc-analysis-001-evidence]].
- [[replication-origin-cumulative-skew]] вҖ” the skew family's *localisation* algorithm (SEQ-REPLICATION-001): predicts the **replication origin from the cumulative GC-skew minimum** and the **terminus from its maximum** (Grigoriev 1998; Rosalind BA1F Minimum Skew Problem). Distinct from the scalar/windowed skew вҖ” uses an **integer** cumulative running sum (G:+1, C:вҲ’1, A/T:0, `Skew_0=0`, `|Genome|+1` prefix values over `iвҲҲ[0,n]`), then argmin=`PredictedOrigin` / argmax=`PredictedTerminus`, first-occurrence tie-break (BA1F sample вҶ’ 53 of {53,97}); the leading strand is G-rich so skew flips sign at origin/terminus (Lobry 1996), making the integral a valley at ori and peak at ter. `IsSignificant` redefined threshold-free as `max>min` (invented `amplitude>countГ—0.01` constant removed); flat diagram (no/balanced G/C) вҮ’ origin=terminus=0/false. Diagram oracles `CCGGGG`/`GGGCCC`/`AATT`; consumes the same G/C tally as [[base-composition]]/[[nucleotide-composition-skew]], localisation counterpart of the [[windowed-gc-profile-and-variance]] variability view. Records [[seq-replication-001-evidence]].
- [[hydrophobicity-gravy-and-profile]] вҖ” protein-property member of the SEQ-\* sequence-statistics family (SEQ-HYDRO-001): the **Kyte-Doolittle (1982) GRAVY index** `ОЈ(kd value)/length` (Expasy/Biopython `gravy()`; positive вҮ’ hydrophobic, negative вҮ’ hydrophilic) + the **unweighted sliding-window hydropathy profile** (exactly `NвҲ’W+1` window means, Biopython `protein_scale(edge=1.0)`); the 20-residue kd table I 4.5вҖҰR вҲ’4.5 (identical to [[transmembrane-helix-prediction]]'s `HydropathyScale`), window-size guidance W=9 surface / W=19 transmembrane peaks > 1.6; oracles `A`вҶ’1.8 / `FLIV`вҶ’3.825 / `RKDE`вҶ’вҲ’3.85, window-3 `FLIV`вҶ’[3.7, 4.1666666667], `W>N`вҶ’empty, case-insensitive; one deviation (unknown residues **skipped** not Biopython `KeyError`), no source contradictions. The whole-sequence-scalar + raw-profile amino-acid analogue of the nucleotide [[base-composition]]; the segment-calling [[transmembrane-helix-prediction]] thresholds this same profile, and it shares the kd scale with [[intrinsic-disorder-prediction-top-idp]]'s `CalculateHydropathy`. Records [[seq-hydro-001-evidence]].
- [[dna-duplex-nearest-neighbor-thermodynamics]] вҖ” full-tuple thermodynamics member of the SEQ-\* family (SEQ-THERMO-001): the **О”HВ°/О”SВ°/О”GВ°вӮғвӮҮ/Tm** of a Watson-Crick DNA duplex from the **nearest-neighbor model** вҖ” a port of Biopython `Tm_NN` over the **DNA_NN3 / Allawi & SantaLucia 1997** table (10 WC dinucleotide О”HВ°/О”SВ° stacks) plus **two-terminus initiation** (`init_A/T` 2.3/4.1 and `init_G/C` 0.1/вҲ’2.8 counted off the two terminal bases). Tm `= (1000В·О”HВ°)/(О”SВ° + RВ·ln k) вҲ’ 273.15`, `R=1.987`, `k=(dnac1вҲ’dnac2/2)В·1eвҲ’9` (default 25 nM each вҮ’ k=C_T/4, the F=4 non-self-complementary factor); SantaLucia-1998 salt correction `О”SВ° += 0.368В·(lenвҲ’1)В·ln[NaвҒә]` вҮ’ Tm monotone in salt; О”GВ°вӮғвӮҮ `= О”HВ° вҲ’ 310.15В·О”SВ°/1000`. Oracles `CGTTCCAAAGATGTGGGCATGAGCTTAC` (25 nM, 50 mM Na) вҶ’ **Tm 60.32 В°C**, `GCGC` вҶ’ О”H вҲ’30.0/О”S вҲ’84.91/О”G вҲ’3.67/Tm вҲ’18.6, `ATCG` (one A/T + one G/C end) вҶ’ О”H вҲ’23.6/О”S вҲ’71.81; **length<2 вҮ’ `(0,0,0,0)`**, case-insensitive, non-self-complementary (F=4) only. Distinct from the legacy Wallace/Marmur scalar Tm ([[melting-temperature]], SEQ-TM-001) and from the 2004-unified PCR-primer engine [[primer-dimer-thermodynamics-tm]] (different init bookkeeping; returns the full tuple). Records [[seq-thermo-001-evidence]]; zero correctness-affecting assumptions, no source contradictions.
- [[melting-temperature]] вҖ” the **legacy %GC scalar** melting-temperature member of the SEQ-\* family and the **third distinct Tm surface** (SEQ-TM-001, `CalculateMeltingTemperature`): a single В°C number **length-dispatched** at `ThermoConstants.WallaceMaxLength = 14` between the **Wallace rule** `Tm = 4В·(G+C)+2В·(A+T)` for short oligos (Thein & Wallace 1986) and the **Marmur-Doty GC formula** `Tm = 64.9 + 41В·(GCвҲ’16.4)/N` (вүЎ `64.9 + 0.41В·%GC вҲ’ 672.4/N`) for lenвүҘ14 (Marmur & Doty 1962). A **rule of thumb carrying no О”HВ°/О”SВ°/О”GВ°**, no concentration term, no salt correction вҖ” the canonical home of the Wallace/Marmur formulas (previously only sketched as the legacy default on [[primer-dimer-thermodynamics-tm]]) and the fast approximation that [[seq-summary-001-evidence|SummarizeNucleotideSequence]]'s `MeltingTemperature` field and the primer engine's *default* per-oligo Tm both use. Oracles `ACGTTGCAATGCCGTA`вҶ’48.0 / `ATGCATGC`вҶ’24.0 (Wallace), `GCGCGCGCGCATATATATAT`вҶ’51.78 / 16-mer `ATGCATGCATGCATGC`вҶ’43.375 (Marmur-Doty); empty/nullвҶ’0, case-insensitive; one ASSUMPTION (14-nt dispatch boundary), formula-variant note (repo 64.9/вҲ’672.4 vs Biopython `Tm_GC` valueset-1 69.3/вҲ’650), no source contradictions. The %GC rule-of-thumb `alternative_to` the two SantaLucia NN engines [[dna-duplex-nearest-neighbor-thermodynamics]] (SEQ-THERMO-001, whose `CalculateThermodynamics` is the NN facet of the same consolidated SEQ-TM-001 registry entry) and [[primer-dimer-thermodynamics-tm]]. Records [[seq-tm-001-evidence]].
- [[molecular-weight]] вҖ” mass member of the SEQ-\* sequence-statistics family (SEQ-MW-001): the average-isotopic **molecular mass in Daltons** of a **protein, DNA or RNA** sequence via one shared polymerization formula `weight = ОЈ (monomer mass) вҲ’ (lenвҲ’1)В·water` (Biopython `Bio.SeqUtils.molecular_weight`; one water removed per bond вҖ” peptide for protein, phosphodiester for nucleic acid; for protein algebraically = the Expasy `ОЈ residue masses + water`), with average free-amino-acid (protein G 75.0666вҖҰW 204.2252) and 5'-monophosphate nucleotide (DNA A 331.2218вҖҰ; RNA A 347.2212вҖҰ) mass tables and `water = 18.0153`; single monomer вҮ’ free-monomer mass, circular вҮ’ вҲ’one more water, double-strand adds the complement (error for protein); oracles `AGC`вҶ’protein 249.29 / DNA 949.61 / RNA 997.61, `G`вҶ’75.0666, `A`вҶ’DNA 331.2218 / RNA 347.2212, empty/nullвҶ’0; case-insensitive, one deviation (unknown symbols **skipped** not Biopython-rejected), no source contradictions. The mass-weighted view of the [[base-composition]] tally and a whole-sequence-scalar sibling of the [[hydrophobicity-gravy-and-profile]] GRAVY scalar (pI/charge is the separate [[isoelectric-point]] unit). Records [[seq-mw-001-evidence]].
- [[isoelectric-point]] вҖ” charge/pH member of the SEQ-\* sequence-statistics family (SEQ-PI-001): the **pH at which a protein's net charge is zero**, found by **bisecting the HendersonвҖ“Hasselbalch net-charge function over [0,14]** to Вұ0.01. Net charge `ОЈ_basic +1/(1+10^(pHвҲ’pKa)) + ОЈ_acidic вҲ’1/(1+10^(pKaвҲ’pH))` (Moore 1985, Peptides `charge_pI.cpp`; monotone-decreasing вҮ’ unique root); basic/positive = {R,K,H,N-term}, acidic/negative = {D,E,C,Y,C-term}, both termini once. **EMBOSS `Epk.dat` pKa scale** (N-term 8.6/C-term 3.6/C 8.5/D 3.9/E 4.1/H 6.5/K 10.8/R 12.5/Y 10.1) вҖ” the single-pKa-per-residue model, *not* position-dependent Bjellqvist. **Composition-only / order-independent** ("no electrostatic interactions" вҖ” a permutation gives identical pI), the trait it shares with [[base-composition]]; the ExPASy Compute pI/Mw partner of [[molecular-weight]] and protein-property sibling of [[hydrophobicity-gravy-and-profile]]. Oracles `A`/`AG`вҶ’6.10, `D`вҶ’3.75, `K`вҶ’9.70, `DDDD`вҶ’3.23, `KKKK`вҶ’11.27, `FLPVLAGLTPSIVPKLVCLLTKKC`вҶ’9.67 (net charge 3.037398/2.914112/0.7184524 @ pH 5/7/9), `ACDEFGHIKLMNPQRSTVWY`вҶ’7.36 (EMBOSS вү  Bjellqvist 6.78454); pIвҲҲ[0,14] invariant, two assumptions (empty/nullвҶ’7.0 guard; scale=EMBOSS parameter choice), small/highly-basic-protein accuracy caveat, no source contradictions. Records [[seq-pi-001-evidence]].
- [[protein-secondary-structure-chou-fasman]] вҖ” conformational-propensity member of the SEQ-\* sequence-statistics family (SEQ-SECSTRUCT-001): the **Chou-Fasman (1978) PОұ/PОІ/Pt sliding-window mean-propensity profile** вҖ” for a window `W`, the arithmetic mean of each of the Оұ-helix/ОІ-sheet/ОІ-turn propensities (observed/expected; A 1.42/0.83/0.66 вҖҰ V 1.06/1.70/0.50) over each window. The **generic profile, not** the classic 4-of-6-helix / 3-of-5-sheet nucleation-extension state machine вҶ’ default `W=7` is an API convenience not a CF constant; shares the exact SEQ-\* sliding-window mechanism with [[hydrophobicity-gravy-and-profile]] (`NвҲ’W+1` unweighted window means, `W>N`вҶ’empty, unknown residues skip-and-excluded, case-insensitive). Oracles single-residue window = that residue's (PОұ,PОІ,Pt) tuple, `AE`вҶ’helix 1.465/sheet 0.60/turn 0.70, `AEV`вҶ’helix 1.330, `AXE` W3 averages only A+E; one contested value resolved (**Lys PОұ 1.14** two-source incl. reference impl vs CSB|SJU 1.16), three assumptions (window-7 default, skip-unknown, Lys 1.14), ~50вҖ“60% Q3 / 29-protein reliability caveat. A raw propensity profile that does **not** emit helix/sheet/turn segments вҖ” distinct from the hydropathy segment-caller [[transmembrane-helix-prediction]], the disorder view [[intrinsic-disorder-prediction-top-idp]] and the SEG scan [[protein-low-complexity-seg]]. Records [[seq-secstruct-001-evidence]].
- [[karyotype-analysis]] вҖ” chromosome karyotyping/ploidy-detection family anchor (third Chromosome-analysis unit): `AnalyzeKaryotype` builds a karyotype from chromosome descriptors (split sex/autosome, group by base name, count copies, compare to expected ploidy, label nullisomy..pentasomy by absolute count; TotalChromosomes/TotalGenomeSize/MeanChromosomeLength invariants) and `DetectPloidy` estimates whole-genome ploidy from read depth (true-median ratio вҶ’ round(ratioГ—2) clamped [1,8], confidence 1вҲ’|ratioГ—2вҲ’ploidy|Г—2, emptyвҶ’(2,0)); Down/Turner + diploid/tetraploid/haploid oracles; DD4 nullisomy-unreachable-via-GroupBy, DD5 disomy-only-aneuploid-in-polyploid; deviations None. Descriptor-count sibling of depth-log-ratio [[aneuploidy-detection]].
- [[synteny-and-rearrangement-detection]] вҖ” shared synteny anchor (fourth Chromosome-analysis unit; comparative-genomics COMPGEN-SYNTENY will reuse it): `FindSyntenyBlocks` builds syntenic blocks from ortholog pairs (group by chr pair, sort by ref position, collinear runs merged under maxGap, emit вүҘminGenes; block carries strand '+'/'-', GeneCount, SequenceIdentity=NaN for coordinate-only input per MCScanX; I1вҖ“I5) + `DetectRearrangements` classifies adjacent-block signals (diff target chrвҶ’Translocation, same chr diff strandвҶ’Inversion, gap asymmetryвҶ’Deletion, overlapping source diff targetsвҶ’Duplication); forward/inverted-block + translocation(50000)/inversion(size 10000) oracles; empty/below-minGenes/maxGap-split/multi-pair edge cases; MCScanX/SyRI/MUMmer + Wikipedia; deviations None.
- [[telomere-analysis]] вҖ” chromosome telomere family anchor (fifth Chromosome-analysis unit): telomere repeat detection + length estimation вҖ” 3вҖІ end forward TTAGGG / 5вҖІ end reverse-complement CCCTAA (6-bp vertebrate unit, Meyne 1989), configurable 70%-per-window purity so imperfect repeats accepted (5/6 for 6-bp, 5/7 for Arabidopsis TTTAGGG; divergent TTAGGAвҶ’0.833), purityвҲҲ[0,1] tracked with length; length direct from run or qPCR T/S ratio (Cawthon 2002) EstimatedLength=referenceLengthГ—(tsRatio/referenceRatio); IsCriticallyShort=(hasTelomere&&length<criticalLength)OR empty; criticalLength 3000 / minTelomereLength 500 / searchLength(truncates) / referenceLength 7000 configurable defaults not biological constants; Wikipedia/Meyne/Cawthon/Blackburn-Gall sources; deviations None. Sibling of [[aneuploidy-detection]].
- [[conserved-gene-clusters-common-intervals]] вҖ” comparative-genomics common-interval / conserved-cluster unit: a conserved gene cluster = a gene-label SET contiguous in EVERY genome (order- and strand-free inside the window), the common-interval model (Uno & Yagiura 2000, Heber & Stoye 2001 k-permutation O(kn+z), Bui-Xuan/Habib/Paul 2013 unifying view, Didier et al. 2013 sequences-with-duplicates/paralogs); interval size вүҘ2 (singletons excluded), whole set (1..n) trivially common, meaningful only for KвүҘ2; Seqeron does the strict O(nВІВ·K) check with minClusterSize filter; strict gap-free model вҖ” maxGap retained for API/MCP back-compat only and does NOT relax it, gene-teams gapped extension (Bergeron 2002) not implemented; golden vector IdвӮҮ vs (7 2 1 3 6 4 5) вҶ’ {1,2}/{1,2,3}/{3,4,5,6}/{4,5}/{4,5,6}/{1..6} + trivial {1..7}, split-negative {2,3}, duplicates T/S вҶ’ {1,2,3,4}; order-free sibling of [[synteny-and-rearrangement-detection]] and [[average-nucleotide-identity]]; deviations None.
- [[average-nucleotide-identity]] вҖ” comparative-genomics ANI family anchor (first COMPGEN unit): the ANIb genome-similarity metric (Goris 2007) that operationalizes the prokaryotic species boundary (ANIвүҲ95%вҶ”70% DDH) вҖ” fragment query into 1020 nt pieces, best-match place each against the reference (`CalculateAni`), keep fragments >30% identity over вүҘ70% alignable (both recalculated over the query-fragment length), average the qualifying per-fragment identities; gapped Smith-Waterman placement recovers indels (`gapped:true`), reciprocal/symmetric ANI = mean of both directions (`CalculateReciprocalAni`, order-independent); null/emptyвҶ’0, non-positive fragmentLength throws; engine decision = SequenceAligner.LocalAlign (full DP, BLAST DNA scoring) not NCBI-BLASTN, indel handling correct; sibling of [[synteny-and-rearrangement-detection]] in the COMPGEN family; deviations None.
- [[dot-plot-word-match]] вҖ” comparative-genomics visual pairwise-comparison unit (`COMPGEN-DOTPLOT-001`): the word-match / k-tuple dot matrix (Gibbs & McIntyre 1970 вҶ’ EMBOSS `dottup`) вҖ” dot at (x,y) iff the length-`wordSize` word at x in seq1 exactly matches the word at y in seq2 (case-insensitive, x=seq1/y=seq2, all overlapping occurrences via suffix tree), diagonals = similarity / main diagonal = self-comparison / repeats = extra diagonals / indels break the diagonal; `wordSize` (EMBOSS default 10) noise-vs-sensitivity trade-off (longer=less noise/less sensitive), `stepSize` x-subsampling; exact-match `dottup` not scored `dotmatcher`; AGCGT/AT k=1вҶ’{(0,0),(4,1)}, ACGTACGT self wordSize4вҶ’{(0,0),(0,4),(1,1),(2,2),(3,3),(4,0),(4,4)}, ACGT self main-diagonal oracles; word>seq/null/empty/disjointвҶ’no dots, non-positive wordSize/stepSize throws; sibling of ANI/synteny/conserved-clusters; orientation + case-insensitivity assumptions, deviations None.
- [[ortholog-detection-reciprocal-best-hits]] вҖ” comparative-genomics ortholog & in-paralog detection unit (`COMPGEN-ORTHO-001`): orthologs by Reciprocal Best Hits (RBH вҖ” each gene the other's best hit across two genomes, Moreno-Hagelsieb 2008 / Tatusov 1997 / Fitch 1970 speciation-vs-duplication), recent (in-)paralogs by within-genome mutual best hits (Remm 2001); best hit=max-similarity with deterministic tie-break, reciprocity mandatory (one-directional best hit is NOT an ortholog = the guarded defect), вүҘ50% coverage + min-similarity gates, partial-matching output, emptyвҶ’no orthologs / single-geneвҶ’no paralogs; reciprocity/non-reciprocity(RBH count 1)/in-paralog oracles; one assumption = alignment-free 5-mer Jaccard replaces BLAST bit-score ranking (reciprocity/coverage/threshold source-backed); shared anchor for COMPGEN-RBH-001, the core/shared-gene sub-unit of [[genome-comparison-core-dispensable]]; sibling of ANI/synteny/conserved-clusters/dot-plot; deviations None.
- [[genome-rearrangement-breakpoint-distance]] вҖ” comparative-genomics signed-permutation / breakpoint rearrangement-detection unit (`COMPGEN-REARR-001` + `COMPGEN-REVERSAL-001`): the HannenhalliвҖ“Pevzner/BafnaвҖ“Pevzner theory вҖ” signed permutation (strand=sign), extended `(0,вҖҰ,n+1)` (endpoints=telomeres), breakpoint = consecutive pair where neither `(x,y)` nor `(вҲ’y,вҲ’x)` survives in ОІ, `b(Оұ)` count = `d_BP=nвҲ’sim(common adjacencies)`, reversal-distance lower bound `dвүҘb/2`; `ClassifyRearrangement` вҶ’ Inversion (reversal = sign-flip + local reverse) vs Transposition (block move preserving orientation), Translocation/Deletion/Insertion/Duplication "Not implemented" (single permutation can't express them); Hunter `(вҲ’2,вҲ’3,+1,+6,вҲ’5,вҲ’4)`вҶ’b=6/dвүҘ3, identityвҶ’0, single-inversion `(+1,вҲ’4,вҲ’3,вҲ’2,+5)`вҶ’b=2 oracles; `bвҲҲ[0,n+1]` invariant; the signed-permutation `alternative_to` the block-signal [[synteny-and-rearrangement-detection]], sibling of ANI/ortholog/clusters/dot-plot; deviations None.
- [[genome-comparison-core-dispensable]] вҖ” comparative-genomics end-to-end pipeline (`CompareGenomes`): partitions each genome's genes into core (conserved = RBH ortholog pairs, Tettelin 2005 pan-genome) vs dispensable (genome-specific = the rest), reports Conserved/Specific1/Specific2 + OverallSynteny=(genes in MCScanX syntenic blocks)/min(|g1|,|g2|) clamped вүӨ1; symmetric partition, emptyвҶ’all-0; orchestrates RBH ortholog detection (COMPGEN-RBH-001) + synteny (COMPGEN-SYNTENY-001); sibling of [[average-nucleotide-identity]] & [[conserved-gene-clusters-common-intervals]]; two source-backed assumptions (alignment-free RBH gate, MCScanX вүҘ5-anchor block threshold вҶ’ OverallSynteny can be 0 with conserved orthologs); deviations None.
- [[morf-prediction-dip-in-disorder]] вҖ” protein-disorder family MoRF unit (DISORDER-MORF-001, second DISORDER-* unit): Molecular Recognition Feature prediction by the "dip within disorder" heuristic (Oldfield 2005 / Cheng-Oldfield PMC2570644 / Mohan 2006) вҖ” a short ordered run (per-residue TOP-IDP disorder score <0.5) of total length 10вҖ“70 flanked on both sides by disorder (score вүҘ0.5) = one MoRF; 0.5 order/disorder threshold, Оұ/ОІ/О№ bound-state sub-types (Mohan 2006), MoRF scoreвҲҲ[0,1] rising with dip depth; terminal dip / fully-ordered / fully-disordered / out-of-band вҶ’ none; TOP-IDP normalized `(raw+0.884)/1.871` per-residue score from `PredictDisorder`; one assumption = exact flank-length params paywalled вҶ’ qualitative criterion (threshold/band/shape source-traceable); distinct sibling of [[protein-low-complexity-seg]]; deviations None.
- [[protein-low-complexity-seg]] вҖ” protein disorder / features family anchor (first DISORDER-* unit, DISORDER-LC-001): the SEG algorithm (Wootton & Federhen 1993/1996) partitioning a protein into low-/high-complexity segments; complexity = Shannon entropy `H=вҲ’ОЈpбөўlogвӮӮpбөў` bits/residue (max logвӮӮ20вүҲ4.322), two-stage scan with W=12 trigger window / K1=2.2 trigger cutoff / K2=2.5 extension cutoff (NCBI `blast_seg.c` defaults); homopolymer H=0 triggers, 12-distinct HвүҲ3.585>K2 no segment; X-rich/X-Y-rich label + greedy single-residue extension are flagged repository extensions not moving boundaries; distinct from [[intrinsic-disorder-prediction-top-idp|intrinsic-disorder prediction]] (TOP-IDP) and the genomic-DNA [[repetitive-element-detection]] low-complexity counterpart.
- [[intrinsic-disorder-prediction-top-idp]] вҖ” protein-disorder family shared anchor (DISORDER-PRED-001 + DISORDER-PROPENSITY-001 + DISORDER-REGION-001): the TOP-IDP `PredictDisorder` sliding-window intrinsic-disorder predictor (Campen 2008) that [[morf-prediction-dip-in-disorder]] + disordered-region detection sit on; also hosts the region-detection layer (contiguous runs вүҘ minRegionLength, default RegionType classification proline-rich/acidic/basic/Ser-Thr-rich > 0.25 + Long/Standard IDR, opt-in MobiDB-lite flavor scheme); per-residue Sбөў=mean over window of min-max-normalized TOP-IDP `(pвҲ’(вҲ’0.884))/1.871 вҲҲ [0,1]`, disordered when SбөўвүҘ0.542 (max-likelihood cutoff), default window 21 (edge-clipped) / minRegionLength 5; Dunker 2001 disorder{A,R,G,Q,S,P,E,K}/order{W,C,F,I,Y,V,L,N}/ambiguous{D,H,M,T} sets + Kyte-Doolittle `CalculateHydropathy`; W30вҶ’0.0/P30вҶ’1.0/E30вҶ’0.866 oracles, null/emptyвҶ’empty, non-canonical skipped (all-unknown windowвҶ’0.0), case-insensitive, O(nВ·w); also anchors the raw per-residue propensity primitives (DISORDER-PROPENSITY-001: `GetDisorderPropensity` returns the RAW un-normalized Table-2 value, unknownвҶ’0.0, + the two public Dunker sets); assumptions None (params source-traced), impl = simplified single-feature heuristic not competitive with IUPred2A/MobiDB-lite; distinct sibling of [[protein-low-complexity-seg]].
- [[coiled-coil-prediction]] вҖ” ProteinMotif family anchor (first ingested unit, PROTMOTIF-CC-001): the heptad a/d hydrophobic-core occupancy coiled-coil predictor `ProteinMotifFinder.PredictCoiledCoils` вҖ” for each window `score = (#a/d positions with residue вҲҲ {I,L,V})/(#a/d positions)` maximised over the 7 heptad registers (`p(k,r)=(kвҲ’r) mod 7`, core a=0/d=3), contiguous windows with score вүҘ threshold mapped to residue regions вүҘ21 residues (3 heptads) with peak `ScoreвҲҲ[0,1]`; defaults window 28 (4 heptads, Lupas 1991) / threshold 0.5 / min-region 21 (Mason & Arndt вүҘ3-heptad); INV-01..05 (scoreвҲҲ[0,1]; regionвүҘ21; len<windowвҶ’empty; off-frame found via 7-register max); (LAALAAA)Г—5вҶ’(0,34,1.0) / no-{I,L,V}вҶ’none / (LAAAAAA)вҶ’0.5 boundary oracles; COILS 21Г—20 PSSM deliberately omitted (weights not retrievable, use COILS/Paircoil2 for P-scores) + {I,L,V}-only core-set assumption (source-verbatim); sequence-only heuristic, distinct from the ProteinPred disorder/features family ([[protein-low-complexity-seg]], [[intrinsic-disorder-prediction-top-idp]], [[morf-prediction-dip-in-disorder]]).
- [[common-protein-motifs]] вҖ” ProteinMotif family second unit (PROTMOTIF-COMMON-001, `ProteinMotifFinder.FindCommonMotifs`): scans an amino-acid sequence against a fixed built-in `CommonMotifs` dictionary of canonical PROSITE patterns and aggregates every hit carrying its accession/name вҖ” PS00001 `ASN_GLYCOSYLATION` `N-{P}-[ST]-{P}`, PS00005 `PKC_PHOSPHO_SITE` `[ST]-x-[RK]`, PS00006 `CK2_PHOSPHO_SITE` `[ST]-x(2)-[DE]`, PS00016 `RGD` `R-G-D`, PS00017 `ATP_GTP_A` `[AG]-x(4)-G-K-[ST]`; PROSITE syntax (`x` wildcard, `[ ]` allowed set, `{ }` excluded set, `x(n)`/`x(m,n)` repetition); 0-based-inclusive `MotifMatch.Start`/`End` (PROSITE reports 1-based) + substring invariant + overlaps-all-reported (ScanProsite "overlaps, no includes"); `NFTA`/Pro-exclusion-no-match/`SAR`/`SAAE`+`SDED`/`GXXXXGKS`/`RGD`+`RGD`-overlap oracles; one API-shape assumption (0- vs 1-based origin, no correctness effect); the **protein** fixed-catalog analogue of the DNA [[regulatory-element-detection]], sibling of the windowed [[coiled-coil-prediction]], distinct from the caller-supplied-set DNA exact [[known-motif-search]].
- [[protein-domain-and-signal-peptide-prediction]] вҖ” ProteinMotif family third unit (PROTMOTIF-DOMAIN-001): protein **domain** prediction + **signal-peptide** prediction. `ProteinMotifFinder.FindDomains` scans PROSITE **domain patterns** (PS00028 C2H2 zinc finger/PF00096, PS00017 P-loop/PF00069, PS00678 WD40 15-residue/PF00400; ScanPrositeвҶ’regex), 0-based inclusive hits, tandem repeats all detected вҖ” SH3/PDZ excluded (PROSITE **PROFILEs**, no deterministic pattern). Opt-in `FindDomainsByHmm`/`Plan7ProfileHmm` reproduces the **HMMER3** engine over 3 bundled CC0 Pfam HMMs (SH3/PDZ/WD40): Viterbi/Forward log-odds (exact 1e-9 hand-HMM), local-multihit `pre_score` vs Swiss-Prot `bg->f` (~1e-5-bit hmmsearch parity), null2 bias (omega 1/256), Gumbel/exponential E-values (`E=PВ·Z`), `p7_domaindef` multi-domain envelope decomposition (GBB1/PF00400вҶ’7 blades exact) + stochastic-traceback clustering for overlapping tandems (fixed-seed Easel LCG 42), verified vs pyhmmer 0.12.1. `PredictSignalPeptide` = von Heijne tripartite n(K/R+)/h(hydrophobic Оұ-helix)/c(polar) + вҲ’1,вҲ’3 rule {A,G,S}, score (n+2h+c)/4 with evidence-based constraints (nScore>0, hScoreвүҘ0.5) and Probability=Score. Six resolved design decisions; MSV/bias prefilters + exact-RNG-bit parity + full-Pfam coverage out of scope (research-grade). Sibling of [[coiled-coil-prediction]] & [[common-protein-motifs]].
- [[protein-motif-pattern-search]] вҖ” ProteinMotif family general engine (PROTMOTIF-FIND-001, `ProteinMotifFinder.FindMotifByPattern`): the **general, arbitrary caller-supplied** PROSITE-pattern protein motif finder underneath the fixed-dictionary [[common-protein-motifs]]. Three primitives вҖ” `ConvertPrositeToRegex` (PROSITEвҶ’regex: `x`вҶ’`.`, `[ABC]`вҶ’`[ABC]`, `{ABC}`вҶ’`[^ABC]`, `x(n)`вҶ’`.{n}`, `x(n,m)`вҶ’`.{n,m}`, `<`вҶ’`^`, `>`вҶ’`$`); `FindMotifByPattern` (all matches incl. overlaps via zero-width lookahead `(?=(pattern))` per ScanProsite, 0-based `MotifMatch.Start`/`End`, case-insensitive, empty/nullвҶ’empty, invalid regex handled gracefully); and information-content scoring `CalculateMotifScore` IC=ОЈlogвӮӮ(20/allowed_count) over constrained positions (`x`=0 bits, fixedвүҲ4.32 bits) + `CalculateEValue` E=(NвҲ’L+1)В·2^(вҲ’IC), Schneider & Stephens 1990 (NOT BLAST statistics вҖ” that citation was removed). Pins the PROSITE-pattern catalog (PS00001/00004вҖ“00009/00016вҖ“00018/00028 C2H2/00029 leucine-zipper) and fixed two impl bugs (PS00007 exact repeat counts; PS00018 EF-hand `{W}`+trailing `[LIVMFYW]`); five non-PROSITE linear motifs literature-verified (NLS1/NES1/SIM1/WW1/SH3_1); SKIP-FLAG=TRUE common sites noted. Sibling of the fixed-catalog [[common-protein-motifs]], windowed [[coiled-coil-prediction]], and longer-signature [[protein-domain-and-signal-peptide-prediction]]; all assumptions eliminated (0-vs-1-based coordinate convention only). Revalidated by PROTMOTIF-PATTERN-001 ([[protmotif-pattern-001-evidence]]), which adds the end-to-end `FindMotifByProsite` path and the `*`-rejection / range-only-on-`x` PA-line grammar contracts.
