- [[transmembrane-helix-prediction]] вҖ” ProteinMotif family transmembrane-helix unit (PROTMOTIF-TM-001): the classic **Kyte-Doolittle (1982) hydropathy sliding window** for membrane-spanning Оұ-helices вҖ” slide a window `W=19`, score each window as the **arithmetic mean** of per-residue Kyte-Doolittle hydropathy (`HydropathyScale` I 4.5вҖҰR вҲ’4.5), emit contiguous runs with window mean **вүҘ threshold 1.6** as segments (`[iвӮҖ, iвӮҒ+WвҲ’1]`, peak `Score`); profile length `nвҲ’W+1`, non-standard residues excluded from the mean, `<W`/null/emptyвҶ’empty; window 19 & min-span=W justified by ~18вҖ“21 residues / ~3вҖ“4 nm bilayer. Oracles `DГ—10+LГ—20+DГ—10`вҶ’(5,34) peak 3.8 / `DГ—40`вҶ’none / `LГ—19`вҶ’(0,18,3.8). One assumption (`End=lastPassingProfileIndex+WвҲ’1` clamped, 2026-06-16 off-by-one fix), no deviations; sequence-only hydrophobicity heuristic вҖ” no in-out topology / positive-inside rule / TMHMM-Phobius HMM. Shares the Kyte-Doolittle scale with [[intrinsic-disorder-prediction-top-idp]]'s `CalculateHydropathy`; distinct sibling of [[coiled-coil-prediction]] (heptad a/d, not window-mean), [[common-protein-motifs]], [[protein-domain-and-signal-peptide-prediction]] (cleaved signal peptide, not membrane span) & [[protein-motif-pattern-search]].
- [[aneuploidy-detection]] вҖ” chromosome copy-number/ploidy family anchor (first Chromosome-analysis unit): abnormal chromosome count from read depth вҖ” per-bin CN=round(2^log2(depth/median)Г—2) clamped [0,10], whole-chromosome call needs dominant CN across вүҘ80% of bins (mosaicism tolerance), confidence=1вҲ’min(1,|CN/2вҲ’2^logRatio|)=1.0 at integer-CN ratios; nullisomy..pentasomy terminology; Down/Edwards/Patau/Turner/Klinefelter oracles; sex-chromosomes-not-special-cased + partial-aneuploidy-needs-80%-bins limitations.
- [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]] вҖ” epigenetics family bisulfite-sequencing unit (second EPIGEN-* unit, EPIGEN-BISULF-001): base-level DNA-methylation calling from sodium-bisulfite reads вҖ” distinct from the age clock (it *produces* the ОІ-values a clock consumes). Three deterministic ops on `EpigeneticsAnalyzer`: (1) `SimulateBisulfiteConversion` вҖ” single-strand per-base Frommer 1992 rule (unprotected CвҶ’T, protected 5mC stays C, non-C unchanged, case preserved, ACGTCGAA{1}вҶ’ACGTTGAA); (2) `CalculateMethylationFromBisulfite` вҖ” reuses `FindCpGSites`, Bismark C=methylated/T=unmethylated tally, level = meth/(meth+unmeth)вҲҲ[0,1], zero-coverage sites excluded (ACGTACGT readsвҶ’0.5&0.0); (3) `GenerateMethylationProfile` вҖ” Schultz 2012 per-context weighted level ОЈ(levelВ·coverage)/ОЈcoverage (0.25вү unweighted 0.5), zero-total-coverage falls back to unweighted mean; CpG needs C+G, neither-C-nor-T call ignored, past-reference ignored; research-grade, no CHG/CHH calling / no complement merge / no non-conversion-rate correction; sibling of [[epigenetic-age-horvath-clock]]; deviations None.
- [[epigenetic-age-horvath-clock]] вҖ” epigenetics family anchor (first EPIGEN-* unit, EPIGEN-AGE-001): DNAm ("epigenetic") age from methylation ОІ-values via the Horvath 2013 multi-tissue clock вҖ” two-stage model, linear predictor `Y = intercept + ОЈ coef_iВ·ОІ_i` over 353 elastic-net-selected clock CpGs (transformed-age units), then the two-branch inverse calibration `anti.trafo` (adult.age=20): `21В·exp(Y)вҲ’1` for Y<0 (exponential), `21В·Y+20` for YвүҘ0 (linear), continuous at (0,20)=age 20; embedded intercept 0.695507258 + 353 `CoefficientTraining` weights cross-verified byte-identical; invariants Y=0вҶ’20 / CpGs-absent-ignored / empty-mapвҶ’FвҒ»В№(intercept); nullвҶ’ArgumentNullException, empty coefficientsвҶ’ArgumentException; anti.trafo oracles (0вҶ’20, 1вҶ’41, вҲ’1вҶ’6.7254682646, вҲ’2.5вҶ’0.7237849711) + Y=0.684247258вҶ’34.369192418; scope = multi-tissue only (algorithm doc later extends to Horvath-2018 skin&blood 391-CpG + Levine-2018 PhenoAge 513-CpG no-transform); no BMIQ input normalisation (research-grade); sibling [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]] (produces the ОІ-values); third Epigenetics sibling [[chromatin-state-prediction]] (histone-mark axis).
- [[cpg-island-detection]] вҖ” epigenetics family CpG site & island unit (fourth EPIGEN-* unit, EPIGEN-CPG-001): sequence-only CpG dinucleotide detection (no methylation state вҖ” distinct from all siblings). Three ops on `EpigeneticsAnalyzer`: `FindCpGSites` (linear scan, 0-based C position, `CGCG`вҶ’2 sites, reused by [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]]); `CalculateCpGObservedExpected` (Gardiner-Garden O/E=CpG/((CВ·G)/L), div-by-zero guardвҶ’0, oracles CGCGГ— 2.0/ACGTCGACG 3.0/ACGT 4.0/AT-only 0); `FindCpGIslands` (sliding-window merge, default вүҘ200bp/GCвүҘ0.5/O-EвүҘ0.6 inclusive, 0-based inclusive-Start/exclusive-End tuple, 400bp CGCGвҶ’1 island, O(nВ·w)); GpCвү CpG, case-insensitive; Takai-Jones 2002 stricter (вүҘ500/55%/0.65) + Saxonov 2006 alt-expected not preset (custom args); Gardiner-Garden & Frommer 1987 + Takai-Jones + Saxonov + Wikipedia; assumptions None. Siblings [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]]/[[epigenetic-age-horvath-clock]]/[[chromatin-state-prediction]].
- [[chromatin-state-prediction]] вҖ” epigenetics family chromatin-state / histone-mark unit (third EPIGEN-* unit, EPIGEN-CHROM-001): ChromHMM-style (Ernst & Kellis 2012) annotation of a locus from the *combination of present histone marks* вҖ” distinct from the methylation siblings (operates on histone ChIP-seq signals, not DNA methylation). Binary present/absent mark model (ChromHMM binarizes then learns; state = function of the SET of present marks, magnitude beyond the call irrelevant = binary invariance); `PredictChromatinState` takes the six Roadmap 18-state marks {H3K4me3, H3K4me1, H3K27ac, H3K36me3, H3K27me3, H3K9me3} as [0,1] signals, calls present > threshold (default 0.5), maps pattern вҶ’ ActivePromoter(TssA, H3K4me3ВұH3K27ac)/ActiveEnhancer(H3K4me1+H3K27ac)/WeakEnhancer(H3K4me1 no H3K27ac)/Transcribed(Tx, H3K36me3)/Repressed(ReprPC, H3K27me3)/Heterochromatin(Het, H3K9me3)/BivalentPromoter(TssBiv, H3K4me3+H3K27me3)/BivalentEnhancer(EnhBiv, H3K4me1+H3K27me3)/LowSignal(Quies, none); two combinatorial rules вҖ” bivalency is a state not a contradiction, promoter(H3K4me3) dominates enhancer(H3K4me1); companions `AnnotateHistoneModifications` (per-mark region label) + `FindAccessibleRegions` (ATAC-like contiguous-merge + minWidth); research-grade вҖ” state-assignment logic source-backed, NOT a trained HMM (no LearnModel/Poisson binarization/spatial context); two assumptions (0.5 threshold, single-locus precedence); sibling of [[epigenetic-age-horvath-clock]] & [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]]; no contradictions.
- [[differentially-methylated-regions]] вҖ” epigenetics family DMR-detection unit (fifth EPIGEN-* unit, EPIGEN-DMR-001): methylKit (Akalin 2012) two-sample tiling-window + Fisher's-exact-test model вҖ” *compares* methylation between two samples (distinct from the single-sample siblings), consuming the per-CpG C/(C+T) ОІ-values [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]] produces over the CpGs [[cpg-island-detection]] locates. Fixed tiles (`win.size=1000/step.size=1000/cov.bases=0`, `tileMethylCounts`), meth.diff=group2%вҲ’group1% (percentage points), per-window pooled 2Г—2 methylated/unmethylated counts вҶ’ Fisher's exact (one sample per group; replicatesвҶ’logistic regression out of scope), hypergeometric single-table p `(a+b)!(c+d)!(a+c)!(b+d)!/(a!b!c!d!n!)` + two-sided вүӨ-observed sum; report q<0.01 AND |meth.diff|>25 strict (`getMethylDiff`): hyper meth.diff>+25 / hypo <вҲ’25; emptyвҶ’no DMRs, zero-coverage group / zero marginalвҶ’p=1.0, |meth.diff|=25вҶ’excluded; oracles Fisher a=1/b=9/c=11/d=3вҶ’вүҲ0.001346076, hyper window g1=0.0/g2=1.0вҶ’+100/pвүҲ0; two evidence-backed assumptions (per-window pooling, numC/numT=round(levelГ—coverage)); research-grade (no logistic path/SLIM/overlapping tiles); siblings [[epigenetic-age-horvath-clock]]/[[chromatin-state-prediction]]; no contradictions.
- [[kmer-jaccard-similarity]] вҖ” Analysis alignment-free pairwise-similarity unit (`GENOMIC-SIMILARITY-001`, `GenomicAnalyzer.CalculateSimilarity`): Jaccard index of the two sequences' distinct k-mer sets (Jaccard 1901 `|AвҲ©B|/|AвҲӘB|` over HashSet k-mer sets, Ondov 2016 *Mash* fraction-of-shared-k-mers), exact (no MinHash sketch) JГ—100 in `[0,100]`, O(n+m); INV symmetry / identicalвҶ’100 / disjointвҶ’0 / distinct-set (repeats once); default k=5, empty-unionвҶ’0 (ASM-1 convention), Г—100 scaling; k=3 oracles 80/(100/3)/100/0; `alternative_to` positional [[alignment-statistics]], the 5-mer-Jaccard metric behind [[ortholog-detection-reciprocal-best-hits]] and the exact-set basis Mash sketches for [[average-nucleotide-identity]]; limitations = exact-match/composition-only; deviations None.
- [[k-mer-euclidean-distance]] вҖ” K-mer family alignment-free word-frequency **distance** unit (`KMER-DIST-001`, `KmerAnalyzer.KmerDistance`): Euclidean (L2) distance between two sequences' normalized k-mer **frequency** vectors `f_s(w)=count/(LвҲ’k+1)` over the union of observed k-mers (absent wordвҶ’0 component), exact/O(n+m); Zielezinski 2017 word-vector model + Lau 2022 frequency normalization + Vinga-Almeida 2003 4^k-vector + Boden 2014 relative-frequency Euclidean; INV d(x,x)=0 / symmetric / вүҘ0 / disjoint-single-kmerвҶ’вҲҡ2; вҲҡ0.11вүҲ0.3316624790 (ATGTGTG/CATGTG k=3) + вҲҡ0.125 (AAAA/AAAT k=1) oracles; case-insensitive (ASM-01) + empty/L<kвҶ’zero-vector (ASM-02); count-based/Manhattan/Canberra/Chebyshev/cosine/D2/spaced-word not implemented, deviations None; `alternative_to` the presence/absence [[kmer-jaccard-similarity]] (this captures abundance), shares the `CountKmers` primitive with [[both-strand-kmer-counting]]/[[asynchronous-kmer-counting]]; record [[kmer-dist-001-evidence]].
- [[asynchronous-kmer-counting]] вҖ” K-mer family async count unit (`KMER-ASYNC-001`, `KmerAnalyzer.CountKmersAsync`): the cooperatively cancelable, progress-reporting thread-pool wrapper over synchronous `CountKmers` вҖ” numeric result identical to the sync reference (counts fixed by the k-mer formula `L вҲ’ k + 1`, nбөҸ possible), so the distinctive validated content is *execution* not arithmetic: the .NET cancellation contract (`ThrowIfCancellationRequested`вҶ’OperationCanceledException + Canceled state, pre-start `Task.Run(func,token)` cancellation, awaiting a canceled task throws) + `IProgress<double>` 0вҶ’1.0; INV ОЈcounts=LвҲ’k+1 / emptyВ·k>LвҶ’empty dict / kвүӨ0вҶ’ArgumentOutOfRangeException via awaited task; uppercased (case-insensitive) + alphabet-agnostic (IUPAC N counted literally); ATGGвҶ’{ATG:1,TGG:1} + GTAGAGCTGT oracles; one assumption = numeric contract identical to sync (non-correctness-affecting); single-thread offload (not parallelized), suffix-tree evaluated-not-used; wraps sync KMER-COUNT-001 (not yet ingested); record [[kmer-async-001-evidence]].
- [[k-mer-generation]] вҖ” K-mer family *space-enumeration* unit (`KMER-GENERATE-001`, `KmerAnalyzer.GenerateAllKmers`): exhaustive enumeration of ALL possible k-mers of length `k` over an alphabet вҖ” the complete k-mer universe `ОЈ^k` of size `n^k` (4^k for DNA), depends only on `k`+alphabet not on any sequence; DISTINCT from counting (produces the full n^k word set / address space, siblings extract observed substrings + counts); k-fold Cartesian product `itertools.product(ОЈ,repeat=k)`, lazy recursive prefix-extension, odometer emission вҶ’ lexicographic for a sorted alphabet; INV n^k count / all-distinct-set / length-k / sortedвҶ’lexicographic; k=1вҶ’{A,C,G,T}, k=2вҶ’16 (AA..TT), k=3вҶ’64, protein 20^2=400, single-letter 1^4=1 oracles; kвүӨ0вҶ’ArgumentOutOfRangeException, empty alphabetвҶ’ArgumentException, unsortedвҶ’positional order, verbatim/no-dedup; O(kВ·n^k) time/O(k) lazy space, suffix-tree N/A (generates not searches); shares the "ACGT"-default + kвүӨ0-throws API contract with [[both-strand-kmer-counting]]/[[asynchronous-kmer-counting]]/[[k-mer-euclidean-distance]] but NOT the `CountKmers` primitive; supplies the index space for [[kmer-jaccard-similarity]]/[[k-mer-euclidean-distance]]/[[de-bruijn-graph-assembly]]; deviations None; record [[kmer-generate-001-evidence]].
- [[k-mer-positions]] вҖ” K-mer family *occurrence-index* unit (`KMER-POSITIONS-001`, `KmerAnalyzer.FindKmerPositions`): the ascending 0-based positions where a given k-mer occurs in a sequence вҖ” *where*, not *how many* (the inverse index to the counting units) вҖ” solving the exact Pattern Matching Problem `Occ(P,T)={iвҲҲ[0,LвҲ’k]:T[i..i+k)=P}` with all overlapping starts reported; INV-01..04 (match predicate / ascending / count=overlap-occurrences / range `[0,LвҲ’k]`, empty when k>L); case-insensitive upper-casing (sibling `CountKmers`), unrestricted-text alphabet, null/empty & k>L & absent вҶ’ empty (no throw), whole-seqвҶ’`[0]`; `ATAT`/`GATATATGCATATACTT`вҶ’`[1,3,9]` + `AA`/`AAAA`вҶ’`[0,1,2]` oracles; O(LВ·k) naive span scan, suffix-tree evaluated-not-used (unordered leaves, single-query no amortization); three API-shape assumptions (0-based, case-fold, empty-not-throw), deviations None; the single-pattern K-mer sibling of multi-pattern [[known-motif-search]], distinct from the counting siblings [[both-strand-kmer-counting]]/[[asynchronous-kmer-counting]]; record [[kmer-positions-001-evidence]].
- [[both-strand-kmer-counting]] вҖ” K-mer family strand-aware count unit (`KMER-BOTH-001`, `KmerAnalyzer.CountKmersBothStrands`): the ADDITIVE / kPAL-"balance" both-strand profile `count[w] = forward[w] + forward[RC(w)]` (count k-mers of S and of RC(S), sum per key), grounded in inversion symmetry (Shporer 2016) + kPAL balance (Anvar 2014); distinct from вҖ” and does NOT implement вҖ” the canonical-collapsing convention (lexicographically-smaller of {w,RC(w)} as one key, Jellyfish `-C` / Mash); INV ОЈcount=2В·(LвҲ’k+1) / count[w]=count[RC(w)] strand-symmetric / palindrome RC(w)=wвҶ’count doubled on one key; two linear passes O(nВ·k), suffix-tree evaluated-not-used; case-insensitive/IUPAC-complemented, emptyВ·k>LвҶ’empty dict, kвүӨ0вҶ’ArgumentOutOfRangeException (inherited from `CountKmers`); ATGGC k=2вҶ’{AT:2,TG:1,GG:1,GC:2,CC:1,CA:1} + ACGTвҶ’{AC:2,CG:2,GT:2} + AAAвҶ’{AA:2,TT:2} oracles; built on the same sync `CountKmers` primitive as [[asynchronous-kmer-counting]]; two API-shape assumptions, deviations None; record [[kmer-both-001-evidence]].
- [[k-mer-statistics]] вҖ” K-mer family *summary-statistics* unit (`KMER-STATS-001`, `KmerAnalyzer.AnalyzeKmers`): a companion summary layer over the shared `CountKmers` multiset that reduces the count profile to `KmerStatistics` {TotalKmers=LвҲ’k+1=ОЈcounts, UniqueKmers=**distinct** count, MaxCount, MinCount, AverageCount=total/distinct (rounded 2dp), Entropy=Shannon **k-entropy** `вҲ’ОЈ p(Оұ)logвӮӮp(Оұ)`, `p=mult/(LвҲ’k+1)`, bits}; the one distinct piece of content is the k-entropy (Manca 2021 + EntropyвҖ“Rank Ratio, corroborated by Wikipedia/BioInfoLogics count tables); GOTCHA `UniqueKmers` = distinct count NOT the count==1 singletons (that is KMER-UNIQUE-001); INV Total=ОЈcounts / Unique=distinct(CountKmers) / homopolymerвҶ’H0,max=min=total / all-distinctвҶ’H logвӮӮD,max=min=1 / k>LВ·emptyвҶ’all-zero; GTAGAGCTGT k=1 (10/4/4/1/2.5/1.8464) + k=3 (8/8/1/1/logвӮӮ8=3.0) + ATCGATCAC k=3 (7/6/2/1/2.5216) + AAAA k=2 (3/1/3/3/0) oracles; case-insensitive, kвүӨ0вҶ’ArgumentOutOfRangeException; two presentation-only assumptions (AverageCount 2dp, Entropy unrounded); shares the `CountKmers` primitive with [[asynchronous-kmer-counting]]/[[both-strand-kmer-counting]], distinct from generation/positions/distance siblings; deviations None; record [[kmer-stats-001-evidence]]. Also the home of the **second entry point** for the same k-entropy: `SequenceComplexity.CalculateKmerEntropy` (SEQ-COMPLEX-KMER-001, record [[seq-complex-kmer-001-evidence]]) вҖ” the entropy member of the `SEQ-COMPLEX-*` complexity family (siblings [[sequence-complexity-compression-lempel-ziv]]/[[dust-low-complexity-score]]), identical formula from a different class.
- [[unique-and-mincount-kmers]] вҖ” K-mer family *frequency-filtering* unit (`KMER-UNIQUE-001`, `KmerAnalyzer.FindUniqueKmers` + `FindKmersWithMinCount`): selects k-mers by their per-k-mer **Count** (overlapping occurrences, Compeau & Pevzner `Count(Text,Pattern)`) at opposite ends of the frequency distribution вҖ” `FindUniqueKmers` = the `Count==1` **singletons**, `FindKmersWithMinCount` = the `CountвүҘminCount` **recurrent** k-mers ordered by count desc; total/distinct/unique terminology (BioInfoLogics: unique = "appear only once"; Wikipedia LвҲ’k+1 total); GOTCHA "unique"=singleton set here вү  [[k-mer-statistics]]'s `UniqueKmers`=distinct count (ATCGATCAC k=3 вҶ’ 5 unique vs 6 distinct, ATC=2 excluded); oracles ATCGATCAC k=3вҶ’{TCG,CGA,GAT,TCA,CAC}, AGAT k=2вҶ’{AG,GA,AT}, ACGTACGT k=4 FindKmersWithMinCount(вҖҰ,2)вҶ’{(ACGT,2)}/(вҖҰ,1)вҶ’all-4-count-desc/FindUniqueKmersвҶ’{CGTA,GTAC,TACG}, AAAAA k=3вҶ’вҲ…; case-insensitive, kвүӨ0вҶ’ArgumentOutOfRangeException, emptyВ·k>LвҶ’empty; two assumptions (minCountвүӨ1вҶ’all distinct count-desc; upper-casing), deviations None; filters the shared `CountKmers` multiset like [[asynchronous-kmer-counting]]/[[both-strand-kmer-counting]]; record [[kmer-unique-001-evidence]].
- [[longest-common-substring]] вҖ” Sequence-Comparison longest-common-substring / common-region-detection unit (`GENOMIC-COMMON-001`): the maximal *contiguous* substring shared by two strings (distinct from the gapped longest common *subsequence*) via a generalized suffix tree (LCS = deepest internal node whose subtree holds leaves from both strings, Оҳ(n+m) build + DFS, Gusfield 1997); `FindLongestCommonRegion` (0-based positions in both) + `FindCommonRegions(minLength)` (all distinct shared runs вүҘ minLength), None=empty/len 0/pos вҲ’1, identicalвҶ’whole seq at 0/0; documented deterministic first-found-in-`other` tie-break (CACAGAG/TACATAGAT ties ACA vs AGA вҶ’ ACA); Wikipedia + GeeksforGeeks sources, shares the suffix-tree exact-match engine with [[dot-plot-word-match]]; deviations None.
- [[longest-repeated-substring]] вҖ” Repeat-Analysis LRS + repeat-enumeration unit (`GENOMIC-REPEAT-001`): the longest substring recurring within *one* DNA sequence (`GenomicAnalyzer.FindLongestRepeat`) + all distinct substrings occurring вүҘ2Г— with length вүҘ minLength (`FindRepeats`), both via the *single-string* suffix tree's deepest internal node with вүҘ2 leaves (string depth = repeat length; CMU В§2.1 / Wikipedia / GeeksforGeeks App-3 / Gusfield 5.4); overlaps counted, no-repeat/emptyвҶ’`RepeatInfo.None`, `minLengthвүӨ0`вҶ’`max(1,minLength)`, ACGT-only, no reverse-complement/maximal-repeat classification; FindRepeats via sorted-suffix adjacent-LCP *every-prefix* enumeration (O(nВІ), FINDINGS_REGISTER short-prefix fix); ATCGATCGAвҶ’ATCGA{0,4}, AAAAAAAAAAвҶ’AAAAAAAAA{0,1}, ATATATAвҶ’ATATA{0,2}, ACGTACGTTTTTACGT@3вҶ’8-substring oracles; the *single-string* sibling of [[longest-common-substring]], distinct from the tandem/inverted [[repetitive-element-detection]] anchor; tie-break + ascending-positions assumptions, deviations None.
- [[open-reading-frame-detection]] вҖ” Analysis ORF-detection unit (`GENOMIC-ORF-001`): six-frame ATGвҶ’first-in-frame-stop enumeration (`GenomicAnalyzer.FindOpenReadingFrames`), standard code (start ATG / stops TAA-TAG-TGA), reported span **includes** the stop (Length%3==0) while the translated protein **excludes** it; THE correctness rule = every in-frame ATG reaching a stop reported, so **nested ORFs sharing a stop** both returned (Rosalind `MGMTPRLGLESLLE`/`MTPRLGLESLLE`), ATG-with-no-stopвҶ’none; `minLength` in **nucleotides** inclusive (default 100), 0-based Position, Frame 1вҖ“3 + IsReverseComplement, INV-01..05 (starts ATG / ends stop / len%3==0 / вүҘminLength / six-frame), O(nВІ) worst / O(n) typical; Rosalind_99вҶ’4 distinct proteins + ATGAAAAAATAAвҶ’MKK oracles; Rosalind + Wikipedia + NCBI ORFfinder + transl_table=1 sources; deviations None (one fixed greedy bug); deliberately **not** contract-equivalent to annotation `GenomeAnnotator.FindOrfs` (ANNOT-ORF-001: ATG/GTG/TTG, aa-length, strand/start flags) or `Translator.FindOrfs` (genetic-code-parameterized); coding potential is a separate step ([[coding-potential-hexamer-score]]).
- [[known-motif-search]] вҖ” Motif-Analysis known-motif-search anchor (`GENOMIC-MOTIFS-001`): multi-pattern **exact** substring matching of a caller-supplied set of known query motifs (`GenomicAnalyzer.FindMotif`) вҖ” the "you know what you're looking for" exact-equality baseline, distinct from motif *discovery* and *degenerate* (IUPAC/PROSITE/PWM) matching; THE correctness rule = all **overlapping** occurrences reported (AAA in AAAAAвҶ’{0,1,2}, per Gusfield/Biopython `count_overlap` 3-not-2); 0-based sorted positions, per-motif position lists with absent motifs omitted, upper-cased result keys, empty/whitespace motifвҶ’no entry (`Array.Empty<int>()`); EcoRI GAATTCвҶ’{0,9} + `{ACGT,AA,TTT}` in ACGTACGTAA oracles; Tufts/Gusfield + Biopython `Seq.search` + Wikipedia "Restriction site" sources; shares exact-all-occurrences semantics with [[longest-common-substring]]/[[dot-plot-word-match]]; deviations None.
- [[alpha-diversity]] вҖ” Metagenomics diversity family anchor (first META-* unit, META-ALPHA-001): within-sample diversity indices from one taxonвҶ’abundance map (`MetagenomicsAnalyzer.CalculateAlphaDiversity` вҶ’ `AlphaDiversity` record) вҖ” observed richness S_obs, Shannon H=вҲ’ОЈpбөўln(pбөў) in nats, Simpson concentration О»=ОЈpбөўВІ, inverse Simpson 1/О» (Hill order-2 effective species), Pielou evenness J=H/ln(S) for S>1 else 0, Chao1 S_obs+fвӮҒВІ/(2fвӮӮ) (fвӮӮ=0вҶ’bias-corrected S_obs+fвӮҒ(fвӮҒвҲ’1)/2, non-integer/proportionalвҶ’S_obs); Whittaker 1960 Оұ/ОІ/Оі framework, Shannon 1948/Simpson 1949/Hill 1973/Chao 1984/Pielou 1966; counts-or-proportions internally normalized, non-positive filtered, O(n); empty/nullвҶ’all-0, single speciesвҶ’H0/О»1/J0; one accepted deviation = Chao1 count-vs-proportion gate; between-sample [[beta-diversity]] its sibling; deviations else None.
- [[metagenomic-binning]] вҖ” Metagenomics family binning unit (third META-* unit, META-BIN-001, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.BinContigs`): groups mixed-community contigs back to their genome of origin (MAGs) by k-means over a composite distance `|О”GC|+|О”coverage|+TNF-Pearson-distance` (GC-sorted deterministic centroid init, вүӨ50 iters, minBinSize 500 kb filter) вҶ’ `GenomeBin` records; completeness=`min(L/expectedGenomeSizeГ—100,100)` (default 4 Mbp) + contamination=`min(gcStdDev/0.5Г—100,100)` are LENGTH-RATIO/GC-VARIANCE **proxies** (CheckM marker-gene QC now built as a SEPARATE opt-in path вҖ” CheckM Eqs. 1вҖ“2 over CC0 Pfam marker sets, `EstimateBinQualityFromMarkerCounts`/`DetectMarkers`, NOT wired into `BinContigs`; see [[meta-bin-001-markerqc-evidence]]); INV unique BinId / metrics [0,100] / GC [0,1] / TotalLength=ОЈ / disjoint partition / Coverage=mean; M5 50.0 / M6 0-100 / M7 1.0-0.0 / M12 25 oracles; opt-in TETRA z-score signature (`CalculateTetranucleotideZScores`/`TetranucleotideZScoreCorrelation`) вҖ” RC-extended strand, 256-word Markov expectation `E=N(n1n2n3)В·N(n2n3n4)/N(n2n3)`, Schbath variance, Pearson correlation of z-vectors (scale-invariant), z(ACGT)=вҲҡ5 for ACGTACGTGGCC, N(n2n3)=0/non-positive-varвҶ’z=0; Maguire 2020 limits (plasmids 1-29%/GIs 38-44% poorly recovered), similar-GC+coverageвҶ’co-bin; three prior assumptions resolved, deviations None; record [[meta-bin-001-evidence]]; Metagenomics-family sibling of [[alpha-diversity]]/[[beta-diversity]].
- [[taxonomic-classification]] вҖ” Metagenomics family taxonomic-classification unit (fourth META-* unit, META-CLASS-001, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.ClassifyReads` + `BuildKmerDatabase` + `TaxonomyTree.Lca`): faithful Kraken (Wood & Salzberg 2014) per-read/contig assignment вҖ” canonical-k-mer (`min(kmer,revcomp)`, default k=31) database mapping each k-mer to the **LCA of all owning reference taxa**, per-read **classification tree** (hit taxa + ancestors weighted by k-mer count) scored over **root-to-leaf (RTL)** paths вҶ’ assigned taxon = max-scoring path's leaf, equal-max вҶ’ LCA of leaves, no k-mer hits вҶ’ **Unclassified** (taxonomy root, C=0); Confidence = **C/Q** (Kraken 2: C = clade k-mers under assigned label, Q = non-ambiguous k-mers queried); ambiguous (non-ACGT) k-mers skipped/not in Q, upper-cased, semicolon/pipe taxonomy strings; invariants |out|=|in| / 0вүӨC/QвүӨ1 / CвүӨQ / Q=lenвҲ’k+1 (all-ACGT) / canonical uniqueness / DB-build LCA / LCA siblingsвҶ’parent, ancestor/descendantвҶ’ancestor, selfвҶ’self, disjointвҶ’root; empty/short-<k/no-match вҶ’ Unclassified, empty DB вҶ’ all Unclassified; scoped to **per-read classification** (abundance *profiling* Taxonomic_Profile is a separate later unit); research-grade, no deviations / no open questions; siblings [[metagenomic-binning]] (per-contig MAGs) & [[alpha-diversity]]/[[beta-diversity]] (consume the abundance profile); record [[meta-class-001-evidence]].
- [[beta-diversity]] вҖ” Metagenomics diversity family between-sample unit (second META-* unit, META-BETA-001): between-sample dissimilarity from two taxonвҶ’abundance maps (`MetagenomicsAnalyzer.CalculateBetaDiversity` вҶ’ `BetaDiversity` record) вҖ” Bray-Curtis BC=1вҲ’2В·ОЈmin(N_ij,N_ik)/ОЈ(N_ij+N_ik) (abundance-sensitive, range [0,1], NOT a true metric) + Jaccard distance J=1вҲ’|AвҲ©B|/|AвҲӘB| (presence/absence via abundance>0, true distance metric); Whittaker 1960 Оұ/ОІ/Оі (beta=turnover), Bray & Curtis 1957, Jaccard 1901; single union-pass O(u), no BC normalization (caller-scaled), +SharedSpecies/UniqueToSample1/2 counts; identicalвҶ’0/0, disjointвҶ’1/1, both-emptyвҶ’0/0 & one-emptyвҶ’1 guards; fish-tank BC 13/33 & J 1/3, symmetry BC 3/5 & J 2/3 oracles; one accepted deviation = UniFracDistance placeholder 0 (no phylo tree); within-sample sibling [[alpha-diversity]]; ecological-Jaccard shares the index math but not domain with sequence [[kmer-jaccard-similarity]].
- [[functional-prediction]] вҖ” Metagenomics family functional-prediction unit (fifth META-* unit, META-FUNC-001, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.PredictFunctions` + `FindPathwayEnrichment`): predicts a community's *functional* capability (PICRUSt / KO-pathway style) in two exact-numeric pieces вҖ” (A) homology-based annotation transfer: exact-signature `string.Contains` hit scored by BLOSUM62 self-score S, bit `S'=(О»SвҲ’lnK)/ln2` and E-value `E=KВ·mВ·nВ·e^(вҲ’О»S)=mВ·nВ·2^(вҲ’S')` (ungapped BLOSUM62 О»=0.3176/K=0.134, Altschul/`blast_stat.c`), best hit = lowest E-value / highest bit (INV-01..03,06); (B) hypergeometric pathway ORA `P(XвүҘx)=1вҲ’ОЈ C(M,i)C(NвҲ’M,nвҲ’i)/C(N,n)` in log-Gamma space, background=union-of-pathways default + query unioned in, sorted ascending, pвҲҲ[0,1], x/M/n=0вҶ’p=1 (INV-04,05); oracles WWWвҶ’S'18.0202932787533/E 3.3852730346546eвҲ’5 + N8000/M400/n100/x20вҶ’7.88eвҲ’8; *Simplified* вҖ” exact substring not gapped alignment (ASM-01, divergent homologs missed), no gapped О»/K / composition stats / HMM / FDR; asks "what can they do" vs the "who is there" of [[taxonomic-classification]]/[[metagenomic-binning]] and the diversity of [[alpha-diversity]]/[[beta-diversity]]; BLAST significance distinct from percent-id [[alignment-statistics]]; ORA half owned by [[pathway-enrichment-ora]] (the dedicated META-PATHWAY-001 unit); record [[meta-func-001-evidence]].
- [[pathway-enrichment-ora]] вҖ” Metagenomics family pathway-enrichment unit (META-PATHWAY-001, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.FindPathwayEnrichment` / `HypergeometricUpperTail`): the GO::TermFinder / clusterProfiler over-representation statistic вҖ” score each pathway by the hypergeometric **right-tail** `P(XвүҘx)=1вҲ’ОЈ_{i=0}^{xвҲ’1}C(M,i)C(NвҲ’M,nвҲ’i)/C(N,n)` (N=background, M=pathway size, n=query, x=overlap; sampling without replacement, upper tail only), `phyper(xвҲ’1,M,NвҲ’M,n,lower.tail=FALSE)` reference (the q=xвҲ’1 shift gives P(XвүҘx)); log-Gamma summation to N=8000, pвҲҲ[0,1], pathways sorted ascending; p=1 when x/M/n=0, **MвҶ”n symmetry**, without-replacement feasibility drops C(В·,В·)=0 terms; background = explicit `backgroundGenes` else union-of-pathway-members default (query always unioned in), members intersected with background; **no BH/Bonferroni FDR** correction; Boyle 2004 + PNNL ORA В§8.2 sources, oracles 7.88eвҲ’8 + 1/252 + 5/6 + 251/252; one caller-overridable background-defaulting assumption; **owns** the ORA machinery that [[functional-prediction]] uses as component B; generic statistic (GO/proteomics), research-grade, no contradictions; record [[meta-pathway-001-evidence]].
- [[taxonomic-profile]] вҖ” Metagenomics family community-abundance profiling unit (sixth META-* unit, META-PROF-001, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.GenerateTaxonomicProfile`): the **aggregation/estimation** step downstream of per-read [[taxonomic-classification]] вҖ” takes an `IEnumerable<TaxonomicClassification>` and returns a `TaxonomicProfile` with **relative-abundance maps at four ranks** (kingdom/phylum/genus/species, abundance = count(taxon)/ОЈcount(classified)), **inline species-level diversity** (Shannon H=вҲ’ОЈpбөўln(pбөў) in nats + Simpson concentration О»=ОЈpбөўВІ), and **read counts** (TotalReads/ClassifiedReads); Unclassified excluded from denominators, empty rank strings filtered, per-rank ОЈвүҲ1.0; invariants ClassifiedReadsвүӨTotalReads / ClassifiedReads=ОЈ(counts any rank) / ShannonвүҘ0 / 0вүӨSimpsonвүӨ1; oracles Shannon=ln(3) (3 uniform), Simpson=0.375 ([2,1,1]); emptyвҶ’0/0/empty & single taxonвҶ’1.0/H0/О»1 (vs emptyвҶ’О»0); count-based tally (NOT MetaPhlAn marker-coverage, no genome-size correction), inherits upstream classifier accuracy; the profiling unit [[taxonomic-classification]] deliberately deferred, sibling of [[alpha-diversity]] (richer six-index within-sample summary) / [[beta-diversity]]; MetaPhlAn/Segata 2012, research-grade, no contradictions; record [[meta-prof-001-evidence]].
- [[antibiotic-resistance-gene-detection]] вҖ” Metagenomics family AMR gene-detection unit (seventh META-* unit, META-RESIST-001, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.FindAntibioticResistanceGenes`): ResFinder-style screen of assembled contigs against a **caller-supplied** resistance-gene reference DB, reporting the single **best-matching gene per contig** вҖ” `BestUngappedMatch` slides each reference across the contig (offsets вҲ’(mвҲ’1)..nвҲ’1, overhanging both ends), keeps the max-match window (tieвҶ’shorter/higher-identity), then identity=matches/w (BLAST gapless, Heng Li 2018) & coverage=w/m (fraction of **reference** length, so contig-edge/split genes still scored), reported iff identityвүҘidThreshold AND coverageвүҘcovThreshold; best match = max identity, tieвҶ’max coverage (Zankari 2012 "best-matching gene", CARD RGI best-hit); INV-01..05, defaults 0.90 ID / 0.60 cov (named constants), Perfect=1.0/1.0 (CARD); oracles CGTACGT@AAACGTACGTвҶ’1.0/1.0, CGTTCGT vs CGTACGTвҶ’6/7вүҲ0.857/1.0, edge CGTAвҶ’1.0 / 4вҒ„7вүҲ0.571; *Simplified* вҖ” gapless ungapped (ASM-01, indel matches under-scored vs gapped BLAST; substitution + edge-truncation exact), no SNP/protein-homology (CARD variant/homolog models out of scope), nucleotide-only case-sensitive, legacy `FindResistanceGenes` motif stub separate; asks "**which known resistance genes are present**" vs the who/what/how-diverse of [[taxonomic-classification]]/[[functional-prediction]]/[[alpha-diversity]]; BLAST-style homology screen sharing machinery with [[functional-prediction]] but scoring nucleotide identity/coverage not BLOSUM62 bit-score (identity denominator = [[alignment-statistics]] rule); provenance note flagged (evidence 0.80/0.98 vs impl 0.90 default); record [[meta-resist-001-evidence]].
- [[significant-taxa-detection]] вҖ” Metagenomics family differential-abundance unit (eighth META-* unit, META-TAXA-001, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.MannWhitneyU` / `FindSignificantTaxa`): per-taxon **two-group MannвҖ“Whitney U (Wilcoxon rank-sum)** test asking "which taxa differ in abundance between two groups?" вҖ” non-parametric, rank-based, suits compositional/zero-inflated data (Xia & Sun 2017). PoolвҶ’midranks (tied values averaged, accumulate ОЈ(tВівҲ’t))вҶ’`U1=R1вҲ’n1(n1+1)/2`, `U2=n1В·n2вҲ’U1`; `m_U=n1В·n2/2`, tie-corrected `Пғ_U=sqrt(n1В·n2В·(n1+n2+1)/12 вҲ’ n1В·n2В·ОЈ(tВівҲ’t)/(12n(nвҲ’1)))`; `z=(|UвҲ’m_U|вҲ’cc)/Пғ_U` on `max(U1,U2)`, ccвҲҲ{0,0.5} (0.5 on by default = SciPy `use_continuity`); two-tailed `p=2В·(1вҲ’ОҰ(z))` clamped [0,1], ОҰ via `StatisticsHelper.NormalCDF` (A&S 7.1.26, вүҲ1eвҲ’6 accuracy). `FindSignificantTaxa` runs it per taxon over label-defined ({1,2}) groups вҶ’ `SignificantTaxon` ascending by p. INV-01..06 (U1+U2=n1В·n2, 0вүӨUвүӨn1В·n2, pвҲҲ[0,1], SignificantвҮ”p<threshold, all-tiedвҶ’Пғ0вҶ’z0вҶ’p1, group-swap symmetric); oracles SciPy x[19,22,16,29,24]/y[20,11,17,12]вҶ’U1=17/U2=3/Пғ=4.0825/z_cc=1.5922вҶ’pвүҲ0.11135 (z_nocc=1.7146вҶ’pвүҲ0.08641) + tortoise/hare U_T=11/U_H=25/sum=36; empty groupвҶ’ArgumentException, absent taxonвҶ’abundance 0 (ASM-03); asymptotic-not-exact, no FDR (caller applies BH), ignores compositionality; **consumes** [[taxonomic-profile]] abundance vectors; distinct-by-**test** from the hypergeometric [[pathway-enrichment-ora]] and Fisher's-exact [[differentially-methylated-regions]]; siblings [[alpha-diversity]] / [[beta-diversity]]; record [[meta-taxa-001-evidence]].
- [[methylation-context-classification]] вҖ” epigenetics family CpG/CHG/CHH context-classification unit (sixth/final EPIGEN-* unit, EPIGEN-METHYL-001): sequence-only trinucleotide classifier partitioning cytosines into CpG/CHG/CHH from the downstream base(s) вҖ” distinct because it handles the *non-CpG* CHG/CHH contexts [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]] does not call from reads. Rule (Cornish-Bowden 1985 IUPAC H={A,C,T}="not G"): CpGвҹәbвӮҒ=G, CHGвҹәbвӮҒвҲҲH & bвӮӮ=G, CHHвҹәbвӮҒвҲҲH & bвӮӮвҲҲH; CpG/CHG symmetric, CHH asymmetric (Krueger-Andrews 2011). Three ops on `EpigeneticsAnalyzer`: `GetMethylationContext` (O(1), null when not a classifiable C), `FindMethylationSites` (O(n) scan вҶ’ one site/classifiable C, 0-based, sequence-only level=0/coverage=0 placeholder), `GenerateMethylationProfile` (shared with [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]], Schultz 2012 weighted ОЈ(levelВ·cov)/ОЈcov, zero-coverageвҶ’unweighted-mean fallback); CGACAGCAAвҶ’CpG@0/CHG@3/CHH@6 + weighted (8+2)/(10+10)=0.5 oracles; G-never-H (CGGвҶ’CpG), terminal-CG-still-CpG, incomplete-trailing / non-ACGT unclassified; Lister 2009 realism (IMR90 99.98% CG vs H1 ES ~25% non-CG); single-strand only, no symmetric-strand pairing; two assumptions (level=0 placeholder, 0.5 MethylatedCpG count cutoff); no contradictions.
- [[rna-base-pairing]] вҖ” MiRNA family anchor + shared RNA base-pairing primitive (first MiRNA unit, MIRNA-PAIR-001, `MiRnaAnalyzer`): deciding **whether two RNA bases can pair** and building the antiparallel miRNA-mRNA duplex from that rule. `CanPair`вҹә{A-U,U-A,G-C,C-G,G-U,U-G} = Watson-Crick {A-U,G-C} (Agarwal 2015) + the single standard **G-U wobble** (Crick 1966); `IsWobblePair`вҹә{G-U,U-G}, wobbleвҠҶpairable, wobble counted **separately** from matches (PMC4870184). `GetReverseComplement` = antiparallel RNA reverse complement for seedвҶ’target motif (Lewis 2005; let-7a `GAGGUAG`вҶ’`CUACCUC`). `AlignMiRnaToTarget` pairs miRNA[i]вҶ”target[lenвҲ’1вҲ’i] over the shorter overlap, ungapped, emitting `|`(WC)/`:`(wobble)/space(mismatch); counts sum to min(len), Gaps=0; О”G = **simplified** Turner-2004 stacking sum over consecutive paired runs (sign reliable вҖ” fully-WC вүӨ0, all-mismatch вүҘ0 вҖ” magnitude not). Oracles AAAA/UUUUвҶ’4 matches, GGGG/UUUUвҶ’4 wobbles, AAAA/AAAAвҶ’4 mismatches; DNA TвҶ’U normalised, unknown baseвҶ’N never pairs, emptyвҶ’empty duplex. The **shared** pairing rule RNA secondary-structure classification also uses; **not** target-site efficacy prediction (that is `FindTargetSites`/MIRNA-TARGET-001), and the A-opposite-position-1 preference is Argonaute recognition, not base pairing; record [[mirna-pair-001-evidence]].
- [[pre-mirna-hairpin-detection]] вҖ” MiRNA family precursor-hairpin unit (second MiRNA unit, MIRNA-PRECURSOR-001, `MiRnaAnalyzer`): finding stem-loop pre-miRNA precursors (~60-120 nt) from which Dicer excises the ~22 nt mature duplex. **Default heuristic** `FindPreMiRnaHairpins` counts uninterrupted complementary pairs ({A-U,G-C}+G-U wobble, [[rna-base-pairing]] primitive) from both ends inward вҶ’ accept iff stem вүҘ18 bp (Krol 2004) + loop 3-25 nt (Bartel 2004); extracts mature(5' arm)/star(3' arm), balanced dot-bracket, Turner-2004 О”G; **documented limitation** вҖ” consecutive-pairing is stricter than real structure, rejects natural miRBase precursors (hsa-mir-21 16 end-pairs, let-7a-1 5, tests M18/M19). **Opt-in** `AssessHairpinByMfe`/`FindPreMiRnaHairpinsByMfe` fold with the RNA-STRUCT-001 ZukerвҖ“Stiegler engine and read the hairpin from the real MFE structure (single dominant hairpin/no multibranch + stem вүҘ16 (Ambros 2003) + loop 3-25 + MFEI вүҘ0.85 (Zhang 2006, AMFE=100В·|О”GВ°|/n, MFEI=AMFE/GC%)) вҶ’ detects hsa-mir-21 (О”GВ° вҲ’35.13/MFEI 1.0037) & let-7a-1; rejects a stronger-О”GВ° multibranch 5S-rRNA-like on **structure**. **Opt-in** `PredictDroshaDicerCleavage` = published ruler (Drosha +11 bp basal junction/Han 2006, Dicer 22-nt 5'-count/Park 2011, RNase III 2-nt overhang/Lee 2003, CNNC 16-18 nt confidence flag/Auyeung 2013; hsa-miR-21-5p cross-check). **Opt-in** `ClassifyPreMiRna` = logistic regression over [О”G,AMFE,MFEI,GC,%paired], 13 public-domain miRBase positives vs Altschul-Erickson di-shuffle negatives (Bonnet 2004 convention), held-out AUC 1.0, no GPL miRDeep2 code; read-stacking miRDeep2 signal out of scope (needs reads); record [[mirna-precursor-001-evidence]].
- [[seed-sequence-analysis]] вҖ” MiRNA family seed-extraction unit (third MiRNA unit, MIRNA-SEED-001, `MiRnaAnalyzer`): **string-level** extraction and comparison of the mature-miRNA 5' seed вҖ” the primary determinant of animal target recognition вҖ” not binding prediction. `GetSeedSequence` returns positions **2-8** (7 nt, extended seed) via `Substring(1,7)` uppercase (casing only, **no** TвҶ’U); `<8 nt`/null/empty вҶ’ `""`. `CreateMiRna(name, sequence)` normalises `ToUpperInvariant()`+`TвҶ’U`, extracts the seed from the normalised sequence, stores `SeedSequence` + fixed **zero-based** `SeedStart=1`/`SeedEnd=7`. `CompareSeedRegions` = Hamming over the 7-nt seed (`Matches`+`Mismatches`=7, mismatches also count any length diff), `IsSameFamily` вҹә **exact seed-string equality**; empty seed вҶ’ zeroed result. **miRNA family = identical 2-8 seed** (let-7a/-7b/-7c-5p all `GAGGUAG` вҶ’ same family; miR-21-5p `AGCUUAU` differs); selfвҶ’0 mismatches. Domain context: TargetScan site ladder 8mer/7mer-m8/7mer-A1/6mer over the 2-7-vs-2-8 distinction, but matching-to-target + site-class assignment is deferred to target-site prediction (MIRNA-TARGET-001, future); seedвҶ’target motif reverse complement is owned by [[rna-base-pairing]] (`GetReverseComplement`). **Intentionally simplified** вҖ” exact-7-mer family equality (no isomiR/offset/noncanonical seeds, not a curated taxonomy); 2-7-vs-2-8 terminology collapse flagged, no source contradictions; record [[mirna-seed-001-evidence]].
- [[mirna-target-site-prediction]] вҖ” MiRNA family target-site-prediction unit (fourth & **final** MiRNA unit, MIRNA-TARGET-001, `MiRnaAnalyzer`, **completes** the family): finding mRNA target sites for a miRNA and classifying the **Bartel/TargetScan hierarchy**. `FindTargetSites(mRna, miRna, minScore=0.5)` = two-pass, `TвҶ’U`, 0-based-inclusive antiparallel scan for the seed reverse complement (`seedRC=revcomp(mвӮӮвҖҰmвӮҲ)`, 6mer core `seedRC[2..7]`): pass-1 upgrades 6mer-core hits to **8mer** (pos 2-8 + A opposite pos 1) / **7mer-m8** (2-8) / **7mer-A1** (2-7 + A1) / **6mer** (2-7); pass-2 finds **offset-6mer** (3-8) only where not overlapping a retained higher-priority site (INV-04). Heuristic `ScoreвҲҲ[0,1]` (base 1.0/0.52/0.32/0.15/0.10, +0.05 >10 matches, вҲ’0.01/mismatch) + heuristic `FreeEnergy` (sign-reliable) вҖ” ranking aid, **not** calibrated repression. **Depends on** [[seed-sequence-analysis]] (the 2-8 seed determines targeting) + [[rna-base-pairing]] (`GetReverseComplement` motif + `AlignMiRnaToTarget` `|`/`:`/space duplex). **Opt-in `ScoreTargetSiteContextPlusPlus`** = source-fitted TargetScan **context++** (Agarwal 2015): per-site-type MLR, sum of `coeffГ—scaledScore`, continuous features min-max scaled + indicators raw; realises Intercept/Local_AU/sRNA1/sRNA8/Site8/3P_score/Min_dist/Len_3UTR/Off6m, **computes** TA_3UTR=log10 N (`ComputeTa3Utr`, Garcia 2011) + SA (Turner-2004 McCaskill partition unpaired-prob) + PCT (Friedman BlsвҶ’published sigmoid); SPS/Len_ORF/ORF8m/PCT-`b0..b3` caller-supplied (compiled TargetScan tables, not bundled) вҶ’ honest **partial** `ContextScorePartial` + `OmittedFeatures` (8mer let-7a all-G-flank partial CS = вҲ’0.7561913315126536). `Centered`/`Supplementary` enum members not emitted (accepted); bulged/centered/supplementary/noncanonical + isoforms out of scope; no contradictions; record [[mirna-target-001-evidence]].
- [[rna-dot-bracket-notation]] вҖ” RNA secondary-structure family **notation layer** (RNA-DOTBRACKET-001, `RnaSecondaryStructure`): parse an extended-**WUSS** structure string into base pairs `(i,j)` and validate well-formedness. `ParseDotBracket` uses **one stack per bracket family** вҖ” `()`/`<>`/`{}`/`[]` + uppercase(5' open)/lowercase(3' close) letter pairs вҖ” each an **independent pairing system** (ViennaRNA / Infernal `vrna_db_from_WUSS()`: any matched pair = a base pair, symbol has no meaning); a shared stack would mis-pair `([)]`. `ValidateDotBracket` вҹә every family's stack empty at end & never underflows; a closer must match a **same-family** opener. **Pseudoknots** (crossing families) are valid; `(]` (mismatched families) is not. Non-bracket WUSS symbols `-`/`,`/`:`/`.` are single-stranded (Rfam). Oracles `((((....))))`вҶ’4 pairs, `([)]`вҶ’(0,2)+(1,3), `<<<<[[[[....>>>>]]]]`вүЎ`((((AAAA....))))aaaa`вҶ’two crossing 4-bp helices; valid `(((...)))`/`(([[]]))`/`([)]`, invalid `(((...)` / `...)` / `)(` / `(]`. Notation-only (does not fold/score); distinct from the base-pairing chemistry [[rna-base-pairing]]; the structure the [[pre-mirna-hairpin-detection]] unit emits and the MFE folder reads. Two API-contract assumptions (malformedвҶ’best-effort parse; empty/nullвҶ’valid). Record [[rna-dotbracket-001-evidence]].
- [[rna-free-energy-turner-model]] вҖ” RNA secondary-structure family **energy layer** (RNA-ENERGY-001, `RnaSecondaryStructure`): the individual **Turner 2004 nearest-neighbor free-energy terms** summed into a fold's О”GВ° at 37 В°C (`CalculateStackingEnergy`/`CalculateStemEnergy`/`CalculateHairpinLoopEnergy`/`CalculateMinimumFreeEnergy`), all verified exact against **NNDB Turner04**. Model `О”GВ°total = init + ОЈstacking + ОЈloops`. **WC stacking all negative**, GC-rich most stable (`GC/CG` вҲ’3.42, `GG/CC` вҲ’3.26; `AA/UU` вҲ’0.93); **G-U wobble variable** вҖ” mostly negative but **two positive** (`UG/GU` +0.30, `GU/UG` +1.29), note-a `GG/UU`=вҲ’0.5, **note-b special 3-stack** `5'GGUC/3'CUGG`=вҲ’4.12 (vs вҲ’1.77). **Hairpin-loop initiation positive and NOT monotonic** (3вҶ’5.4, 4вҶ’5.6, 6вҶ’5.4, 8вҶ’5.5, 9вҶ’6.4; Jacobson-Stockmayer `О”G(n)=О”G(9)+1.75RTВ·ln(n/9)` beyond 9). **Special UNCG/GNRA tri/tetra/hexaloops** use NNDB total energies keyed by closing pair+loop (replace the model; GNRA>random). **All-C loop** penalty (3-nt +1.5, >3-nt 0.3n+1.6), terminal mismatch (96 entries), **+0.45 per-AU/GU-end**. A single base pair contributes **0** stacking (needs вүҘ2 adjacent); empty/poly-AвҶ’0. Oracles GC 3-bp stem вҲ’5.78, NNDB hairpin example-1 `GGGAUAAAUCCC` вҲ’3.42, GGUC/CUGG вҲ’4.12. The **energy** the folding units consume (pre-miRNA `FreeEnergy`, RNA-STRUCT-001 MFE), assigned to [[rna-base-pairing]] pairs, distinct from the [[rna-dot-bracket-notation]] notation. No contradictions; three defined conditions (37 В°C, 2-dp, unknown stacksвҶ’0), not assumptions. Record [[rna-energy-001-evidence]].
- [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding]] вҖ” RNA secondary-structure family **folding/search layer** (RNA-MFE-001, `RnaSecondaryStructure`): the **ZukerвҖ“Stiegler dynamic-programming MFE folder** that searches structure space for the fold of lowest total free energy (`CalculateMinimumFreeEnergy` / `PredictStructure`). Loop decomposition (hairpin / stacking / bulge-interior / multibranch); DP matrices **C(i,j)=min(hairpin, interior/bulge over an inner pair, multiloop)** + multiloop **M** (вүҘ1 component)/**M1** (exactly one) + exterior **F** (Ward 2017); **standard affine multiloop model вҶ’ O(nВі) time / O(nВІ) space** ("simplest model is best"; logarithmic model would be O(nвҒҙ)). The unit that **consumes** the [[rna-free-energy-turner-model]] Turner-2004 terms (summing them over candidate structures) and **produces** a [[rna-dot-bracket-notation]] structure; builds on [[rna-base-pairing]]. Oracles `CACAAAAAAAUGUG`вҶ’`((((......))))` вҲ’1.41 (NNDB Example 1), `CACAGAAAGUGUG` вҲ’1.91 (Example 2). Invariants MFE вүӨ 0 (INV-01, empty structure always available), suffix-monotone `MFE(s) вүӨ MFE(prefix)` (INV-02), optimized DP == classic O(nВі) baseline (INV-03); empty/null / unfoldable homopolymer / sequence `< minLoopSize+2` вҶ’ 0 (hairpin loop вүҘ 3 nt); intramolecular вҮ’ no helix-init constant. The folder the [[pre-mirna-hairpin-detection]] opt-in `AssessHairpinByMfe` path uses (once generically called *RNA-STRUCT-001* before that artifact was ingested вҖ” RNA-STRUCT-001 is now the **distinct sibling** Nussinov predictor [[rna-secondary-structure-prediction]], sharing this unit's Zuker MFE machinery). Two documented simplifications (multiloop per-unpaired `c=0`; 2-dp rounding), no source contradictions; sources Zuker & Stiegler 1981 + Lorenz 2011 (ViennaRNA) + Ward 2017 + NNDB Turner 2004 + Mathews 2004. Record [[rna-mfe-001-evidence]].
- [[rna-partition-function-mccaskill]] вҖ” RNA secondary-structure family **probabilistic/ensemble layer** (RNA-PARTITION-001, `RnaSecondaryStructure`): the **McCaskill 1990** partition function вҖ” the Boltzmann-weighted counterpart of MFE folding that computes the equilibrium `Z = ОЈ_P exp(вҲ’E(P)/RT)` over all pseudoknot-free structures plus per-base-pair binding probabilities and the Boltzmann probability of a given structure, in **O(nВі) time / O(nВІ) space**. Inside recursion `Q_ij = Q_{i,j-1} + ОЈ_{iвүӨk<j-m} Q_{i,k-1}В·Q^b_{kj}` (base `Q_ij=1` for iвүҘjвҲ’m), total **`Z = Q_{1n}`** (disjoint/unambiguous decomposition); pair probability needs the **outside** recursion `p_kl = Q^b_klВ·O_kl/Z` вҖ” the external-only term is **wrong for nestable pairs** (`GGGAAACCC` P(2,6)=6/20 not 1/20; outside matches Boltzmann brute force to 3.3e-16). Oracles (E_bp=0 вҮ’ Z counts structures) `AAAA`вҶ’1, `GC`вҶ’1, `GGGGCCCC`вҶ’16, `GGGAAACCC`вҶ’20; invariants Z вүҘ 1 (empty structure weight 1), P(i,j) вҲҲ [0,1] + symmetric, per-base pairing sum вүӨ 1, monotone in E_bp; WC + GU pairing only, min-loop forbids jвҲ’k вүӨ m. The **`alternative_to` / ensemble counterpart** of the single-optimum [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding]] MFE folder; Boltzmann-weights the [[rna-free-energy-turner-model]] energies (ViennaRNA default 37 В°C = Turner standard); builds on [[rna-base-pairing]]. One simplification (fixed-per-pair `E_bp` energy model vs full Turner NN вҖ” energy model only, invariants conformant with McCaskill 1990), no source contradictions. Record [[rna-partition-001-evidence]].
- [[rna-pseudoknot-prediction]] вҖ” RNA secondary-structure family **crossing-helix layer** (RNA-PKPREDICT-001, `RnaSecondaryStructure`): predict the optimal fold that may contain a single **canonical H-type pseudoknot** вҖ” two helices whose pairs **cross** (`i<k<j<l`), the one feature the nested [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding|MFE folder]] and [[rna-partition-function-mccaskill|McCaskill ensemble]] cannot represent. **pknotsRG class** (Reeder & Giegerich 2004): "two crossing helices with three intervening loops", H-type 5'вҶ’3' stem1-5'вҶ’loop1вҶ’stem2-5'вҶ’loop2вҶ’stem1-3'вҶ’loop3вҶ’stem2-3', two-layer dot-bracket `((((..[[[[..))))..]]]]`; full grammar **O(nвҒҙ)/O(nВІ)**. Canonization rules (equal-length bulge-free helices / maximal extent / fixed overlap boundary) bound the search. Energy = Turner NN stacking on **both** helices (same model as nested, `Energy.lhs`) + penalties **initiation 9.0** (anti-spurious-knot gate вҖ” a knot is reported only when it beats both the penalty and the best nested alternative) / **unpaired loop nt 0.3** / **base pair inside knot 0.0** kcal/mol. **Depends on** [[rna-free-energy-turner-model]] (helix scoring) and [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding]] (MFE fallback baseline `FreeEnergy вүӨ CalculateMfeStructure().FreeEnergy` + folds internal loops); emits two-layer [[rna-dot-bracket-notation]]; builds on [[rna-base-pairing]]. Oracles designed H-type `GGGGAACCCCAACCCCAAGGGG`вҶ’knot with two crossing 4-bp helices; plain `GGGGAAAACCCC`вҶ’no knot = MFE; BWYV `GGCGCGGCACCGUCCGCGGAACAAACGG` (PDB 437D) **not** recovered (tertiary-stabilized, outside NN model вҖ” documented limit of all NN-only pseudoknot predictors). Two boundaries: PARTIAL pknotsRG coverage (single H-type only; recursive/over-arching/multiple knots not implemented) + tertiary-stabilized knots not recovered. No contradictions. Record [[rna-pkpredict-001-evidence]].
- [[rna-pseudoknot-detection]] вҖ” RNA secondary-structure family **crossing detection layer** (RNA-PSEUDOKNOT-001, `RnaSecondaryStructure.DetectPseudoknots`): given a **set of base pairs** describing a known structure, a pure **O(nВІ) combinatorial scan** finds every **crossing** pair-of-pairs `i<k<j<l` (Antczak 2018) вҖ” one pair's opener inside the other while its closer lies outside. Two exhaustive negatives: **nested** `i<k<l<j` (one pair fully inside) and **disjoint** `j<k` (side-by-side). Each crossing pair-of-pairs = one pseudoknot (binary relation); вүҘ2 pairs required, endpoints normalized min-max to open<close, deterministic. Oracles `([)]`=(0,2)+(1,3)вҶ’one, nested (0,5)+(1,4)вҶ’none, disjoint (0,2)+(3,5)вҶ’none. The **detection/analysis facet** вҖ” genuinely distinct from the energy-driven [[rna-pseudoknot-prediction]] predictor (input = pair set vs sequence, machinery = combinatorial scan vs Turner-NN energy DP, cost = O(nВІ) vs O(nвҒҙ)) вҖ” and the crossing primitive that predictor's validity invariant leans on. Operates on the pairs the [[rna-dot-bracket-notation]] parser emits; complements the nested-only [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding]] / [[rna-partition-function-mccaskill]]. One scope note: pseudoknot-**order** assignment (Antczak DBL layering / Smit 2008 removal) Not Implemented. Sources Antczak 2018 + Smit & Knight 2008 + biotite + Wikipedia, no contradictions. Record [[rna-pseudoknot-001-evidence]].
- [[rna-stem-loop-enumeration]] вҖ” RNA secondary-structure family **enumeration layer** (RNA-STEMLOOP-001, `RnaSecondaryStructure`): **scan a sequence for every stem-loop (hairpin)** it can form under size constraints вҖ” `FindStemLoops(sequence, minStem, minLoop, maxLoop, allowWobble)` / `FindHairpins`, extending an antiparallel WC/wobble stem outward around each candidate loop, **O(nВІВ·L)**. The general, sequence-agnostic hairpin *finder* вҖ” distinct from the single-optimal-fold [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding|MFE folder]] (O(nВі) DP), the hairpin *energy* unit [[rna-hairpin-001-evidence]], and the miRNA-specific [[pre-mirna-hairpin-detection]] precursor detector. Loop **вүҘ3 nt** (steric floor, shared with the MFE/Turner units), optimal **4-8 nt**. **Tetraloops** вҖ” GNRA / UNCG / CUUG, UUCG the most stable, UUCG+GNRA ~70% of 16S-rRNA tetraloops, ~3.0 kcal/mol bonus via [[rna-free-energy-turner-model|Turner 2004]]. `FindPseudoknots` shares the `i<k<j<l` crossing primitive with [[rna-pseudoknot-detection]]. Builds on [[rna-base-pairing]], emits [[rna-dot-bracket-notation]]. Invariants non-overlap / вүӨ1 pair per base / contiguous loop / antiparallel stem; limitations no PK-from-sequence, simplified energy, hairpin loops only, single structure. Record [[rna-stemloop-001-evidence]].
- [[rna-secondary-structure-prediction]] вҖ” RNA secondary-structure family **top-level prediction umbrella** (RNA-STRUCT-001, `RnaSecondaryStructure`): predict a structure from a sequence by a **Nussinov base-pair-maximizing** DP вҖ” `Predict` / `PredictWithConstraints` (forced pairs, Mathews 2004) / `ToDotBracket` / `FromDotBracket`. Nussinov & Jacobson 1980 O(nВі)/O(nВІ) maximizes the **(weighted) base-pair count** (WC вҲ’2.0 / wobble вҲ’1.0), signalling **relative stability, not physical energy units** вҖ” the **`alternative_to`** the physical Turner-kcal/mol [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding|MFE folder]] (RNA-MFE-001), same problem / different objective. A **distinct sibling** test unit, **not an alias** of RNA-MFE-001: both share the `RnaSecondaryStructure` Zuker MFE machinery (this unit's D5 added `CalculateMfeStructure`/`PredictStructureMfe`). Builds on [[rna-base-pairing]], converts to/from [[rna-dot-bracket-notation]], consumes [[rna-free-energy-turner-model]] stem-loop terms, shares the `i<k<j<l` crossing test with [[rna-pseudoknot-detection]] (detects, never predicts, pseudoknots). Oracles `GGGGAAAACCCC`вҶ’`((((....))))`, poly-AвҶ’MFE 0; min loop 3 nt (steric), single-sequence only, int21/int22 lookup tables blocked. Record [[rna-struct-001-evidence]].
- [[clinical-actionability-oncokb-levels]] вҖ” Oncology family anchor (first ONCO-* unit, ONCO-ACTION-001): **clinical actionability assessment** by the OncoKB Therapeutic Levels of Evidence (Chakravarty 2017). A **pure ranking** вҖ” given a variant's caller-supplied leveled drug associations, return the **maximum** level under the fixed combined order `R1 > 1 > 2 > 3A > 3B > 4 > R2` (sensitivity axis `1 > 2 > 3A > 3B > 4`, resistance axis `R1 > R2`), the two axes reported separately (a variant may carry both); no leveled association вҶ’ **NotActionable**. Seven tiers: 1 (FDA in-indication) / 2 (NCCN in-indication) / 3A (clinical evidence in-indication) / 3B (another indication) / 4 (biological evidence) / R1 (standard resistance) / R2 (investigational resistance); 1/2/R1 = standard vs 3A/3B/4/R2 = investigational (SOP v3, consistent with AMP/ASCO/CAP Li 2017). **Knowledgebase is a caller input** вҖ” the library ranks, it does not embed/annotate the OncoKB DB; NotActionable-name is the library's; not for clinical use; record [[onco-action-001-evidence]].
- [[cancer-variant-tier-classification-amp-asco-cap]] вҖ” Oncology family, second ONCO-* unit (ONCO-ANNOT-001): **cancer variant tier classification** by the **AMP/ASCO/CAP 2017 four-tier** consensus (Li MM et al. 2017). A **pure decision rule** over caller-supplied evidence level (AвҖ“D) + population MAF + cancer-association flag вҶ’ **Tier I** (strong, Level A/B) / **II** (potential, Level C/D) / **III** (unknown, no level + rare + cancer assoc) / **IV** (benign, no level + MAF вүҘ 1% **or** no assoc). Population frequency is the **IIIвҶ”IV discriminator**; **evidence level dominates frequency** (a significant biomarker stays Tier I at high MAF). 1% (0.01) is the guideline **primary benign cutoff**, inclusive (MAF 0.01 вҶ’ Tier IV). `AnnotateCancerVariants` = one annotation per variant in input order; `GetCOSMICAnnotation` = null-on-miss lookup against a **caller-supplied** COSMIC catalog (external DB, not embedded). Distinct from but **consistent with** the sibling OncoKB level-ranking [[clinical-actionability-oncokb-levels]]; not for clinical use; record [[onco-annot-001-evidence]].
- [[sequencing-artifact-detection]] вҖ” Oncology family, third ONCO-* unit (ONCO-ARTIFACT-001): **sequencing artifact detection** (`FilterArtifacts`) вҖ” the **QC** sibling that removes false-positive somatic calls from DNA damage / mapping bias **before** clinical interpretation (distinct from the two clinical-significance ONCO units). Three disjoint signals: **substitution class** (OxoG oxidation G>T/C>A per Chen 2017 vs FFPE cytosine-deamination C>T/G>A per Do & Dobrovic 2015; else not-an-artifact), the **GIV** read-pair imbalance ratio (`GIV_G_T = count(G>T in R1)/count(G>T in R2)`, neutral 1 / damaged > 1.5, Chen 2017 + Damage-estimator), and **FisherStrand** FS = вҲ’10В·log10(two-sided Fisher-exact p) on the `[ref_fwd,ref_rev,alt_fwd,alt_rev]` 2Г—2 table (GATK, FS вүҲ 0 no bias / high = artifact). Result вҠҶ input; **no BAM parser** (per-strand/read-mate evidence supplied on the variant record); GIV thresholds from the Nature Methods summary; not for clinical use; record [[onco-artifact-001-evidence]].
- [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]] вҖ” Oncology family, fourth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-ASCAT-001): the **upstream tumor copy-number layer** вҖ” allele-specific integer copy number (nA/nB) from per-locus **logR/BAF** by a joint **purity ПҒ / ploidy ПҲ** grid fit (**ASCAT**, Van Loo 2010: `nA/nB` inversion, minimise length-weighted squared minor-allele distance to non-negative integers, BAF=0.5 down-weighted Г—0.05, GoF = (1вҲ’d/maxdist)В·100, **Оі=1 for sequencing**). Four disjoint stages: (1) ASCAT core (ПҒ,ПҲ) fit; (2) **ASPCF** penalised-least-squares joint segmentation `L=ОЈ(yвҲ’Иі)ВІ+Оі|S|` via O(nВІ) DP (Nilsen 2012) with common change points + BAF mirroring (Ross 2021); (3) **subclonal** two-state mixture `n_obs=fВ·nвӮҒ+(1вҲ’f)В·nвӮӮ` over bracketing integers (Battenberg / Nik-Zainal 2012); (4) **multiplicity/CCF** VAF inversion `VAF=(mВ·CCFВ·p)/(cВ·p+2(1вҲ’p))`, clamp m to [1,major-CN] (McGranahan 2016 / PICTograph / DeCiFering). Planted-truth tests invert the forward model (ПҒвӮҖ=0.80, ПҲвӮҖвҲҲ{2,3}). The allele-specific/clonal counterpart to the total-CN [[aneuploidy-detection]]; substrate beneath the clinical-interpretation ONCO siblings; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-ascat-001-evidence]].
- [[cancer-cell-fraction-clonal-clustering]] вҖ” Oncology family, fifth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-CCF-001): the **downstream clonal-structure layer** вҖ” estimate each mutation's **cancer cell fraction** `CCF = fВ·(ПҒВ·N_T+2(1вҲ’ПҒ))/(ПҒВ·m)` (`EstimateCCF`; McGranahan 2016 / PICTograph / Tarabichi 2021, corroborated three ways; m вҲҲ [1,tumor CN], ПҒ вҲҲ (0,1]) with a reported-value **[0,1] cap** that exposes the uncapped raw (the raw formula can exceed 1 вҖ” CNAqc 1.06 noise case), then **`ClusterCCFValues`** deconvolutes the CCF vector into clones/subclones by a **deterministic 1D Lloyd k-means** (Lloyd 1982, quantile seeding, no RNG) with **highest-centroid = clonal** (Tarabichi 2021). Consumes the purity ПҒ / copy number N_T / multiplicity m from the upstream [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]] (whose В§4 carries the same CCF closed form); two source-consistent assumptions ([0,1] cap; Lloyd k-means as the concrete 1D method); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-ccf-001-evidence]].
- [[clonal-hematopoiesis-cfdna-filtering]] вҖ” Oncology family, sixth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-CHIP-001): the **pre-interpretation biological-origin filter** for liquid biopsy вҖ” removes **clonal-hematopoiesis (CHIP)** false positives, the dominant cfDNA confounder (Razavi 2019: 81.6% controls / 53.2% cancer). `IdentifyCHIPVariants` flags a driver-gene variant ({DNMT3A,TET2,ASXL1,TP53,JAK2,SF3B1,SRSF2,PPM1D}, top-3 DNMT3A/TET2/ASXL1) at **VAF вүҘ 0.02** (Steensma 2015 / Genovese 2014); `FilterCHIP` removes CH calls by **matched-WBC subtraction** (present in matched WBC вҮ’ blood-derived, the definitive origin test, Razavi 2019) plus a **conservative labelled gene+VAF heuristic fallback** (over-removes; strict mode = empty gene panel); `CallVariantOrigin` = the strict **Bolton 2020** rule (WBC VAF вүҘ 2% AND вүҘ 10 reads AND вүҘ ПҶГ— tumour VAF, ПҶ=2.0 / 1.5 lymph node). The **biological-origin sibling** of the technical-artifact QC filter [[sequencing-artifact-detection]], upstream of the clinical-interpretation and clonal-structure ONCO units; two source-consistent assumptions (canonical default gene set, вүҘ1-alt-read WBC presence test); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-chip-001-evidence]].
- [[clonal-subclonal-classification-ccf-posterior]] вҖ” Oncology family, seventh ONCO-* unit (ONCO-CLONAL-001): the **probabilistic clonal-structure classifier** вҖ” per-mutation **Bayesian CCF posterior** `P(c) вҲқ Binom(a|N,f(c))` (uniform prior, 100-point grid `cвҲҲ[0.01,1]`) with expected allele fraction `f(c) = ОұMc/(2(1вҲ’Оұ)+Оұq)` (Landau 2013 ABSOLUTE-style; multiplicity M generalisation, Satas 2021 DeCiFering Eq. 1), classified **clonal iff `P(CCF>0.95) > 0.5`** (two distinct thresholds: 0.95 CCF cut, 0.5 posterior-mass cut) via `ClassifyClonality(variants, purity)`, plus the point-estimate `IdentifyClonalMutations` (strict CCF > 0.95, boundary excluded вҶ’ indices {0,2,4}). The **`alternative_to`** the point-estimate + Lloyd-k-means [[cancer-cell-fraction-clonal-clustering]] вҖ” same clonal/subclonal question, but classifies each mutation on its own read-count uncertainty without clustering; consumes purity Оұ / local copy number q / multiplicity M from the upstream [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]]; one API-shape assumption (per-variant local copy number q over a genome-wide ploidy scalar); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-clonal-001-evidence]].
- [[copy-number-alteration-classification]] вҖ” Oncology family, eighth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-CNA-001): the **total-copy-number classification layer** вҖ” a single **log2 copy ratio** вҶ’ absolute integer CN `n = 2В·2^log2` (CNVkit `_log2_ratio_to_absolute_pure`, diploid ref_copies=2) вҶ’ discrete **CNA state** via CNVkit's `absolute_threshold` hard-threshold caller (default `вҲ’1.1/вҲ’0.25/0.2/0.7` вҶ’ DeepDeletion/Loss/Neutral/Gain/Amplification; CN = index of the **first** threshold with `log2 <= thresh`, **boundary-inclusive вҶ’ lower bin**; above the last вҶ’ `ceil(2В·2^log2)` open-ended Amplification; NaN вҶ’ neutral CN 2), corroborated by **GISTIC2** (Mermel 2011: Вұ0.1 noise band subsumed by the neutral bin + +0.848/вҲ’0.737 high-amplitude cutoffs). The **total-CN** counterpart to the allele-specific [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]] and the per-segment oncology-state sibling of the whole-chromosome [[aneuploidy-detection]] (both share the `n = 2В·2^log2` conversion); distinct from SV-CNV-001's `round`-based integer CN (no state classification). One diploid-ploidy=2 assumption; threshold-variant note (docs germline `вҲ’0.4/0.3` vs code tumor `вҲ’0.25/0.2`); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-cna-001-evidence]].
- [[focal-amplification-detection]] вҖ” Oncology family, ninth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-CNA-002): the **focal-amplification layer** вҖ” a two-part predicate `DetectFocalAmplifications` keeps segments both **amplified** (log2 gain > GISTIC2 `t_amp` 0.1) **and** **focal** (SegLen / ArmLength < `broad_len_cutoff` 0.98 вҖ” Mermel 2011's length-based, not amplitude-based, focal-vs-arm-level split; strict `< 0.98`, exactly 0.98 вҶ’ arm-level), then `IdentifyAmplifiedOncogenes` maps each focal amplification's arm prefix to a built-in oncogene panel (17qвҶ’ERBB2 В· 8qвҶ’MYC В· 7pвҶ’EGFR В· 11qвҶ’CCND1 В· 12qвҶ’MDM2 **and** CDK4, NCBI Gene cytobands). Orthogonal to the log2вҶ’5-state [[copy-number-alteration-classification]] (ONCO-CNA-001) вҖ” a **length** question, not an amplitude bin вҖ” sharing only the GISTIC2 `t_amp`=0.1 amplitude gate. Sources GISTIC2 Mermel 2011 + GISTIC2 docs (`broad_len_cutoff`/`t_amp`) + CNVkit (single-copy gain log2 0.585 > 0.1) + NCBI Gene. Worked oracles A 17q 0.50вҶ’ERBB2 / B 8q 0.99 arm-level / C 7p log2 0.05 not-amplified / D 11q 0.98 boundary. Two assumptions (amplitude+length fusion; caller-supplied arm label + length, no cytoband table); deletions out of scope (ONCO-CNA-003); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-cna-002-evidence]].
- [[homozygous-deletion-detection]] вҖ” Oncology family, tenth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-CNA-003): the **deep-deletion layer**, the **deletion mirror of ONCO-CNA-002** вҖ” filter segments whose classified integer copy number is **exactly 0** (a homozygous / deep deletion: cBioPortal `вҲ’2` "Deep Deletion", Cheng et al. 2017 "zero copies of both alleles" / two hits; **reuses** [[copy-number-alteration-classification]]'s CN-0 = `DeepDeletion` call, **no new threshold**), then `IdentifyDeletedTumorSuppressors` maps each arm prefix to a built-in tumour-suppressor panel (17pвҶ’TP53 В· 13qвҶ’RB1 **and** BRCA2 В· 9pвҶ’CDKN2A В· 10qвҶ’PTEN В· 17qвҶ’BRCA1, NCBI Gene cytobands). A single-copy loss (`вҲ’1`, heterozygous, CN вүҘ 1) is NOT a homozygous deletion. The loss-side counterpart of the amplification unit [[focal-amplification-detection]] (`IdentifyDeletedTumorSuppressors` mirrors `IdentifyAmplifiedOncogenes`) and a consumer of [[copy-number-alteration-classification]]'s CN-0 state. Two assumptions (CN-0 reuse, caller-fixed panel); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-cna-003-evidence]].
- [[ctdna-detection-and-tumor-fraction]] вҖ” Oncology family, eleventh ONCO-* unit (ONCO-CTDNA-001): the liquid-biopsy **quantification / limit-of-detection** layer for **circulating tumor DNA (ctDNA)** вҖ” the Poisson detection probability `DetectionProbability` **p = 1 вҲ’ e^(вҲ’nВ·dВ·k)** (n genome equivalents, d mutant allele fraction, k reporters; Patent US 11,085,084 restating Avanzini 2020, corroborated by Pessoa 2023's О» = nВ·d = 15) with a detectability test (caller threshold default 0.95 **and** О» = nВ·dВ·k вүҘ 1; only p is non-assumption), **`CalculateTumorFraction` = 2 Г— mean clonal-heterozygous VAF** (copy-neutral diploid, CNAqc/Antonello 2024 v = ПҖ/2), `CalculateMeanVaf` = mean altReads/totalReads across reporters (Newman 2014 CAPP-Seq across-reporter fraction, detection 0.025%вҖ“10%), and a genome-equivalents helper (3.3 pg/haploid, Devonshire 2014 вҮ’ вүҲ303 GE/ng, Alcaide 2020). The **quantification counterpart** on the same cfDNA input as the biological-origin filter [[clonal-hematopoiesis-cfdna-filtering]] (measures signal vs filters it), sharing the diploid-heterozygous VAF inversion with [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]] / [[cancer-cell-fraction-clonal-clustering]]; underpins MRD monitoring; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-ctdna-001-evidence]].
- [[driver-gene-classification-20-20-rule]] вҖ” Oncology family, twelfth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-DRIVER-001): the **gene-level** driver classifier вҖ” the Vogelstein 2013 **20/20 rule** classifying a cancer gene **Oncogene** (> 20% missense at **recurrent** positions, вүҘ 2Г— = activating), **TumorSuppressor** (> 20% **truncating / inactivating** вҖ” nonsense / frameshift / splice donor-acceptor / stop gain-loss = loss of function), or **Ambiguous** (neither criterion, or exact dual-pass tie), via `IdentifyDriverMutations` (driver вҠҶ somatic) + `MatchCancerHotspots` (caller-supplied (gene, position) hotspot set) + `ScoreDriverPotential` (= max of the two criterion fractions in [0,1]; CADD/SIFT/PolyPhen are caller-supplied, not implemented). Oracles: IDH1 10 missense@codon 132 вҶ’ recurrent-missense 1.00 вҶ’ Oncogene; dispersed 8/10 truncating вҶ’ 0.80 вҶ’ TumorSuppressor; truncating exactly 0.20 вҶ’ NOT TSG (strict `>`). A **heuristic, not a statistical test** (passenger truncations / low-recurrence drivers mislead it; 20/20+ / MutSigCV successors out of scope), **orthogonal** to the variant-level clinical classifiers [[cancer-variant-tier-classification-amp-asco-cap]] and [[clinical-actionability-oncokb-levels]]. Three assumptions (strict `> 0.20`, dual-pass tie-break by larger fraction with Ambiguous on tie, ScoreDriverPotential proxy); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-driver-001-evidence]].
- [[expression-outlier-zscore-signature-score]] вҖ” Oncology family, thirteenth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-EXPR-001), and the wiki's **first expression/transcriptome method**: the per-gene **outlier z-score** `z = (r вҲ’ Ој)/Пғ` against a caller-supplied **reference (base) population** (cBioPortal's diploid or all-samples convention) with **Пғ = sample SD, divisor (n вҲ’ 1)** (settled by `NormalizeExpressionLevels.java`), classified over/under-expressed under the **strict Вұ2** default threshold (exactly Вұ2 is NOT an outlier), plus the **combined-z signature/pathway activity** `a = (ОЈбөў zбөў)/вҲҡk` (Lee et al. 2008, the GSVA `zscore` method). Zero-SD reference **throws** (reference-code `fatalError`, a behavioural deviation from the prose "z вҶҗ NA" spec вҖ” the two cBioPortal sources disagree); reference `{2,2,4,6,6}` вҶ’ Пғ=2 so x=10вҶ’3.0 over / x=8вҶ’2.0 boundary-not-outlier / x=4вҶ’0.0 / x=вҲ’1вҶ’вҲ’2.5 under, signature `{3,1,вҲ’1,1}`вҶ’2.0 & single-gene `{2.5}`вҶ’2.5 oracles. **Orthogonal** to the copy-number / clonal-structure ONCO units ([[copy-number-alteration-classification]], [[cancer-cell-fraction-clonal-clustering]]) вҖ” the diploid reference option touches copy number only as an input filter. Two scope assumptions (caller-supplied cohort + signature; inputs pre-normalized) + one behavioural deviation (throw not NA); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-expr-001-evidence]].
- [[gene-fusion-detection-read-evidence]] вҖ” Oncology family, fourteenth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-FUSION-001), and the wiki's **first gene-fusion / read-evidence structural-rearrangement method**: the STAR-Fusion / Arriba **split-read + discordant-pair + minimum-support** candidate-fusion caller (BCR-ABL1 / EML4-ALK / TMPRSS2-ERG). **DETECTED** iff (junction вүҘ `MIN_JUNCTION_READS`=1 AND total вүҘ `MIN_SUM_FRAGS`=2) OR (zero junction AND discordant вүҘ `MIN_SPANNING_FRAGS_ONLY`=5), where **total support = split_reads1 + split_reads2 + discordant_mates** (Arriba) and the **gene5p вү  gene3p** distinct-gene invariant rejects self-fusions; results ordered by descending support (STAR-Fusion scores by "abundance of fusion-supporting reads"). Plus a standalone **exon-phase in-frame** check `(5' coding bases вҲ’ 3' start phase) mod 3 == 0` (Genomics England / Wikipedia Reading-frame). Oracles: EML4-ALK(3,2,4)/TMPRSS2-ERG(1,0,1)/CD74-ROS1(0,0,5) DETECTED, NCOA4-RET(0,0,4) span<5 / KIF5B-RET(1,0,0) sum<2 / ALK-ALK same-gene REJECTED, frame 300/0вҶ’in 301/0вҶ’out 301/1вҶ’in. Consumes **already-grouped candidate breakpoint counts** (Arriba schema, not raw BAM вҖ” chimeric-read extraction is a separate `FindChimericReads`) and does **not** scan for a premature stop before the junction (Arriba `stop-codon` value, ONCO-FUSION-003 scope). **Orthogonal** to the copy-number/clonal and clinical-interpretation ONCO units, distinct from the gene-order [[genome-rearrangement-breakpoint-distance]]. Two scope assumptions; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-fusion-001-evidence]].
- [[gene-fusion-nomenclature-known-fusion-lookup]] вҖ” Oncology family, fifteenth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-FUSION-002), the wiki's fusion **annotation/naming** method: the **HGNC gene-fusion designation** `GetFusionAnnotation(5p,3p) = "5p::3p"` (Bruford et al. 2021 вҖ” `::` double-colon separator, **5вҖІ-partner-first** directional order irrespective of chromosomal location, HGNC approved symbols, read-throughs keep the hyphen `INS-IGF2`) plus the **directional known-fusion match** `MatchKnownFusions` against a **caller-supplied** set keyed by `5вҖІ::3вҖІ`, case-insensitive. A **Framework** algorithm вҖ” format/keying source-backed (Bruford 2021 + consortium extension letter), set contents caller-supplied (no bundled Mitelman/COSMIC/ChimerDB). `BCR::ABL1` worked example; `A::B вү  B::A` reciprocal-direction and hyphen вү  `::` corner cases; null/empty rejected. The **naming layer downstream** of the read-evidence caller [[gene-fusion-detection-read-evidence]] (annotation round-trips through a `DetectFusions` `FusionCall`), distinct from the ONCO-FUSION-003 premature-stop scope; orthogonal to the copy-number/clonal and clinical-interpretation ONCO units. Two assumptions (caller-supplied set, case-insensitivity); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-fusion-002-evidence]].
- [[fusion-breakpoint-frame-and-protein-prediction]] вҖ” Oncology family, sixteenth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-FUSION-003), the **protein-consequence** third member of the fusion trio: given a fusion breakpoint it computes the **four-state** `BreakpointFrameStatus` (`InFrame`/`OutOfFrame`/`StopCodon`/`NotPredicted`) and reconstructs the **fusion protein**. Follows **Arriba's two-way** native-frame model (Uhrig 2021 `reading_frame`/`site` columns) вҖ” the in/out call is whether the 3вҖІ gene is read in its NATIVE frame via the exon-phase rule `(5' coding bases вҲ’ 3' start phase) mod 3 == 0` (reused from [[gene-fusion-detection-read-evidence]] ONCO-FUSION-001) вҖ” deliberately **not** AGFusion's three-way class (`in-frame (with mutation)`, contiguous ORF multiple-of-3 but 3вҖІ frameshifted, maps to **`OutOfFrame`**). Gated by breakpoint-site classification: a breakpoint in UTR/intron/non-coding-exon/intergenic вҶ’ `NotPredicted`. `PredictFusionProtein` follows AGFusion `model.py` exactly: 5вҖІ CDS prefix + 3вҖІ CDS suffix вҶ’ concatenate вҶ’ translate (transl_table=1) вҶ’ **truncate at first stop** (out-of-frame trims to whole codons first). Oracles `ATGAAA|GATGGT`вҶ’`MKDG`, `ATGAAA|GATTAAGGT`вҶ’`MKD` (in-frame premature stop), `ATGA|AAGGT` phase-0вҶ’`OutOfFrame` yet clean `MKG` (the Arriba-vs-AGFusion divergence point) / phase-1вҶ’in-frame, `ATGAA|GATGGT`вҶ’trim-to-9 `MKM`. Downstream of ONCO-FUSION-001 (elaborates its binary in-frame check into a full consequence + transcript/peptide reconstruction, the premature-stop scope both siblings deferred here), orthogonal to the naming unit [[gene-fusion-nomenclature-known-fusion-lookup]] and to the copy-number/clonal and clinical-interpretation ONCO units. One API-shape assumption (caller supplies CDS strings + junction offsets, no bundled GTF); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-fusion-003-evidence]].
- [[intratumor-heterogeneity-metrics]] вҖ” Oncology family, seventeenth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-HETERO-001): the **scalar-summary ITH-metric layer** that reduces the reconstructed clonal structure to comparable numbers вҖ” the **MATH score** `100В·1.4826В·median(|VAFвҲ’median VAF|)/median(VAF)` (Mroz & Rocco 2013 / Mroz 2015 / maftools `mathScore.R`, three-way identical; the ratio of the width to the centre of the mutant-allele-fraction distribution, no clustering needed), the **Shannon clonal diversity** `H = вҲ’ОЈ pбөў ln pбөў` (natural log, Liu 2017 / Shannon 1948), the **subclone count** (Liu richness = number of occupied CCF clusters), and the **subclonal fraction** `#(CCF<0.95)/n` (Landau 2013 threshold). MATH oracles 49.42 (odd) / 59.304 (even); Shannon 0 / ln2 / ln4; zero-median-VAFвҶ’throw, MAD=0вҶ’MATH=0. **Depends on** [[cancer-cell-fraction-clonal-clustering]] (subclone count + Shannon pбөў consume its CCF clusters) and reuses the 0.95 clonal threshold of [[clonal-subclonal-classification-ccf-posterior]]; a summary layer, NOT per-mutation reconstruction; shares the Shannon-index math but not the domain with [[alpha-diversity]]. Two source-consistent assumptions (Shannon pбөў = per-cluster mutation proportions; R even-count median); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-hetero-001-evidence]].
- [[hla-nomenclature-and-allele-specific-loh]] вҖ” Oncology family, eighteenth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-HLA-001), the wiki's **first HLA / immuno-oncology antigen-presentation method**: two disjoint pieces sharing the HLA locus вҖ” (1) **HLA allele nomenclature parsing/validation** of the WHO IPD-IMGT/HLA name `HLA-[Gene]*[F1]:[F2][:F3][:F4][suffix]` (Marsh 2010 colon-delimited convention; Field1 type/allele-group / Field2 specific protein / Field3 synonymous / Field4 non-coding; **two-field "four-digit" minimum**, four-field maximum, `HLA-` prefix required, numeric fields, `N/L/S/C/A/Q` expression-suffix set вҖ” `HLA-A*24:02:01:02L` valid, `HLA-A*02`/`A*02:01`/five-fields/`вҖҰX` rejected), and (2) **allele-specific HLA LOH** by the **LOHHLA** rule (McGranahan 2017 *Cell* / `mskcc/lohhla`): per-allele copy number from tumor-vs-germline logR + BAF, call HLA LOH iff min copy number **< 0.5** AND allelic-imbalance paired Student's t-test **p < 0.01** вҖ” both strict `<`, the p-test the explicit "avoid over-calling LOH" guard; oracles (1.8, 0.30, 0.001)вҶ’LOH allele 2 / (1.60, 0.40, 0.05)вҶ’no (pвүҘ0.01) / (1.50, 0.50, 0.001)вҶ’no (0.5 not <0.5) / (1.70, 0.40, 0.01)вҶ’no (0.01 not <0.01); the **HLA-locus specialization** of the genome-wide allele-specific copy-number / LOH derivation [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]] (same logR + BAF allelic-contrast idea restricted to the HLA genes), a mechanism of immune escape via lost neoantigen presentation; one assumption (both alleles <0.5 вҶ’ distinct `HomozygousLoss` label, thresholds unchanged); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-hla-001-evidence]].
- [[homologous-recombination-deficiency-score]] вҖ” Oncology family, nineteenth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-HRD-001): the **HRD composite genomic-scar score** `HRD = LOH + TAI + LST`, an **unweighted sum** of three large-scale copy-number scar counts with the **HRD-high cutoff вүҘ 42** inclusive (Telli 2016 + Stewart 2022, independently corroborated). All three components **derived per segment** from the [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]] major/minor CN substrate in `DetectHRD(segments)`: **HRD-LOH** = LOH regions > 15 Mb & < whole chromosome, excluding whole-chr-LOH chromosomes (Abkevich 2012 / oncoscanR / scarHRD `calc.hrd.R`, no centromere table needed); **TAI** = imbalanced (major вү  minor CN) segments reaching a sub-telomere but not crossing the centromere (Birkbak 2012 / scarHRD `calc.ai_new.R`, sub-1 Mb dropped, single-segment whole-chr imbalance excluded); **LST** = adjacent вүҘ 10 Mb same-arm regions separated by < 3 Mb after iterative 3 Mb smoothing (Popova 2012 / scarHRD `calc.lst.R`, autosomes only). TAI + LST need the per-chromosome centromere `[start,end]` **acen** table embedded for GRCh38/GRCh37 (UCSC cytoBand cross-verified vs NCBI GRC вҖ” resolving the prior "centromere table unretrievable" blocker). Oracles (14,14,14)вҶ’42 HRD-high / (14,13,14)вҶ’41 negative / (0,0,0)вҶ’0. The genomic-scar aggregation layer above [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]], distinct from the total-CN [[aneuploidy-detection]]; one even-ploidy AI-path assumption; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-hrd-001-evidence]].
- [[immune-infiltration-deconvolution]] вҖ” Oncology family, twentieth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-IMMUNE-001), the wiki's **second expression/transcriptome method**: **immune infiltration estimation** вҖ” quantifies the tumor immune microenvironment two ways. (1) **Cell-type deconvolution** of the linear mixture `m = SВ·f` (ОЈf=1, fвүҘ0): CIBERSORT **ОҪ-SVR** `DeconvoluteImmuneCellsNuSvr` (Newman 2015 / SchГ¶lkopf 2000 linear-kernel ОҪ-SVR вҖ” z-standardize m + signature columns, sweep ОҪвҲҲ{0.25,0.5,0.75} by **lowest RMSE**, zero-clip negatives + normalize to ОЈ=1; cross-validated by planted-truth `m=SВ·f` recovery + scikit-learn `NuSVR`/libsvm match) with the NNLS/LLSR baseline `DeconvoluteImmuneCells` (Abbas 2009) retained. (2) **ESTIMATE** ssGSEA immune/stromal enrichment `EstimateInfiltration` (**simplified** = rank-weighted mean of signature genes, not full KS running-sum) + opt-in **tumor purity** `EstimateTumorPurity` = `cos(0.6049872018 + 0.0001467884В·ESTIMATE)` (verbatim, confirmed 3 sources + tidyestimate R; **Affymetrix-only** calibration, negative cosine вҶ’ **NaN**, monotone-decreasing). MCP-counter geometric-mean marker abundance noted.
