Signature matrices: **LM22** (547 genes Г— 22 cell types) **caller-supplied** вҖ” Stanford licence forbids redistribution/modification/commercial use, no exact-CIBERSORT parity claim, `LoadSignatureMatrix` LM22-format loader only; **ABIS-Seq** (Monaco 2019, CC BY 4.0, 1296 genes Г— 17 types) **bundled** as embedded resource via `LoadBundledAbisSignatureMatrix` so deconvolution works out-of-the-box (not an LM22 substitute); synthetic 5-marker `DefaultSignatureMatrix` for tests. Oracles: planted {CD8 0.60,B_naive 0.30,Mono 0.10}вҶ’{0.5971,0.2989,0.1040} corr 0.99997; sklearn cross-check ОҪ=0.75 {A 0.5085,B 0.1795,C 0.3120}; ABIS {NK 0.60,MonoC 0.40}вҶ’{вүҲ0.650,вүҲ0.350} corr 0.996 (tol 0.06) & pure MonoC 1.0 exactly; ABIS ref `CD8A`/T CD8 Mem=1060.1507652944399. Corner cases: collinear cell types (resting/activated NK) recover support but looser proportions; missing/non-overlapping genes вҶ’ unreliable/zero; non-hematopoietic content in residual; ESTIMATE solid-tumors-only. Antigen-agnostic quantitative sibling of the immuno-oncology [[hla-nomenclature-and-allele-specific-loh]], shares the ssGSEA signature-scoring layer with [[expression-outlier-zscore-signature-score]]; two scope assumptions (LM22 caller-supplied, simplified ssGSEA) + Affymetrix purity domain, no contradictions; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-immune-001-evidence]].
- [[loss-of-heterozygosity-detection]] вҖ” Oncology family, twenty-first ONCO-* unit (ONCO-LOH-001): the standalone genome-wide **LOH caller** вҖ” `DetectLOH` counts **HRD-LOH** regions (minor CN 0 **and** major CN вү  0 = allelic loss not homozygous deletion; length **strictly > 15 Mb**, length = end вҲ’ start; excluding any **whole-chromosome** global-LOH chromosome via `chrDel`) and `CalculateLOHFraction` returns the length-weighted per-chromosome LOH fraction вҲҲ [0,1]. Abkevich 2012 (intermediate-size LOH вҶ” BRCA1/2 deficiency) + scarHRD `calc.hrd.R`/`scar_score.R` (exact R criterion + 15 Mb cut-off + `chrDel`; major CN capped to 1 so LOH state, not absolute CN, drives merging) + oncoscanR `score_loh` (independent corroboration; adjacent/overlapping LOH merged вүӨ 1 bp first). Synthetic 7-segment dataset вҶ’ score **1** (only the 20 Mb chr1 segment; exactly-15 Mb / het-retained / homozygous-deletion / whole-chr-LOH all excluded); LOH-fraction 0.333/0.0/1.0. This **is** the LOH term the composite [[homologous-recombination-deficiency-score]] sums with TAI + LST (centromere-free, unlike its siblings), reads its segments off [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]], and is the genome-wide counterpart of the HLA-locus [[hla-nomenclature-and-allele-specific-loh]] (LOHHLA). Two assumptions (segment input shape; length-weighted LOH-fraction is a definitional/API choice); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-loh-001-evidence]].
- [[mhc-peptide-binding-prediction]] вҖ” Oncology family, twenty-second ONCO-* unit (ONCO-MHC-001): the wiki's first **MHC / peptide-presentation prediction** method вҖ” the affinity gate of neoantigen candidate scoring, three layers over one `Strong`/`Weak`/`NonBinder` output. (1) **Classification**: IC50 tiers `< 50` Strong / `< 500` Weak / `вүҘ 500` NonBinder (Sette 1994 вүҲ 500 nM CTL threshold + IEDB) and NetMHCpan-4.1 %Rank tiers (class I SB `< 0.5` / WB `< 2`, class II `< 2` / `< 10`, all strict `<`; Reynisson 2020), + peptide-length validity (class I **8вҖ“14**, class II 13вҖ“25). (2) **Matrix prediction**: BIMAS **product rule** (TВҪ = const В· вҲҸ coeffs, 180 coeffs + const, unlisted = 1.0; Parker 1994) and SMM **additive** rule `IC50 = 50000^(1вҲ’score)` (Peters & Sette 2005 / IEDB log50k; 0вҶ’50000, 0.5вҶ’223.6068, 1вҶ’1 nM). (3) Ported **MHCflurry 2.0** pan-allele class-I NN (BLOSUM62 `left_pad_centered_right_pad` 45Г—21 peptide + 37-residue allele pseudosequence 37Г—21, `tanh` Dense `feedforward`/`with-skip-connections`, `to_ic50 = 50000^(1вҲ’x)`, geometric-mean ensemble; matches `mhcflurry` 2.1.5 to < 0.03 %). **Framework/packaging** вҖ” trained matrices caller-supplied (BIMAS CGI defunct / Parker paywalled / IEDB non-commercial) and 80 MB ensemble not embedded (one member for CI + `LoadWeightPack`), explicitly analogized in-file to CIBERSORT LM22 of [[immune-infiltration-deconvolution]]. Downstream of neoantigen generation [[neoantigen-peptide-generation]] (ONCO-NEO-001), presentation-machinery sibling of [[hla-nomenclature-and-allele-specific-loh]] (HLA LOH removes the platform); class I 8вҖ“14 resolved vs NetMHCpan-4.1; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-mhc-001-evidence]].
- [[tumor-informed-mrd-detection]] вҖ” Oncology family, twenty-third ONCO-* unit (ONCO-MRD-001): the liquid-biopsy **MRD calling / statistical-detection** layer that `depends_on` and reuses the Poisson quantification primitive [[ctdna-detection-and-tumor-fraction]] (ONCO-CTDNA-001). Two engines. (1) **Signatera positivity** (`DetectMRD`): tumor-informed workflow вҖ” up to 16 WES-selected clonal somatic SNVs tracked in plasma cfDNA вҖ” **MRD-positive iff вүҘ 2 of the 16 tracked variants are detected** (Reinert 2019 / PMC9265001 Table 1; 0/1вҶ’negative, 2/3вҶ’positive), panel Poisson `p = 1 вҲ’ e^(вҲ’nfm)`, sensitivity scales with panel size (>8 markers at вүӨ0.1% VAF, LoD 0.01% / specificity >99.5%; post-op ctDNA+ вҶ’ HR 7.2 relapse), longitudinal `TrackVariantsOverTime` (per-timepoint + first-positive). (2) **INVAR GLRT** (Wan 2020 + INVAR2 verbatim): per-locus mixture `q = pВ·g + e(1вҲ’p)`, EM ctDNA-fraction, `LR = logL(pМӮ) вҲ’ logL(0)` (pure background вҶ’ pМӮвүҲ0/LRвүҲ0; AF/SNR-weighted, monotone), `IntegratedMutantAlleleFractionV2` background-subtracted depth-weighted, fragment-size-weighted GLRT (`EstimateInvarSignalWithSize`/`FragmentSizeProfile`/`InvarMolecule`; discrete `COUNT/TOTAL` default + opt-in Gaussian-KDE `FromKernelDensity`; flat P1==P0 вҶ’ reduces to no-size), outlier suppression `SuppressOutlierLoci` (repolish binomial + Bonferroni), control-derived background `EstimateLocusBackground`/`PassesBothStrandsFilter`. Distinct from ONCO-CTDNA-001 (multi-variant verdict vs single-reporter probability); one flagged per-variant "detected"=вүҘ1 alt read assumption (tunable); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-mrd-001-evidence]].
- [[microsatellite-instability-detection]] вҖ” Oncology family, twenty-fourth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-MSI-001): the **microsatellite-instability biomarker** вҖ” MSI from unstable-loci fraction + status classification. Two inputs, two classifiers. (1) **Continuous MSI score** = `unstable loci / valid loci` (as %) with **MSI-High cutoff вүҘ 20%** inclusive (MSIsensor2 niu-lab README verbatim; per-site **chi-square** tumor-vs-normal repeat-length test at **FDR 0.05**, score = "% sites with a somatic indel", Niu 2014; tumor-only mode unchanged; the original cohort's **3.5%** separation is dataset-specific, not the production cutoff) вҶ’ classified **binary** MSI-H (вүҘ20%) vs not-High only. (2) **Categorical Bethesda** marker-count over the validated 5-marker panel (BAT-25/BAT-26/D2S123/D5S346/D17S250): **0/5вҶ’MSS В· 1/5вҶ’MSI-L В· вүҘ2/5вҶ’MSI-H** (Boland 1998, cross-checked vs the 2004 revised-Bethesda вүҘ40% / вүҘ20%&<40% fraction form BJC 2014). Key modelling choice: **no MSI-L band is fabricated for the continuous score** вҖ” the three-way MSS/MSI-L/MSI-H scheme applies only to the discrete marker count. Oracles 5/25вҶ’20%вҶ’MSI-H(boundary) В· 4/25вҶ’16%вҶ’not-High В· 0/25вҶ’0%вҶ’MSS-range; corner cases zero-valid-lociвҶ’undefined(throws) В· unstable>valid/negativeвҶ’throws В· MSS-vs-MSI-L 1-marker low-confidence. An independent immunotherapy/mismatch-repair biomarker orthogonal to the copy-number-scar [[homologous-recombination-deficiency-score]], consumed by [[cancer-variant-tier-classification-amp-asco-cap]] / [[clinical-actionability-oncokb-levels]]; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-msi-001-evidence]].
- [[neoantigen-peptide-generation]] вҖ” Oncology family, twenty-fifth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-NEO-001): the **upstream partner** of the affinity gate [[mhc-peptide-binding-prediction]] вҖ” **neoantigen candidate peptide window generation** (`GenerateNeoantigenPeptides`). Given a somatic **missense SNV** at 1-based position `p` in a protein of length `L`, enumerate **every length-`k` window of the mutant protein that spans the mutated residue** (valid 0-based start `s вҲҲ [max(0, pвҲ’1вҲ’k+1), min(pвҲ’1, LвҲ’k)]`, count `= last вҲ’ first + 1`; an interior mutation gives exactly `k` windows per length), each paired with its matched **wild-type (germline)** peptide at the same coordinates + the mutation offset вҖ” the mutant/WT **agretope** on which the differential agretopic index (DAI, Wells 2020 TESLA) is computed. Class I search lengths **8вҖ“11** (pVACtools Hundal 2020; a 21-mer with the substitution centred = ProGeo-neo Li 2020's Вұ10-flank construction contains exactly every overlapping 8вҖ“11-mer; NetMHCpan 8вҖ“14 / 9-mer-dominant Jurtz 2017 motivates enumerating 8вҖ“11 not 9 alone). Oracles: interior **Y5C** on `MKTAYIAKQRSTVWLNDEFGH` вҶ’ 5 windows per k = 8/9/10/11 вҶ’ **20** candidates (each WT = mutant with `C`вҶ’`Y` at the offset); **terminal M1V** k = 9 вҶ’ exactly 1 truncated window `VKTAYIAKQ`/`MKTAYIAKQ` offset 0; corner cases non-coding/synonymous вҶ’ no peptide, length outside 8вҖ“11 not enumerated, short-protein skips that `k`. **Missense-only** (frameshift/indel/fusion neopeptides out of scope, separate translation) and **binding affinity out of scope** (IC50/%Rank scoring caller-supplied via the downstream [[mhc-peptide-binding-prediction]] ONCO-MHC-001 gate, whose resolved class I 8вҖ“14 window propagates to this generator's default); presentation-platform sibling [[hla-nomenclature-and-allele-specific-loh]] (HLA LOH removes the restricted allele). Two source-backed scoping assumptions; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-neo-001-evidence]].
- [[tumor-phylogeny-clonal-tree-reconstruction]] вҖ” Oncology family, twenty-sixth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-PHYLO-001): the **clonal-tree reconstruction** layer вҖ” assemble per-cluster **cancer cell fractions (CCF)** into a rooted **clonal-evolution tree**, deciding parentвҶ’child descent via two per-sample CCF-ordering constraints from **LICHeE** (Popic 2015) and **PICTograph** (Zheng 2022): **lineage precedence** (ancestor CCF вүҘ descendant CCF вҲ’ Оө per sample, + presence pattern `u.CCF=0 вҮ’ v.CCF=0`; LICHeE Eq. 2) and the **sum rule** (children CCF sum вүӨ parent CCF + Оө per node вҖ” the cell-fraction **pigeonhole generalization**; LICHeE Eq. 5 / PICTograph sum condition вҖ” what forces **branching vs nesting**), plus **trunk** (CCF-вүҲ1 root-path clusters = clonal) vs **branch** (subclones) identification. A **constraint-satisfaction / perfect-phylogeny** builder, **not** distance-based Neighbor-Joining / UPGMA. Oracles: linear NormalвҶ’AвҶ’BвҶ’C (1.0/1.0/0.6/0.3, Trunk {A}); two-sample branching AвҶ’{B,C} (B 0.6/0.0, C 0.0/0.7 вҖ” each private, absent in the other's sample, so mutually non-ancestral; sum under A per sample 0.6 & 0.7 вүӨ 1.0); equal 0.6/0.6 siblings forced into a chain NormalвҶ’AвҶ’BвҶ’C by the sum rule (0.6+0.6=1.2 > 1.0). Two reconstructed-tree **invariants** as oracles (ancestor CCF вүҘ descendant per edge; per-node sum rule); emptyвҶ’root-only, single clusterвҶ’trunk. **Downstream of** the CCF clustering [[cancer-cell-fraction-clonal-clustering]] (ONCO-CCF-001, which produces the clusters it orders), the structural counterpart of the per-mutation trunkвҶ”clonal / branchвҶ”subclonal [[clonal-subclonal-classification-ccf-posterior]], and the structure the heterogeneity metrics [[intratumor-heterogeneity-metrics]] summarize. Two source-consistent assumptions (deepest-valid-ancestor deterministic tie-break; default Оө=0 strict inequalities); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-phylo-001-evidence]].
- [[tumor-ploidy-estimation-and-whole-genome-doubling]] вҖ” Oncology family, twenty-seventh ONCO-* unit (ONCO-PLOIDY-001): two **post-hoc genome-state summaries** over already-called allele-specific segments (shared `AlleleSpecificSegment` = Major+Minor CN, not raw logR/BAF): (1) **average ploidy** `EstimatePloidy` = length-weighted mean total CN **ПҲ = ОЈ(CN_iВ·L_i)/ОЈ(L_i)** (Patchwork PMC4053982; n-scale Van Loo 2010, pure diploid вҶ’ 2.0, >2.7n aneuploidy; CN 2/4/3 at 100/100/50 Mb вҶ’ 3.0, genuinely length-weighted not plain segment mean); (2) **whole-genome doubling** `DetectWholeGenomeDoubling` = facets-suite `is_genome_doubled` / Bielski 2018 rule вҖ” WGD iff **autosome-restricted fraction at major CN вүҘ 2 strictly > 0.5** (`mcn = tcn вҲ’ lcn`; major not total CN, so all-1:1 вҶ’ not doubled), denominator = **reference chromosome-size table** (`ReferenceGenome {GRCh38,GRCh37}`, UCSC hg38/hg19 Ensembl-verified, ОЈchr1вҖ“22 = 2,875,001,522 / 2,881,033,286 bp) NOT supplied segments, autosomes only (sex chromosomes excluded); half+1вҶ’true / exactly-halfвҶ’false (strict) / 100 Mb ampвҶ’0.035 false / chrX-onlyвҶ’false oracles, legacy `DetectWholeGenomeDoublingFromSuppliedLength` keeps the supplied-length denominator (60%вҶ’true/50%вҶ’false). **Distinct from** the joint grid fit [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]] (ONCO-ASCAT-001 *fits* ПҒ/ПҲ from raw logR/BAF; this *summarizes* ПҲ post-segmentation), reads the same segment substrate as [[loss-of-heterozygosity-detection]] / [[homologous-recombination-deficiency-score]]. Two assumptions (input shape; resolved reference-genome WGD denominator); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-ploidy-001-evidence]].
- [[tumor-purity-from-mutation-vaf]] вҖ” Oncology family, twenty-eighth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-PURITY-001): a **standalone closed-form tumor-purity estimator** that inverts the **CNAqc expected-VAF generative model** `v = mВ·ПҖВ·c/[2(1вҲ’ПҖ)+ПҖ(n_A+n_B)]` (Antonello 2024) to recover purity ПҖ from a somatic-SNV VAF + local allele-specific copy number: `EstimatePurityFromVAF` = the copy-neutral diploid heterozygous special case **ПҖ = 2В·VAF** (clonal c=1, het m=1, n_tot=2; VAF 0.30вҶ’0.60, band 0.55вҖ“0.65вҶ”VAF 0.275вҖ“0.325, invariant 0вүӨПҖвүӨ1) and `EstimatePurity` = the general inversion `ПҖ = 2v/(mВ·c + 2v вҲ’ vВ·n_tot)` recovering ПҖ=1 on a 2:1 (n_tot=3) segment for both m=1 (v=1/3) and m=2 (v=2/3). The `2(1вҲ’ПҖ)+ПҖВ·n_tot` denominator (normal diploid weighted 1вҲ’ПҖ + tumour) is confirmed by **FACETS** (Shen & Seshan 2016) and inverted the other way by **ABSOLUTE** (Carter 2012). Corner cases: multiplicity ambiguity on amplified segments (two VAF peaks 1/3, 2/3 вҖ” need CN state + m), subclonal c<1 depresses VAF (use **clonal** mutations or underestimate purity), purity <0.1 below detection, no informative variants вҶ’ undefined. **`alternative_to`** the joint logR/BAF grid fit [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]] (ONCO-ASCAT-001 вҖ” same purity scalar, different substrate + method), mutation-VAF counterpart to the ploidy-side [[tumor-ploidy-estimation-and-whole-genome-doubling]], shares the diploid `ПҖ=2В·VAF` inversion with [[ctdna-detection-and-tumor-fraction]]. Two modelling-scope assumptions (copy-neutral-diploid default, median cross-variant aggregation); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-purity-001-evidence]].
- [[sbs96-mutational-signature-catalog]] вҖ” Oncology family, twenty-ninth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-SIG-001): the wiki's first **mutational-signature** method вҖ” the **SBS-96 trinucleotide context catalog**, the classification step that builds the 96-channel single-base-substitution spectrum downstream signature fitting decomposes. A **channel** = a substitution + its centred trinucleotide context: **6** subtypes named by the **pyrimidine** of the mutated WatsonвҖ“Crick pair (`C>A/C>G/C>T/T>A/T>C/T>G`) **Г— 4** 5вҖІ bases **Г— 4** 3вҖІ bases = **96**, labelled `5'[REF>ALT]3'` (COSMIC SBS96 + SigProfilerMatrixGenerator Bergstrom 2019 + Alexandrov 2013, identical 6Г—4Г—4 definition). The defining rule is **pyrimidine-strand folding**: a **purine (A/G) reference** base is reverse-complemented (context via AвҶ”T/CвҶ”G then reverse, plus the substitution) onto the pyrimidine strand before counting; a C/T reference classifies to itself, centre unchanged. Worked fold TGA/GвҶ’T вҶ’ revcomp TCA + G>TвҶ’C>A вҶ’ `T[C>A]A`; oracles A,C,A,AвҶ’A[C>A]A В· G,T,C,AвҶ’G[T>C]A В· A,A,T,AвҶ’T[T>A]T. Catalog **partition** invariants: exactly 96 canonical keys, ОЈ per-channel counts = number of classifiable SBS variants. Corner cases: purine-ref must fold (never counted directly), non-SBS variants (indels/DBS) excluded, non-ACGT context unclassifiable, ref==alt out of scope. **Catalog/classification only** вҖ” the NMF/NNLS signature-exposure fitting against COSMIC reference signatures is a separate downstream concern. A somatic-mutation-spectrum biomarker orthogonal to the copy-number-scar [[homologous-recombination-deficiency-score]] and the mismatch-repair [[microsatellite-instability-detection]]; one cosmetic label-rendering assumption; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-sig-001-evidence]].
- [[mutational-signature-fitting-and-extraction]] вҖ” Oncology family, thirtieth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-SIG-002): the **downstream signature-deconvolution** partner of the catalog [[sbs96-mutational-signature-catalog]] (which it `depends_on`) вҖ” decompose the 96-channel SBS spectrum into **signatures Г— exposures** two ways. **Supervised refit** by **non-negative least squares** `min_x вҖ–SВ·xвҲ’dвҖ–вӮӮВІ, xвүҘ0` (MutationalPatterns/deconstructSigs; Lawson-Hanson active-set вҖ” clamp any would-be-negative coefficient to 0 and refit, S=[[1,1],[0,1]], d=[0,1]вҶ’x=[0,0.5]; reconstruction `SВ·x`, **cosine вүҘ 0.95** quality gate, raw counts + proportion `x/ОЈx` exposures). **Unsupervised de-novo extraction** by **NMF** `V вүҲ WH` (Lee & Seung multiplicative updates, **Frobenius** default + **KL/Poisson** enhancement, both **monotonically non-increasing**; Alexandrov blind-source-separation W=signatures/H=exposures; COSMIC **L1-normalize** each W column to 1). Shared **cosine similarity** `AВ·B/(вҖ–AвҖ–вҖ–BвҖ–)вҲҲ[0,1]` (identicalвҶ’1, orthogonalвҶ’0, [1,1]/[1,0]вҶ’1/вҲҡ2, scale-invariant, **zero-normвҶ’0.0** by convention). **Rank selection** = Brunet-2004 **cophenetic correlation** (consensus of argmax-over-H connectivity matrices; rank-1 trivially 1.0) + SigProfiler **silhouette stability**; **reference matching** = greedy best-cosine to COSMIC. Sharp edges: NMF **non-convex вҶ’ local minimum** (planted-truth + fixed-seed recovery only), **permutation/scale ambiguity**, Оө-guarded denominators. The NNLS refit and NMF extraction are `alternative_to` each other over the same `V вүҲ WH` model; the fitted exposure profile feeds the clinical-interpretation ONCO units, orthogonal to [[homologous-recombination-deficiency-score]] / [[microsatellite-instability-detection]]; five modelling assumptions (Frobenius, seeded init, proportions, zero-cosine, consensus/silhouette/greedy matching); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-sig-002-evidence]].
- [[signature-exposure-bootstrap-confidence-intervals]] вҖ” Oncology family, thirty-first ONCO-* unit (ONCO-SIG-003): the **signature-exposure uncertainty** layer over the NNLS refit [[mutational-signature-fitting-and-extraction]] (which it `depends_on`) вҖ” a **resample вҶ’ refit вҶ’ percentile** loop that turns the point-estimate exposure vector into a **per-signature confidence interval**. Resample the 96-channel catalog `R` times (default 1000; sigminer вүҘ100), re-run the ONCO-SIG-002 **NNLS** `FitSignatures` per replicate, and report the **[2.5%, 97.5%] percentiles** (Efron 1979 percentile CI) read off the finite bootstrap sample by the **type-7** quantile (Hyndman & Fan 1996, `h=pВ·(nвҲ’1)`, R/NumPy default). **Two resampling schemes** differing only by whether total burden N is fixed: **multinomial** (sigminer `sample(...,prob=catalog/ОЈ)` = fixed-N multinomial(N,p), the byte-for-byte **default**) vs **Poisson** (Senkin 2021 MSA variant, each channel `Poisson(observedвӮ–)`, N unfixed, justified by the PoissonвҶ”multinomial conditional equivalence). The **discriminating** corner case is a single non-zero channel: multinomial **collapses deterministically** (width 0, point=mean=lower=upper) while **Poisson(О»>0) fluctuates** (variance=mean вҶ’ positive width вҖ” the reason the Poisson variant was added); plus N=0вҶ’[0,0] and R=1вҶ’lower=upper=mean. Invariants LowerвүӨMeanвүӨUpper, exposures вүҘ0 (NNLS), fixed-seed determinism; type-7 oracles [0,1,2,3,4]вҶ’0.1/2.0/3.9 and [2,4,6,8]вҶ’2.15/5.0/7.85. The uncertainty layer two steps above the [[sbs96-mutational-signature-catalog]] spectrum; two source-aligned assumptions (type-7 interpolation, fixed seed 42); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-sig-003-evidence]].
- [[mutational-process-classification]] вҖ” Oncology family, thirty-second ONCO-* unit (ONCO-SIG-004): the **aetiology-annotation** layer over the fit [[mutational-signature-fitting-and-extraction]] (which it `depends_on`) вҖ” turn per-signature **exposures** into a set of **active mutational processes** via **normalize вҶ’ cutoff вҶ’ map вҶ’ aggregate**. Normalize to relative contributions `Wбөў = exposureбөў/ОЈexposure` (deconstructSigs "weights between 0 and 1"); drop any `Wбөў < 0.06` (the deconstructSigs `signature.cutoff = 0.06` / `weights[weights < signature.cutoff] <- 0`, **strict `<`** so exactly 0.06 is retained, empirically 1.4% false-negative rate); map each surviving COSMIC label to its **proposed aetiology** (SBS1/5вҶ’**Aging** clock-like, SBS2/13вҶ’**APOBEC**, SBS4вҶ’**Tobacco**, SBS7aвҖ“dвҶ’**UV**, SBS6/15/20/26вҶ’**MMR deficiency**; COSMIC + Alexandrov 2020); **sum** member contributions per process вҶ’ **active-process set** + `argmax` **dominant process**. Worked oracle SBS2/13/1/4 = 50/30/15/5 (ОЈ=100) вҶ’ APOBEC 0.80 (dominant) / Aging 0.15 / Tobacco 0 (SBS4 0.05 below cutoff). Corner cases: surviving mass can sum < 1 (rest "unknown"), several processes reported simultaneously, an unmapped or "Unknown"-aetiology label contributes to no process (SBS5's aetiology is literally "Unknown (clock-like)" yet grouped as Aging), ОЈ=0 вҶ’ no active/dominant process, custom `signature.cutoff` overridable. The interpretation layer answering "**which processes are active?**" one step above ONCO-SIG-002's "how much of each signature?" and ONCO-SIG-003's "how confident?"; orthogonal to the copy-number-scar [[homologous-recombination-deficiency-score]] and mismatch-repair [[microsatellite-instability-detection]] (whose MMR signal SBS6/15/20/26 echo here as a signature-based read), feeds [[cancer-variant-tier-classification-amp-asco-cap]] / [[clinical-actionability-oncokb-levels]]; two source-aligned assumptions (per-process summation, per-signature-cutoff-then-group); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-sig-004-evidence]].
- [[somatic-variant-calling-tumor-normal]] вҖ” Oncology family, thirty-third ONCO-* unit (ONCO-SOMATIC-001): the **foundational somatic SNV caller** at the head of the pipeline вҖ” classify each candidate variant **Somatic / Germline / NotDetected** by comparing **tumor allele frequency `f_t`** against **matched-normal `f_n`** (`VAF = altReads/totalReads`). Strelka's somatic state `S = {(f_t,f_n): f_tвү f_n}` restricted to a **ref/ref normal genotype** (Saunders 2012; the raw somatic probability over-calls in LOH/CN regions) / Strelka2 continuous-VAF somatic-LOD+VAF comparison (Kim 2018). **Three configurable thresholds**: tumor **LoD f_t вүҘ 0.05** (Yan 2021 WES 5% LoD, вүӨ5% frequently sequencing errors вҶ’ NotDetected), normal **"absent" ceiling f_n вүӨ 0.01** (`normalVafThreshold`), f_n above ceiling with substantial f_t вҶ’ **Germline** (Mutect2 germline filter, Benjamin 2019). Bounded monotone **somatic score `max(0, f_t вҲ’ f_n)` вҲҲ [0,1]** (a documented simplification, not a caller LOD). **Tumor-only mode**: no matched normal вҶ’ Mutect2 `в„“_n = 1`, tumor-only call; `FilterGermlineVariants` returns the somatic **subset** of input. Oracles A 0.25/0.00вҶ’Somatic(0.25) В· B 0.48/0.50вҶ’Germline(0) В· C 0.02вҶ’NotDetected В· D CHIP-like 0.30/0.03вҶ’Germline В· E tumor-only 0.20/(0/0)вҶ’Somatic В· boundaries f_t=0.05 present / f_n=0.01 absent. The **upstream caller** whose raw call set the two pre-interpretation QC filters clean вҖ” technical-artifact [[sequencing-artifact-detection]] + biological-origin [[clonal-hematopoiesis-cfdna-filtering]] вҖ” before the clinical-significance units; two flagged source-consistent assumptions (1% normal ceiling parameterized not invented; score a documented simplification); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-somatic-001-evidence]].
- [[chromothripsis-inference]] вҖ” Oncology family, thirty-fourth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-SV-001), and the wiki's **first complex-rearrangement / chromothripsis** method: a **region-level pattern classifier** that consumes a per-segment integer copy-number profile (+ breakpoints / a clustered-SV count) and classifies **Chromothripsis** vs **NotComplex** by the **Korbel & Campbell 2013** six hallmark criteria, computing two directly вҖ” criterion B **oscillating copy-number states** (an oscillation = an adjacent-segment CN-state reversal; profile must alternate between вүӨ3, canonically **two**, states) gated by the Magrangeas-2011 **вүҘ10 first-pass oscillation screen**, the CortГ©s-Ciriano-2020 confidence tiers (**вүҘ7** adjacent oscillating segments high / **4вҖ“6** low / **<4** not-called), the **>60%** two-state fraction, and the **вүҘ6 clustered intrachromosomal SV** burden floor; and criterion A **breakpoint clustering** via the exponential-null coefficient-of-variation flag (**CV>1**, exponential CV=1). Oracles `2,1,2,1,2,1,2,1,2,1,2`вҶ’10 two-stateвҶ’Chromothripsis В· `2,1,2,1,2,1`вҶ’5<10вҶ’NotComplex В· `2,3,4,5,6,7` monotoneвҶ’0 oscillations/>2 statesвҶ’NotComplex (progressive amplification/BFB вҖ” the "clustering necessary but not sufficient" failure mode). **Consumes** the per-segment CN states of [[copy-number-alteration-classification]] (ONCO-CNA-001) вҖ” a pattern classifier over that profile, not a per-segment caller вҖ” orthogonal to the single-junction [[gene-fusion-detection-read-evidence]] and the length-based [[focal-amplification-detection]], distinct from the gene-order [[genome-rearrangement-breakpoint-distance]]. Two operationalisation assumptions (oscillation = CN-state-transition count; clustering = CV>1 vs exponential null); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-sv-001-evidence]].
- [[tumor-mutational-burden]] вҖ” Oncology family, thirty-fifth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-TMB-001): the **tumor-agnostic immunotherapy biomarker** вҖ” the continuous **TMB = (counted somatic mutations) / (sequenced coding region in Mb)** in mut/Mb (Chalmers 2017 Methods; the assay's **coding footprint** is the denominator вҖ” FoundationOne 315-gene = **1.1 Mb**, F1CDx 324-gene вүҲ 0.8 Mb, WES вүҲ 30вҖ“40 Mb, taken as a parameter) and the **TMB-High = TMB вүҘ 10 mut/Mb** classification (FDA pembrolizumab tumor-agnostic approval June 16 2020, F1CDx companion diagnostic, Marcus 2021; boundary **inclusive** вҖ” 10.0 High, 9.9 not; mut/Mb reporting + cutoff cross-confirmed by the Friends of Cancer Research Harmonization Project, Merino 2020). Panel counting **includes synonymous** alterations to reduce sampling noise while WES counts nonsynonymous; germline/driver filtering happens **upstream** вҖ” this unit counts the caller-supplied somatic list of [[somatic-variant-calling-tumor-normal]] (ONCO-SOMATIC-001). Oracles 11/1.1вҶ’10.0 High (315-gene) В· 300/30вҶ’10.0 High (WES) В· 150/10вҶ’15.0 High В· 99/10вҶ’9.9 not-High В· 0вҶ’not-High; corner cases `targetRegionMb=0`вҶ’division-by-zero throws, negative count/region rejected, **<0.5 Mb** panels compute but are known-unstable (documentation, not error), TMB monotone non-decreasing in count / non-increasing in region. An independent immunotherapy biomarker alongside [[microsatellite-instability-detection]] (MSI-H) and correlated with the neoantigen load of [[neoantigen-peptide-generation]], acted on by [[cancer-variant-tier-classification-amp-asco-cap]] / [[clinical-actionability-oncokb-levels]]. **One flagged conflict**: the unsupported registry three-tier "Low <6 / Intermediate 6вҖ“20 / High >20" scheme (no authoritative source for the 6/20 boundaries) resolved to the single source-backed two-tier вүҘ10 cutoff; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-tmb-001-evidence]].
- [[variant-allele-frequency-and-binomial-ci]] вҖ” Oncology family, thirty-sixth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-VAF-001): the **foundational VAF primitive** the VAF-based Oncology family sits on вҖ” three model-free quantities. (1) **Empirical VAF = altReads/totalReads** (= alt AD / sum AD, GATK Mutect2 FAQ; the model-free ratio, **not** Mutect2's model-estimate `AF` field). (2) The **Wilson score binomial confidence interval** on the proportion `center=(pМӮ+zВІ/2n)/(1+zВІ/n)`, `margin=(z/(1+zВІ/n))В·вҲҡ(pМӮ(1вҲ’pМӮ)/n+zВІ/4nВІ)`, **z=1.96** for 95% (Wilson 1927) вҖ” the genuinely distinct statistical content **not represented elsewhere**, chosen over **Wald** because it stays within [0,1] with non-zero width at the extremes (`pМӮ=0`вҶ’lower exactly 0 / `pМӮ=1`вҶ’upper exactly 1) where Wald overshoots/collapses. (3) The CNAqc purity/ploidy correction **`AdjustVAFForPurity`** = `mВ·CCF = VAFВ·(2(1вҲ’ПҖ)+ПҖВ·n_tot)/ПҖ` (inverting CNAqc *Genome Biology* 2024 `v=mПҖ/(2(1вҲ’ПҖ)+ПҖВ·n_tot)`, normal ploidy 2). Oracles 25/100вҶ’0.25 В· 0/10вҶ’0.00 В· 10/10вҶ’1.00, Wilson (25,100)вҶ’0.2592 [0.1755,0.3430] & no-overshoot (0,10)вҶ’[0,0.2775] / (10,10)вҶ’[0.7225,1], correction (0.40,0.80,2)вҶ’1.00 / (0.20,0.50,2)вҶ’0.80 / (0.30,0.50,4)вҶ’1.80; corner cases VAF>1 alignment-artifact/totalReads=0/ПҖ=0 all guarded. The empirical VAF is the same `altReads/totalReads` [[somatic-variant-calling-tumor-normal]] compares and [[ctdna-detection-and-tumor-fraction]] averages; `AdjustVAFForPurity` shares the CNAqc/Tarabichi model [[tumor-purity-from-mutation-vaf]] inverts for ПҖ and [[cancer-cell-fraction-clonal-clustering]] divides by m for CCF; two source-backed assumptions (z=1.96 verbatim, normal CN=2); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-vaf-001-evidence]].
- [[pan-genome-gene-clustering]] вҖ” comparative-genomics pan-genome family anchor (first PANGEN-* unit, PANGEN-CLUSTER-001): greedy incremental homolog/ortholog clustering (`ClusterGenes`) on the CD-HIT model (Li & Godzik 2006) вҖ” process genes longвҶ’short, assign each to the first existing cluster whose representative it matches at вүҘ identity threshold else start a new cluster; global identity = identical aligned positions / alignment length (`-G 1`), Roary default 95% for orthologs (Page 2015); homolog groups only (no gene-neighbourhood/synteny paralog-split step), alignment-free identity may underestimate when internal indels are needed; sibling of [[genome-comparison-core-dispensable]] / [[ortholog-detection-reciprocal-best-hits]] / [[average-nucleotide-identity]]; upstream of [[pan-genome-core-accessory-partition]]; deviations None; record [[pangen-cluster-001-evidence]].
- [[pan-genome-core-accessory-partition]] вҖ” comparative-genomics pan-genome family, second PANGEN-* unit (PANGEN-CORE-001): the **pan-genome partition** `ConstructPanGenome` **downstream** of the clustering step вҖ” split gene clusters across N genomes into **core / accessory / unique** by cluster **occupancy** with the fractional Roary rule `occupancy/N вүҘ coreFraction` ("at least 99% of samples", **not** `floor(coreFractionВ·N)`; hard core >99% / soft core 95вҖ“99% / shell 15вҖ“95% / cloud <15%, Page 2015), compute **genomic fluidity** `ПҶ=[2/(N(NвҲ’1))]В·ОЈ_{k<l}(U_k+U_l)/(M_k+M_l)` вҲҲ[0,1] (Kislyuk 2011; 0 identical / 1 disjoint; 3-genome oracle 10/18=0.5М„), and classify **open вҹә alpha<1 / closed вҹә alpha>1** by the **Heaps'-law** decay exponent (Tettelin 2008, micropan); the N-genome occupancy counterpart of the pairwise-RBH [[genome-comparison-core-dispensable]], both the Tettelin 2005 core/dispensable model; downstream of [[pan-genome-gene-clustering]]; two source-backed assumptions (clustering delegated to k-mer-Jaccard `ClusterGenes`, empty-pair fluidity termвҶ’0); no contradictions; record [[pangen-core-001-evidence]].
- [[pan-genome-heaps-law-fit]] вҖ” comparative-genomics pan-genome family, third PANGEN-* unit (PANGEN-HEAP-001): the **pan-genome growth model** / dedicated **Heaps'-law fitting engine** underneath the partition's open/closed facet вҖ” binarize the gene **presence/absence matrix** (count>0вҶ’1), extract the **new-gene curve** by the micropan first-appearance rule (a cluster is new at genome iвүҘ2 when cumulative presence is 1 at row i and 0 at row iвҲ’1; genome index starts at 2), pool over random orderings (n.perm 100), fit the **power law** `y=KВ·x^(-alpha)` by bounded least squares `J=sqrt(ОЈ(yвҲ’KВ·x^(-alpha))ВІ)/|x|` over KвҲҲ[0,10000]/alphaвҲҲ[0,2] from start `(mean(y at x==2),1)`, classify **open вҹә alpha<1 / closed вҹә alpha>1** (micropan verbatim, boundary not-open); exact oracles x=[2,3] y=[8,4]вҶ’alpha ln2/ln(3/2)вүҲ1.7095 KвүҲ26.164 closed, constant y=[1,1]вҶ’alpha 0 K 1 open, Tettelin 2005 qualitative anchor; the fitting engine whose alpha [[pan-genome-core-accessory-partition]] reports, consuming the families of [[pan-genome-gene-clustering]]; two assumptions (optimizer method non-correctness-affecting, fixed-seed RNG); no contradictions; record [[pangen-heap-001-evidence]].
- [[phylogenetic-marker-selection]] вҖ” comparative-genomics pan-genome family, fourth PANGEN-* unit (PANGEN-MARKER-001): **phylogenetic marker selection** `SelectPhylogeneticMarkers` + the `CountParsimonyInformativeSites` primitive вҖ” from gene clusters across N genomes pick **single-copy core genes** (present **exactly once in every genome**, panX; **core** = "at least 99% of samples", Roary; paralog clusters filtered out) that carry **variable positions**, then **rank by descending parsimony-informative-site count** capped at `maxMarkers`; a **parsimony-informative site** (Zvelebil & Baum 2008) = a column with вүҘ2 states, each in вүҘ2 sequences вҶ’ **monomorphic**/**singleton** columns score 0, a single-copy core cluster with **0 PIS** excluded; the input-selection step **upstream of** core-genome tree building (panXвҶ’FastTree), makes no tree-accuracy claim (recombination caveat); oracles `AAAAA`/`AAACA`/`AACCG`/`ACCTG`вҶ’PIS 2 (cols 3,5), 3-genome selection excludes paralog/not-core/conserved; selects the single-copy subset of [[pan-genome-core-accessory-partition]], consumes families of [[pan-genome-gene-clustering]], single-copy-ortholog constraint shared with [[ortholog-detection-reciprocal-best-hits]]; one assumption (no in-repo aligner вҶ’ PIS over equal-length members, unequalвҶ’PIS 0); no contradictions; record [[pangen-marker-001-evidence]].
- [[phylogenetic-bootstrap-support]] вҖ” the anchor for the **phylogenetics** `PHYLO-*` family (first PHYLO-* unit, PHYLO-BOOT-001): **Felsenstein's bootstrap** (Felsenstein 1985) вҖ” attach a **confidence to each clade** of an inferred tree by **resampling alignment columns (sites) with replacement** into same-length pseudo-alignments (taxa kept, characters resampled), rebuilding a tree per replicate (distance matrix вҶ’ UPGMA/NJ), and scoring each **non-terminal clade of the reference tree** by the **fraction of replicate trees containing a clade with the identical terminal-leaf-name set** (Biopython `get_support`; Lemoine 2018 "proportion of pseudo-trees containing that branch"); binary per-replicate, only reference-tree clades scored, support = `count/replicates`, thresholds 70%/95% descriptive; oracles two-group `AAAAAAAAAA`/`GGGGGGGGGG` UPGMA+JukesCantor seed 42 вҶ’ support{A,B}={C,D}=1.0, all-identical `ACGTACGT`вҶ’all clades 1.0; invariants supportвҲҲ[0,1] / determinism / keys=non-trivial reference clades / null/<2-seq/replicates<1 throw; the **first general distance-based-phylogenetics concept** in the wiki (no NJ/UPGMA/distance-matrix page yet), **distinct from** the CCF-constraint oncology builder [[tumor-phylogeny-clonal-tree-reconstruction]] (no distance matrix, no resampling) and a confidence layer over the tree the marker selector [[phylogenetic-marker-selection]] feeds; two source-consistent assumptions (rooted-clade scoring vs unrooted bipartitions matching Biopython, proportion [0,1] vs percentage Г—100); no contradictions; record [[phylo-boot-001-evidence]].
- [[tree-comparison-metrics]] вҖ” the second phylogenetics `PHYLO-*` unit (PHYLO-COMP-001): **tree comparison** вҖ” three operations on an already-built rooted binary `PhyloNode` tree. **RobinsonвҖ“Foulds distance** (`RobinsonFouldsDistance` = symmetric difference `A+B` of the two trees' canonical split/bipartition sets, Robinson & Foulds 1981; raw count, proper metric, **even**, rooted-clade = Wikipedia dummy-leaf-at-root; **max RF = 2(nвҲ’2) rooted vs 2(nвҲ’3) unrooted**), **MRCA** (`FindMRCA`, deepest common ancestor, O(n) recursive leaf-name match, not-in-treeвҶ’null), **patristic distance** (`PatristicDistance` = `dist(x,MRCA)+dist(y,MRCA)` branch-length sum, not-in-treeвҶ’NaN, zero-branchesвҶ’0); invariants RF identity/symmetric/вүҘ0/even, MRCA symmetric/always-ancestor/unique, patristic PD(x,x)=0/symmetric/вүҘ0; scope rooted-binary-only (two В§7 decisions); the deterministic **compare** counterpart to the resampling-confidence [[phylogenetic-bootstrap-support]] (agreement vs disagreement of the same split primitive, no resampling), distinct from [[tumor-phylogeny-clonal-tree-reconstruction]]; no deviations, no contradictions; record [[phylo-comp-001-evidence]].
- [[evolutionary-distance-matrix]] вҖ” the third phylogenetics `PHYLO-*` unit (PHYLO-DIST-001): the **pairwise evolutionary-distance** primitive emitting the symmetric *nГ—n* matrix distance-based tree building (NJ/UPGMA) consumes вҖ” `CalculatePairwiseDistance`/`CalculateDistanceMatrix` over four methods **Hamming** (raw diff count) / **p-distance** (`differences/comparableSites`, uncorrected) / **JukesвҖ“Cantor JC69** (`-3/4В·ln(1вҲ’4p/3)`, equal-base/equal-rate) / **Kimura-2-parameter K2P** (`-1/2В·ln((1вҲ’2SвҲ’V)В·вҲҡ(1вҲ’2V))`, S=transition/V=transversion); matrix symmetric / zero-diagonal / non-negative / *nГ—n*, correction ordering **JC69вүҘp & K2PвүҘp**, triangle inequality expected-not-guaranteed; **pairwise deletion** (gaps + ambiguous IUPAC N/R/Y skipped, only A,C,G,T compared), case-insensitive; **saturation** JC69вҶ’+вҲһ at pвүҘ3/4 / K2PвҶ’+вҲһ at VвүҘ1/2, all-gap/emptyвҶ’0 (`0/nвҶ’0`), unequal-lengthвҶ’ArgumentException, nullвҶ’ArgumentNullException; oracles `ACGTACGT`/`TCGTACGT`вҶ’Hamming 1/p 0.125/JC69вүҲ0.137, pure-transition `GCGT` K2PвүҲ0.34657 vs pure-transversion `CCGT`вүҲ0.31713, mixedвүҲ0.30679, gapвҶ’7 comparable sites; the **upstream substrate** the family sits on вҖ” [[phylogenetic-bootstrap-support]] resamples + re-runs it per replicate, [[tree-comparison-metrics]] compares the trees it feeds; distinct from the column-selecting [[phylogenetic-marker-selection]] and the distance-matrix-free [[tumor-phylogeny-clonal-tree-reconstruction]]; two API-contract assumptions (empty/all-gapвҶ’0, pairwise deletion); no contradictions; record [[phylo-dist-001-evidence]].
- [[tree-statistics]] вҖ” a phylogenetics `PHYLO-*` unit (PHYLO-STATS-001): **whole-tree descriptive statistics** read off a single rooted binary `PhyloNode` вҖ” `GetLeaves` (terminal nodes, no children; count via `.Count()` = Biopython `count_terminals`), `CalculateTreeLength` (**total tree length = ОЈ all branch lengths**; undefined/default 0 branch вҶ’ 0; the minimum-evolution quantity, Rzhetsky & Nei 1992; Biopython `total_branch_length`/DendroPy `Tree.length()`), `GetTreeDepth` (**tree height = edges on the longest root-to-leaf path**, counts edges not nodes; single-node 0; empty tree вҲ’1); oracles balanced `((A:1,B:1):1,(C:1,D:1):1)`вҶ’4/6/2, caterpillarвҶ’4/5/3, single leafвҶ’1/branch-len/0, null rootвҶ’вҲ…/0/вҲ’1; the **descriptive-summary** sibling of the **compare/query** [[tree-comparison-metrics]] (its ОЈ-all-branches length is the whole-tree analogue of patristic distance's per-path sum), over the same `PhyloNode` [[phylogenetic-bootstrap-support]] resamples and [[evolutionary-distance-matrix]] feeds via UPGMA/NJ; one assumption (null `PhyloNode`вҶ”empty-tree convention); no deviations, no contradictions; record [[phylo-stats-001-evidence]].
- [[distance-based-tree-construction]] вҖ” the phylogenetics `PHYLO-*` **tree-building core** (PHYLO-TREE-001): the step that **consumes an [[evolutionary-distance-matrix]] and emits a `PhyloNode` tree** via two agglomerative methods on `PhylogeneticAnalyzer` (`BuildTree` from sequences / `BuildTreeFromMatrix` from a pre-computed matrix; returns `PhylogeneticTree` Root/Taxa/DistanceMatrix/Method). **UPGMA** (Sokal & Michener 1958) вҖ” rooted **ultrametric**, molecular-clock, nearest-pair merge, arithmetic-mean distance update, **height = d/2**, incremental branch lengths, O(nВі)/O(nВІ). **Neighbor-Joining** (Saitou & Nei 1987) вҖ” **unrooted** (midpoint-rooted final join preserving patristic distances), clock-free, join the **minimum-Q** pair `Q(i,j)=(nвҲ’2)В·d(i,j)вҲ’ОЈd(i,k)вҲ’ОЈd(j,k)`, branch lengths `Оҙ(f,u)=d(f,g)/2+(ОЈd(f,k)вҲ’ОЈd(g,k))/(2(nвҲ’2))`, **correct topology for additive matrices**, **negative branches preserved (no clamping)**, O(nВі); invariants INV-01..05 (all taxa leaves, binary, n leaves / nвҲ’1 internal, UPGMAвүҘ0) + UPGMA ultrametric/rooted/height=d/2 + NJ additive-correct/may-be-negative/no-clock; oracles UPGMA 5S-rRNA вҶ’(a,b)@17вҶ’((a,b),e)@22вҶ’(c,d)@28вҶ’final@33 (root 16.5, all tips 16.5), NJ 5-taxon вҶ’QвӮҒ(a,b)=вҲ’50, Оҙ(a,u)=2вҖҰОҙ(e,w)=1; the **hinge** of the family вҖ” downstream of [[evolutionary-distance-matrix]], wrapped per-replicate by [[phylogenetic-bootstrap-support]], its output compared/queried by [[tree-comparison-metrics]] and summarized by [[tree-statistics]], serialized by Newick ([[phylo-newick-001-evidence]]); distinct from [[tumor-phylogeny-clonal-tree-reconstruction]] (no distance matrix) and [[phylogenetic-marker-selection]] (selects columns, builds no tree); no deviations, no contradictions; record [[phylo-tree-001-evidence]].
- [[bed-format-parsing]] вҖ” FileIO file-parsing `PARSE-*` family anchor (first PARSE-* unit, PARSE-BED-001): UCSC **BED** interval parsing keyed on the **0-based half-open** coordinate model (`chromStart` 0-based / `chromEnd` 1-based-exclusive, length `chromEndвҲ’chromStart`, `chromStart==chromEnd` = zero-length insertion; contrast 1-based GFF/GTF/VCF), the **BED3вҶ’BED12** column ladder (`chrom`/`chromStart`/`chromEnd` + optional `name`/`score`/`strand`/`thick*`/`itemRgb`/`block*`), and the UCSC validation rules (`chromStart вүӨ chromEnd` else null, score clamp [0,1000], strand вҲҲ +/вҲ’/., first-line column-count lock, BED12 first-blockStart-0 / blockCount = array lengths / no-overlap / last-block-reaches-end); the malformed-input target of [[fuzzing]]; deviations None (rules verbatim from UCSC FAQ + Wikipedia); record [[parse-bed-001-evidence]].
- [[phred-quality-encoding]] вҖ” the FASTQ quality-score encoding concept (shared by FileIO parsing + Assembly trimming): Phred score `Q=вҲ’10В·logвӮҒвӮҖ(p)` / `p=10^(вҲ’Q/10)`, the +10-Q=10Г—-fewer-errors ladder (Q20/Q30 QC thresholds), the two live ASCII offsets **Phred+33** (Sanger/Illumina 1.8+, ASCII 33вҖ“126, Q0вҖ“93) vs **Phred+64** (Illumina 1.3вҖ“1.7, ASCII 64вҖ“126, Q0вҖ“62) with boundary chars (`!`=Q0/`I`=Q40/`~`=Q93 vs `@`=Q0/`h`=Q40/`~`=Q62), deterministic per-record offset auto-detection (`<'@'`вҶ’+33, high-bandвҶ’+64, ambiguous `@`вҖ“`I`вҶ’default +33), why a mis-detected offset silently corrupts all downstream Q-stats/trim/filter, and **cross-variant conversion** as a pure Вұ31 re-offset (score invariant; Phred+64вҶ’Phred+33 always safe, Phred+33вҶ’Phred+64 overflows for Q>62); anchored on the primary FASTQ spec **Cock et al. 2010**; traced by [[parse-fastq-001-evidence]] and the dedicated Phred-handling unit [[quality-phred-001-evidence]], reused by [[quality-trimming-running-sum]].
- [[fastq-quality-statistics]] вҖ” the FASTQ **quality-statistics** surface (QUALITY-STATS-001), **distinct from and downstream of** [[phred-quality-encoding]] (which the encoding concept explicitly flags as a separate surface): summary/QC scalars over the **decoded** per-base Phred scores вҖ” **mean** (arithmetic mean of scores, *not* error-probability-averaged), **median** (odd = middle, **even = mean of the two central order statistics**), **min/max**, **population variance/std dev** (`ПғВІ=(1/N)ОЈ(QбөўвҲ’Ој)ВІ`, **Г·N not NвҲ’1** вҖ” the quality string is the complete population), and the **`% вүҘ Q20` / `% вүҘ Q30`** fractions with **inclusive `вүҘ`** thresholds (Illumina: `% вүҘ Q30` the NGS run-quality benchmark); **encoding-independent** (operates on decoded scores, so Phred+64 with the same scores gives identical stats вҖ” **consumes** the decode contract of [[quality-phred-001-evidence]] / [[phred-quality-encoding]]); `CalculateQ30Percentage` == `CalculateStatistics(...).PercentAboveQ30`; oracles `5?I`вҶ’20/30/40 mean 30.0/median 30/var 200/3/ПғвүҲ8.16497/%вүҘQ20 100/%вүҘQ30вүҲ66.67, even `5II?`вҶ’median 35.0, single `I`вҶ’Пғ=0; corner cases even/odd median, single-element Пғ=0, empty/null вҶ’ zeroed `QualityStatistics` (TotalBases=0); record [[quality-stats-001-evidence]].
- [[insdc-feature-location]] вҖ” the shared INSDC (DDBJ/ENA/GenBank) feature-table **location-descriptor** grammar underlying both GenBank and EMBL flat files (same location string, different line syntax): 1-based-inclusive coordinates (contrast BED 0-based), descriptors `n..m`/single `n`/between-bases `n^m`/`<`/`>` partials/`complement`/`join`/`order`/`complement(join(вҖҰ))` with the no-nested-join/order rule, remote refs `accession.version:span`; operator assembly semantics (`join`/`order` concatenate in order, `complement` reverse-complements, `complement(join(a,b))==join(complement(b),complement(a))`), offline-first caller-supplied remote resolver, `<`/`>`-verbatim-slice assumption; oracles `join(1..3,7..9)`/`ACGTACGTAC`вҶ’`ACGGTA`, `complement(Y.1:1..4)`вҶ’`GTTT`; traced jointly by [[parse-genbank-001-evidence]] and [[parse-embl-001-evidence]].
- [[ancestry-estimation-admixture]] вҖ” anchor for the **population-genetics** `POP-*` family (**first POP-\* unit**, POP-ANCESTRY-001): estimate an individual's **ancestry proportions Q** (genome fraction from each of K reference populations) from unlinked SNP genotypes via **supervised/projection ADMIXTURE** вҖ” reference allele frequencies **F fixed/known**, only Q estimated by EM. Alexander, Novembre & Lange 2009 model: genotype gвҲҲ{0,1,2}=allele-1 copy count, **log-likelihood Eq. 2** `L=ОЈбөўОЈвұј{gВ·ln(ОЈ_k qВ·f)+(2вҲ’g)В·ln(ОЈ_k qВ·(1вҲ’f))}` under simplex `ОЈ_k q_ik=1`; **FRAPPE EM Eq. 4** `q^{n+1}=(1/2J)ОЈвұј[gВ·a_ijk+(2вҲ’g)В·b_ijk]` (a/b = posteriors an allele-1/allele-2 copy came from k), EM monotone ascent, convergence Eq. 5 О”L<Оө=10вҒ»вҒҙ, O(IJKВІ); oracles symmetric K=2/J=2 f_A=[0.8,0.2]/f_B=[0.2,0.8] g=[2,0] вҶ’ one EM iter **(0.8,0.2) exactly** вҶ’ converges (1.0,0.0), single-SNP g=2вҶ’(0.9,0.1)/g=1вҶ’(0.5,0.5) uninformative-het/g=0вҶ’(0.1,0.9), identical panels uniform fixed point; INV simplex ОЈ_k q=1 & EM L non-decreasing, missing gвҲү{0,1,2} skipped, empty inputsвҶ’empty; **label non-identifiability** (K! maxima under population relabeling) **pinned by fixed labelled reference panels** (ADMIXTURE manual В§2.10/В§2.14) so Q interpretable relative to supplied labels; scope = estimate-Q-given-fixed-F only (does NOT jointly learn F, run unsupervised block-relaxation, choose K, or model linkage); **distinct from** the tree-building phylogenetics `PHYLO-*` family ([[distance-based-tree-construction]], [[evolutionary-distance-matrix]]) вҖ” a mixture-weight/EM decomposition of one admixed individual, not a tree; two research-grade assumptions (maxIterations budget + Оө convergence; skip-missing); no contradictions; record [[pop-ancestry-001-evidence]].
- [[genetic-diversity-statistics]] вҖ” population-genetics `POP-*` family diversity-statistics unit (**second POP-\* unit**, POP-DIV-001, sibling of the anchor [[ancestry-estimation-admixture]]): four classical within-population variation scalars from an aligned sample (n seqs, length L, S segregating sites) вҖ” **nucleotide diversity ПҖ** = ОЈ_{i<j} d_ij/(C(n,2)В·L) (Nei & Li 1979, mean per-site pairwise differences), **Watterson's Оё_W** = S/a_n with harmonic a_n = ОЈ_{i=1}^{nвҲ’1} 1/i (per-site S/(a_nВ·L); Watterson 1975), **Tajima's D** = (kМӮ вҲ’ S/a_1)/вҲҡ(e_1В·S+e_2В·S(SвҲ’1)) (Tajima 1989 вҖ” normalized ПҖ-vs-Watterson difference; **kМӮ = pairwise-difference COUNT not per-site ПҖ**; DвүҲ0 neutral, D<0 excess rare allelesвҶ’sweep/expansion, D>0 deficitвҶ’balancing/contraction), and **heterozygosity/gene diversity** H_exp = (1/L)ОЈ(1вҲ’ОЈpВІ) with unbiased haploid H_obs = n/(nвҲ’1)В·H_exp вүЎ ПҖ (Nei 1978); Wikipedia oracle n=5/L=20/S=4 вҶ’ kМӮ=2.0/ПҖ=0.1/S/a_1вүҲ1.92/Оё_WвүҲ0.096/**DвүҲ0.273** (TD-C01/TD-C02); guards n<3вҶ’D undefinedвҶ’0, S=0/monomorphicвҶ’all 0, VarвүӨ0вҶ’D=0, `CalculateTajimasD(kМӮ,S,n)` expects kМӮ not ПҖ; **distinct from** the anchor's ancestry-proportion EM (within-population *variation amount* vs *ancestry decomposition*), summary-only (no variant calling / phasing / recombination / Fu-Li / Fay-Wu); all formulae exact-match, no deviations; record [[pop-div-001-evidence]].
- [[allele-genotype-frequencies]] вҖ” **foundational** population-genetics `POP-*` primitive (POP-FREQ-001): turn per-locus **genotype counts** into **allele frequencies**, derive **minor allele frequency (MAF)**, and **filter variants by MAF** вҖ” the numeric substrate under the rest of the POP family (the fixed reference frequencies **F** of [[ancestry-estimation-admixture]] and the per-site `p_i` behind the heterozygosity term of [[genetic-diversity-statistics]] are exactly these quantities). Biallelic allele freq `p = f(AA)+ВҪf(AB)` / `q = f(BB)+ВҪf(AB)` via counts `total=2В·(n_AA+n_AB+n_BB)`, `major=2В·n_AA+n_AB`, `minor=2В·n_BB+n_AB` (**INV `p+q=1`**, `major+minor=total`; oracle 49/42/9 вҶ’ 0.70/0.30); VCF/PLINK dosage `alt_freq = ОЈg/(2n)`, `MAF = min(alt_freq, 1вҲ’alt_freq)` (**INV `0 вүӨ MAF вүӨ 0.5`**, symmetric вҖ” alt_freq 0.7 вҶ’ MAF 0.3; monomorphic вҶ’ 0; 50/50 вҶ’ 0.5); MAF filter = inclusive `[minMAF,maxMAF]` band with conventional HapMap/common(>0.05)-vs-rare(<0.05) thresholds; edge cases zero samplesвҶ’(0,0), empty vectorвҶ’MAF 0, **negative count вҶ’ `ArgumentOutOfRangeException`**; scope = biallelic counting/normalization only (no HWE test, no multiallelic, no phasing/imputation); no deviations/contradictions; record [[pop-freq-001-evidence]].
- [[population-differentiation-fst]] вҖ” population-genetics `POP-*` differentiation unit (POP-FST-001): measure **how differentiated populations are** вҖ” fraction of total variation due to between-population structure вҖ” from per-population allele frequencies (**consumes** [[allele-genotype-frequencies]]; distinct from within-sample [[genetic-diversity-statistics]] and from ancestry decomposition [[ancestry-estimation-admixture]]). **Wright 1965 variance Fst** `Fst = Пғ_SВІ/(pBar(1вҲ’pBar))`, two-pop size-weighted `pBar=(n1В·p1+n2В·p2)/(n1+n2)` / `Пғ_SВІ=(n1(p1вҲ’pBar)ВІ+n2(p2вҲ’pBar)ВІ)/(n1+n2)`, multi-locus **ratio-of-sums** `ОЈПғ_SВІ/ОЈhet` вҖ” the **population parameter from known allele freqs**, explicitly **NOT** the Weir & Cockerham 1984 Оё estimator (no bias correction); **F-statistics** heterozygosity partition `Fis=1вҲ’Hi/Hs`/`Fit=1вҲ’Hi/Ht`/`Fst=1вҲ’Hs/Ht` with **exact** `(1вҲ’Fit)=(1вҲ’Fis)(1вҲ’Fst)`; INV FstвҲҲ[0,1] (0=panmixia/1=fixed differences), FisвҲҲ[вҲ’1,1] (negative under excess heterozygotes), pairwise matrix symmetric + zero diagonal, **not a metric** (fails triangle inequality); oracles fixed p1=1/p2=0вҶ’**1.0 exactly**, pop1=(.9,.8)/pop2=(.1,.2)вҶ’1/2, Cavalli-Sforza/Elhaik ref values, Hartl-Clark bands (0.05/0.15/0.25); edge cases denominator 0 (empty/both-fixed-same/monomorphic)вҶ’**return 0**; scope = Wright Fst + heterozygosity F-statistics only (no significance test, no bootstrap CI); no deviations/contradictions; record [[pop-fst-001-evidence]].
- [[hardy-weinberg-equilibrium-test]] вҖ” population-genetics `POP-*` unit (POP-HW-001): the **Hardy-Weinberg equilibrium chi-square test** вҖ” does a biallelic locus's observed genotype counts match the `pВІ/2pq/qВІ` proportions expected under random mating? **Consumes** genotype counts from [[allele-genotype-frequencies]] (POP-FREQ-001, whose scope explicitly leaves the HWE test here) and turns them into a **hypothesis test**. Estimate `p = (2В·n_AA + n_Aa)/(2n)` / `q = 1вҲ’p`, expected counts `E = {pВІn, 2pqn, qВІn}`, **Pearson ПҮВІ = ОЈ (OвҲ’E)ВІ/E** over the 3 genotype classes, **df = 1** (`#genotypes вҲ’ #alleles = 3 вҲ’ 2`), p-value from chi-square CDF (lower-incomplete-gamma approx), default **Оұ = 0.05** critical value **3.841**; returns `InEquilibrium`/`ChiSquare`/`PValue`. Oracles Ford moth (1469,138,5)вҶ’`pвүҲ0.954`/`ПҮВІвүҲ0.83`вҶ’in-eq, perfect (25,50,25)вҶ’`ПҮВІ=0`, excess-het (10,80,10)вҶ’`ПҮВІ=36 вү« 3.84`вҶ’out-of-eq; edge cases **zero samplesвҶ’InEquilibrium true, PValue 1** (no evidence against HвӮҖ), monomorphicвҶ’`ПҮВІ=0`, **expected-0 term skipped** (div-by-zero guard); deviation causes non-random mating/selection/mutation/migration/drift/**genotyping error**; scope = biallelic chi-square only (no Wigginton 2005 **exact test**, no multiallelic); no deviations/contradictions; record [[pop-hw-001-evidence]].
- [[linkage-disequilibrium]] вҖ” population-genetics `POP-*` unit (POP-LD-001): **non-random association between alleles at two loci** вҖ” a **pairwise inter-locus** quantity distinct from per-locus counting ([[allele-genotype-frequencies]]), within-sample diversity ([[genetic-diversity-statistics]]), between-population differentiation ([[population-differentiation-fst]]), and the single-locus [[hardy-weinberg-equilibrium-test]]; **consumes** allele/haplotype frequencies from [[allele-genotype-frequencies]]. `D = p_AB вҲ’ p_AВ·p_B` (Robbins 1918), normalized `D' = |D|/D_max` clamped [0,1] (Lewontin 1964, sign-branched `D_max`) and `rВІ = DВІ/(p_AВ·q_AВ·p_BВ·q_B)` (Hill & Robertson 1968); implemented **phase-free** via the diploid-frequency result `R_AB=r_AB` (Wright 1933) вҖ” `rВІ` = squared Pearson correlation of 0/1/2 genotype dosage vectors `CovВІ/(VarВ·Var)`, `D` recovered from `Cov_diploid=2D вҮ’ D=Cov/2`; `FindHaplotypeBlocks` = simplified adjacent-pair Gabriel 2002 (consecutive `rВІ вүҘ threshold`, default **0.7**, вүҘ2 variants); INV `0вүӨrВІвүӨ1`/`0вүӨ|D'|вүӨ1`, emptyвҶ’`rВІ=0,D'=0`, monomorphic/zero-varianceвҶ’`rВІ=0` (guarded div), distance+IDs preserved, blocks StartвүӨEnd/вүҘ2/non-overlapping/position-ordered; perfect correlation **and** perfect anti-correlation both вҶ’`rВІ=1`/`D'=1` (sign-blind); scope = two-biallelic-loci rВІ/D' + adjacent-pair blocks only (no full LD matrix, no phasing/EM, no LD-decay fit, no exact Gabriel CI); no deviations/contradictions; record [[pop-ld-001-evidence]].
- [[runs-of-homozygosity-inbreeding]] вҖ” population-genetics `POP-*` unit (POP-ROH-001): detect **long uninterrupted homozygous stretches** (**runs of homozygosity**, `FindROH`) in one individual and summarize their burden as the genomic inbreeding coefficient **F_ROH** вҖ” a **per-individual segment-detection** problem distinct from per-locus counting ([[allele-genotype-frequencies]]), within-sample diversity ([[genetic-diversity-statistics]]), between-population differentiation ([[population-differentiation-fst]]), two-locus [[linkage-disequilibrium]], and single-locus [[hardy-weinberg-equilibrium-test]]. **Window-free consecutive-runs** scan (Marras 2015 / detectRUNS): walk position-sorted 0/1/2 genotypes (1 = heterozygous = "opposite"), grow a run, **terminate** when opposite calls exceed `maxOppRun` (a few tolerated to absorb genotyping error) or an inter-SNP gap exceeds `maxGap` (breaks even an all-homozygous run); retain a stretch only if it passes **both** `minSNP` **and** `minLengthBps` (PLINK `--homozyg-snp 100` **and** `--homozyg-kb 1000`, one alone insufficient). **F_ROH = ОЈL_roh / L_auto** (McQuillan 2008 verbatim; `L_auto` = SNP-covered autosome вүҲ2,674 Mb; r=0.86 vs pedigree; min-length lever вүҘ0.5/1.5/5 Mb, 1.5 Mb best); oracle ОЈL_roh=20 Mb/L_auto=100 Mb вҶ’ **0.20**, whole-genome вҶ’ 1.0; INV each run once/StartвүӨEnd/SnpCount, one tolerated het keeps one run / het beyond splits, gap>maxGap breaks, below minSNP-or-minLength discarded, unsorted ordered internally, genotype 2 = homozygous, leading hets skipped, F_ROHвҲҲ[0,1]; two API-encoding assumptions (0/1/2 encoding; **missing-genotype handling out of scope** вҖ” no missing sentinel, non-`1` treated homozygous); scope = consecutive-runs scan + F_ROH only (no PLINK sliding-window scoring, no missing bounding, no LOD/model-based callers, no cohort ROH-island mapping); no deviations/contradictions; record [[pop-roh-001-evidence]].
- [[selection-scan-ihs-ehh]] вҖ” population-genetics `POP-*` unit (POP-SELECT-001): detect **recent positive selection** from **haplotype structure** вҖ” a selective sweep leaves an unusually long, low-diversity haplotype around the selected allele. A **haplotype-length/decay** statistic distinct from per-locus counting ([[allele-genotype-frequencies]]), within-sample diversity ([[genetic-diversity-statistics]]), between-population differentiation ([[population-differentiation-fst]]), single-locus [[hardy-weinberg-equilibrium-test]], pairwise [[linkage-disequilibrium]], and autozygosity [[runs-of-homozygosity-inbreeding]]; **consumes** derived/ancestral allele freqs from [[allele-genotype-frequencies]]. Pipeline **EHHвҶ’iHHвҶ’iHSвҶ’scan**: `EHH_c=ОЈC(n_h,2)/C(n_c,2)` (Sabeti 2002 / selscan Eq.3, decays 1вҶ’0 with distance), `iHH` = trapezoidal area under EHH both directions truncated at **EHH<0.05**, **unstandardized iHS = ln(iHH_A/iHH_D)** (Voight 2006, ancestral numerator), standardized to std-normal in derived-allele-freq bins, `ScanForSelection` = proportion `|iHS|>2` in ~50-SNP windows; **sign convention critical** вҖ” Voight (A/D) is the opposite of selscan (D/A), large negative iHS вҮ’ long *derived* haplotype, balanced decay вҮ’ iHSвүҲ0; oracles rehh F1205400вҶ’**вҲ’1.978569274**, constructed panel iHH_A=10/iHH_D=40вҶ’ln(0.25)=**вҲ’1.386294361**; INV EHHвҲҲ[0,1] (1 single chromosome / 0 all-distinct), single-element binвҶ’std iHS 0, NвҲ’1 SD + 20 default 0.05 bins (overridable) affect magnitude only, throws on monomorphic core / null / empty / inconsistent length / invalid core allele / OOR coreIndex; scope = single-core iHS/EHH scan (no XP-EHH, no Fst-outlier or Tajima's-D scan, no genetic-map interpolation, no >200 kb gap masking); no deviations/contradictions; record [[pop-select-001-evidence]].
- [[primer-dimer-thermodynamics-tm]] вҖ” PCR primer-design `PRIMER-*` / MolTools family anchor (PRIMER-TM-001): the **self-/hetero-dimer melting temperature (Tm)** of two primers via the Primer3 `ntthal` **thermodynamic alignment** over the SantaLucia & Hicks 2004 unified **DNA nearest-neighbour** model вҖ” the **DNA** counterpart of the **RNA** Turner-2004 folding [[rna-base-pairing]] / [[pre-mirna-hairpin-detection]], distinct by modelling an intermolecular duplex at finite strand concentration. Duplex О”HВ°/О”SВ° = ОЈ 10 Watson-Crick NN stacks + duplex-initiation + per-end terminal-AВ·T-penalty + self-complementary symmetry; **bimolecular Tm** `О”HВ°В·1000/(О”SВ°+RВ·ln(C_T/x))вҲ’273.15` with **symmetry factor x=1 (reverse-complement palindrome) / x=4 (otherwise)**; **[NaвҒә] entropy salt correction** `0.368В·(N/2)В·ln[NaвҒә]` (Tm monotone in salt); the dimer DP finds the possibly-**non-contiguous** most-stable structure (internal mismatch/loop, single/multi-base bulge, `tstack2` terminal overhang), reproducing primer3-py 2.3.0 `calc_homodimer`/`calc_heterodimer` to machine precision (GCGCGCGC self x=1 Tm 40.0906 В°C, TGCATGCATG/CATGCATGCA x=4 Tm 25.6596 В°C, GCGCATGCGC 2Г—2 loop Tm 43.1572 В°C); **no stable dimer** (poly-A) вҶ’ `structure_found=False` вҶ’ null/NaN, invalid input (null / <2 bases / non-ACGT) вҶ’ null/NaN; deviations none remaining after the 2026-06-25 full-ntthal-DP port. Also covers the **intramolecular hairpin self-folding** extension (same engine): stem NN stacks (`NnUnifiedParams`) + **Table 4 hairpin-loop О”GВ°37** (loop О”HВ°=0, О”SВ°=вҲ’О”GВ°37В·1000/310.15) + Jacobson-Stockmayer large-loop, **unimolecular hairpin Tm Eq. 11 with NO concentration term** (Vallone & Benight concentration-independent), bimolecular init & terminal-AВ·T penalty excluded, **bundled** special tri/tetraloop hairpin bonus tables (16 triloop / 76 tetraloop rows, applied in `calc_hairpin`, key incl. closing pair; oracle tetraloop GGGGCGAAAGCCCC Tm 85.0335 В°C) plus the legacy opt-in caller increment (oracle GGGCTTTTGCCC Tm 68.6404 В°C, poly-A вҶ’ null/NaN); Also covers the **per-oligo (single-strand) design Tm** path (Eq. 3 applied to a primer vs its own complement; opt-in NN Tm, legacy Wallace/Marmur-Doty unchanged default) with the **Owczarzy 2004** monovalent-quadratic and **Owczarzy 2008** divalent-MgВІвҒә/dNTP 1/Tm salt corrections (Biopython `salt_correction` methods 5вҖ“7) and the internal-mismatch/dangling-end tables (`NnInternalMismatch`/`NnDanglingEnd`); records [[primer-tm-001-dimer-evidence]], [[primer-tm-001-hairpin-evidence]], [[primer-tm-001-nn-evidence]], [[primer-tm-001-special-loop-evidence]].
- [[primer3-weighted-penalty-objective]] вҖ” PCR primer-design `PRIMER-*` / MolTools family (PRIMER-TM-001, **base** unit): the **Primer3 weighted per-primer penalty / objective function** `p_obj_fn` вҖ” the *only* score Primer3 sorts candidate primers by (**lower is better**), a **selection/scoring** algorithm distinct from the thermodynamic sibling [[primer-dimer-thermodynamics-tm]] (Tm enters only as one input *term*). Weighted sum of **sign-gated one-sided deviations** from each parameter optimum: Tm `temp_gtВ·(TmвҲ’opt_tm)`/`temp_ltВ·(opt_tmвҲ’Tm)`, GC% (percent 0вҖ“100) `gc_content_gt/lt`, size `length_gt/lt`, plus non-thermodynamic `compl_anyВ·self_any + compl_endВ·self_end + num_nsВ·#N`; left/right primers identical (`p_args`). Defaults `opt_tm=60`/`opt_size=20`, weights `temp_*=length_*=1` and `gc/self/num_ns=0` (GC optimum undefined in header) вҮ’ **default objective collapses to `|TmвҲ’60|+|lenвҲ’20|`**; sign-gated (term=0 exactly at optimum), weight-zero short-circuit, penalty вүҘ 0 with **0 iff all-optimal**; `self_any`/`self_end` are caller-supplied Primer3 `dpal` local-alignment scores (arithmetic exact, value external, vanish under default 0 weights); oracles (60,20)вҶ’0.0/(63,20)вҶ’3.0/(57,18)вҶ’5.0/combinedвҶ’8.0; record [[primer-tm-001-evidence]].
- [[taqman-probe-design-rules]] вҖ” **PROBE** family anchor (PROBE-DESIGN-001): the **TaqMan (5'-nuclease hydrolysis-probe) design rules** вҖ” an opt-in extension over the unchanged generic hybridization-probe designer, a distinct MolTools reagent-design algorithm alongside the primer units [[primer-dimer-thermodynamics-tm]] / [[primer3-weighted-penalty-objective]]. The probe-specific hard constraints (no analogue in primer selection): **no G at the 5' end** (a 5'-G quenches the reporter dye *even after cleavage*, so it cannot be rescued вҖ” hard rule; `SelectTaqManStrand` moves the design to the complement/antisense strand when a compliant sense probe is impossible), **more Cs than Gs**, **no run of вүҘ4 consecutive Gs** (flagged separately from the generic homopolymer cap), **G+C 30вҖ“80%**, **length 18вҖ“22 nt** (default, `minLength`/`maxLength` parameterised вҖ” ABI/PREMIER 18вҖ“22 vs IDT/Thermo up to 30), and the **probe Tm вүҘ primer Tm + 10 В°C** gate (so the probe binds before Taq reaches it) with the primer Tm caller-supplied and the probe Tm via the PRIMER-TM-001-validated salt-adjusted `81.5+16.6В·logвӮҒвӮҖ[NaвҒә]+41В·GCвҲ’600/N` formula (not a TaqMan-specific nearest-neighbour calc); a `NoGuanineAt5Prime`/`PassesAll`-style checker; oracles CCATCACCCTACATCACC passes-all (primerTm вүӨ 39.35), 5'-G/GGGG-run/more-G-than-C/len<18/GC-100% each fail, sense GTTAGGGTTAGGGTTAGG вҶ’ RC CCTAACCCTAACCCTAAC strand selection; two parameterisation assumptions (18вҖ“22 default window, repository salt-adjusted Tm engine), no source contradictions; record [[probe-design-001-evidence]].
- [[probe-offtarget-specificity-scan]] вҖ” **PROBE** family (PROBE-VALID-001): the **hybridization-probe off-target specificity scan** вҖ” align a candidate probe against a pooled reference with a **gapped SmithвҖ“Waterman local alignment** and report every site whose identity clears a threshold. The **specificity-checking sibling** of [[taqman-probe-design-rules]] (composition rules), a genuinely distinct algorithm. Core improvement over the earlier **ungapped Hamming scan**: SW's gap-length maxima + **zero floor** (Smith & Waterman 1981) make it *local* and **indel-aware**, so an off-target reachable only through an insertion/deletion (which frame-shifts every downstream base and hides from a fixed window) is found вҖ” the **gapped-vs-ungapped BLAST** improvement (Altschul 1990вҶ’1997), realized as an *exact* full SW scan (not seed-and-extend). Zero-floor traceback **trims a mismatched tail** so identity is over the matched core. Off-target call at **вүҘ0.75 identity** (Kane et al. 2000 microarray cross-hyb threshold; `minIdentity` caller-configurable). On/off labelling (assumption): the first perfect ungapped full-coverage exact match = intended on-target, all else off-target. Opt-in **KarlinвҖ“Altschul** significance (`ComputeLambdaNucleotide`/`ComputeKarlinAltschul`): `E=KВ·mВ·nВ·e^(вҲ’О»S)`, О» = root of `ОЈ p_i p_j e^(О» s_ij)=1`, bit `S'=(О»SвҲ’ln K)/ln 2`, `E=mВ·nВ·2^(вҲ’S')`, preconditions expected-score<0 + a positive score, K caller-supplied; +1/вҲ’3 uniform-0.25 вҶ’ О»=1.3740631 (вүҲ blastn 1.37), example bit 59.9627 / E 1.7802eвҲ’14. Oracles: exact + indel `ACGTAC-GTACGT` 12/12=1.0 (gapped finds, ungapped misses), indel+mismatch trimmed to 10/12=0.8333 (in @0.75, out @0.90); BLAST DNA scoring +2/вҲ’3 gap вҲ’2. No source contradictions; record [[probe-valid-001-evidence]].
- [[sequence-complexity-compression-lempel-ziv]] вҖ” compression-based member of the sequence complexity/entropy family (SEQ-COMPLEX-COMPRESS-001): **LempelвҖ“Ziv (LZ76) complexity** `c(S)` = number of distinct phrases in a left-to-right exhaustive-history parse, length-normalized as `c/(n/log_b n)` (b<2 clamps log base to 2, returns the normalized value). A **distinct scalar measure** from the composition Shannon-entropy [[protein-low-complexity-seg]], the fixed-k [[k-mer-statistics]] k-entropy, and the explicit-repeat [[repetitive-element-detection]] вҖ” LZ is low exactly where those low-complexity/repeat tracts are. Records [[seq-complex-compress-001-evidence]].
- [[dust-low-complexity-score]] вҖ” triplet-frequency member of the sequence complexity/entropy family and the DNA-sequence low-complexity **masker** (SEQ-COMPLEX-DUST-001): the **DUST** score `score = вҲ‘_t c(cвҲ’1)/2 / (LвҲ’2)` over nucleotide triplet counts (Morgulis et al. 2006, `k=3` hardcoded), where a **HIGH score вҮ’ LOW complexity**; default window 64 / mask threshold 2.0 (level 20); a **distinct scalar measure** from the compression [[sequence-complexity-compression-lempel-ziv]], the fixed-k [[k-mer-statistics]] k-entropy, the protein [[protein-low-complexity-seg]] (opposite direction вҖ” Shannon entropy, low вҮ’ low complexity), and the explicit-repeat [[repetitive-element-detection]]. Oracles `ATGC`вҶ’0.0 / `ACGTACGT`вҶ’0.333вҖҰ / `AAAAAA`вҶ’1.5 / `AAAAAAAAAA`вҶ’3.5; homopolymer max `(LвҲ’3)/2`. Records [[seq-complex-dust-001-evidence]].
- [[windowed-sequence-complexity-profile]] вҖ” the **profiling / scanning** member of the sequence complexity/entropy family (SEQ-COMPLEX-WINDOW-001): a **sliding-window** scan that emits a per-position `ComplexityPoint` *profile*, each window carrying a **Shannon entropy** of base composition (`H = вҲ’ОЈ p logвӮӮ p`, uniform вҮ’ 2.0, homopolymer вҮ’ 0) **and** a **linguistic complexity** `LC = ОЈ Vбөў / ОЈ Vmax,i` (`Vmax,i = min(4^i, NвҲ’i+1)`, `maxWordLength = min(6, w)`; Gabrielian & Bolshoy 1999 / Troyanskaya 2002). The family's **only profile** and its first home of linguistic complexity вҖ” distinct from the whole-sequence scalars [[sequence-complexity-compression-lempel-ziv]] / [[dust-low-complexity-score]] / [[k-mer-statistics]] k-entropy, and the DNA profiling analogue of the protein [[protein-low-complexity-seg]]. Window count `floor((LвҲ’w)/s)+1` (LвүҘw else 0), only fully-contained windows emitted, Position = `WindowStart + w/2`; oracles `ACGTACGT`вҶ’2.0 / 23-29ths, poly-AвҶ’0.0 / 6-29ths, L=24/w=8/s=8вҶ’3 windows. Records [[seq-complex-window-001-evidence]]. Also hosts the **second entry point** for the same per-window Shannon scan: the standalone **Shannon entropy profile** SEQ-ENTROPY-PROFILE-001 (entropy channel only, no linguistic complexity; record [[seq-entropy-profile-001-evidence]]).
- [[restriction-enzyme-filtering]] вҖ” **RESTR** family anchor (RESTR-FILTER-001): filtering/selecting a restriction-enzyme **library** by properties of the cut (not searching a sequence for cut sites) вҖ” a MolTools reagent-selection algorithm alongside [[codon-optimization]] and the primer/probe units. Two filter axes: (1) **end type** вҖ” every Type II end is either **blunt** (center cut, both strands terminate in a base pair) or **sticky** (staggered cut, 5'/3' overhang), a **total, disjoint partition** (`GetBluntCutters()` вҲӘ `GetStickyCutters()` = full library, no third category, blunt-blunt always compatible); (2) **recognition-site length** вҖ” `GetEnzymesByCutLength(min, max)` over the **inclusive** `[min,max]` interval, undivided Type II sites canonically **4вҖ“8 nt**. Blunt: SmaI/EcoRV/AluI/HaeIII; sticky: EcoRI(5')/KpnI(3')/PstI(3')/NotI/TaqI. Invariants: partition totality+disjointness; inclusive bounds (API-shape assumption); single-length overload == range at `min==max`; `min>max`/negative/zeroвҶ’empty; the **interrupted palindrome** SfiI (`GGCCNNNN^NGGCC`, 13 nt) is sticky but correctly **excluded** by `[4,8]` (undivided sites only). Sources Wikipedia sticky/blunt + restriction enzyme + cutting-site list + NEB/REBASE + PMC; record [[restr-filter-001-evidence]].
- [[crispr-guide-rna-design]] вҖ” **MolTools / CrisprDesigner** family (CRISPR-PAM-001 + CRISPR-GUIDE-001 + CRISPR-OFF-001): CRISPR **guide RNA (gRNA/sgRNA) design, on-target efficacy, and off-target scoring**, a distinct reagent-design algorithm alongside the primer units [[primer-dimer-thermodynamics-tm]] / [[primer3-weighted-penalty-objective]] and probe units [[taqman-probe-design-rules]] / [[probe-offtarget-specificity-scan]]. **Layer 0 вҖ” PAM site detection** (CRISPR-PAM-001, `FindPamSites`/`GetSystem`): the geometric front end resolving 7 systems' PAM/orientation/guide-len (SpCas9 `NGG`/3вҖІ/20, SaCas9 `NNGRRT`/21, Cas12a `TTTV`/5вҖІ/23, CasX `TTCN`/20, вҖҰ) and scanning **both strands** (forward `CCN` = revcomp reverse `NGG`), 0-based `Position` always forward-strand; validated [[crispr-pam-001-report]] (PASS/PASS-WITH-NOTES CLEAN, 58/58). Then **three separated layers:** (1) a **composition heuristic** `DesignGuideRnas`/`EvaluateGuideRna` вҖ” extract PAM-adjacent candidates, score from base 100 with GC (40вҖ“70), poly-T `TTTT` (вҲ’20), self-complementarity (>0.3), seed-GC (30вҖ“80% over the 10 nt PAM-proximal window) and common-restriction-site deductions, clamp вүҘ0, keep `Score вүҘ MinScore` (50) вҖ” that **ranks/filters**, it is not a learned activity model (`AvoidPolyT`/`CheckSelfComplementarity` flags are stored but not honored; some non-SpCas9 systems reuse SpCas9 metadata вҖ” by-design); (2) **experimentally-calibrated on-target efficacy** вҖ” **Doench-2014 Rule Set 1** `CalculateOnTargetDoench2014`, a logistic linear model over a **30-nt context 4+20+3+3** (intercept 0.59763615, GC term over `seq[4..24)`, 70-entry table, sigmoid Г—100; NGG PAM guard), byte-identical to the CRISPOR reference; and **Doench-2016 Rule Set 2 / Azimuth** `CalculateOnTargetRuleSet2`, an sklearn-free GBRT from embedded Azimuth pickles with externally-derived oracles; and (3) **off-target risk scoring** (CRISPR-OFF-001) вҖ” the **MIT/Hsu-Zhang 2013** specificity `CalculateMitHitScore` (20-element `W` = CRISPOR `hitScoreM`, `О (1вҲ’W[i])В·score2В·score3В·100`; seed = PAM-proximal) + aggregate `CalculateMitSpecificityScore`, and the **CFD (Doench 2016)** `CalculateCfdScore` вҲҲ [0,1] (240+16-entry matrices, 240/240+16/16 identical across CRISPOR + iGWOS). On-target [[crispr-guide-001-report]] (PASS/PASS CLEAN, 54/54) + off-target [[crispr-off-001-report]] (PASS/PASS CLEAN, 71/71). Research-grade, not clinical.
- [[splice-acceptor-site-prediction]] вҖ” **splicing** family anchor (SPLICE-ACCEPTOR-001): **3' splice site / acceptor** detection вҖ” score candidate `AG` dinucleotides for the three cis-elements of a real 3'ss under the canonical **GU-AG rule**: (1) the **branch point** (`yUnAy` adenosine ~18вҖ“50 nt upstream), (2) the **polypyrimidine tract** (C/U-rich, U2AF65), (3) the **AG + context** (`(Yn)NYAG|G`). Three scoring surfaces вҖ” default **PWM+PPT** `FindAcceptorSites`, opt-in **branch-point** `FindAcceptorBranchPoint` (Gao 2008 `yUnAy`), opt-in **MaxEntScan score3ss** `ScoreAcceptorMaxEnt` (Yeo & Burge 2004, canonical 2.89 cross-check) вҖ” plus U12 **YCCAC** non-canonical scoring. The PWM branch is a worked biological instance of the position-weight-matrix motif family (cf. [[known-motif-search]] / [[regulatory-element-detection]]). Record [[splice-acceptor-001-evidence]].
- [[splice-donor-site-prediction]] вҖ” **splicing** family, **donor / 5' splice site** (SPLICE-DONOR-001), the 5' partner of [[splice-acceptor-site-prediction]]: score candidate `GT/GU` dinucleotides for the almost-invariant `GU` intron start under the **GU-AG rule** against a single contiguous **`MAG|GURAGU`** consensus (positions вҲ’3..+6; 0-G/+1-U ~100%, вҲ’1-G ~80% for U1 snRNP base-pairing). Unlike the acceptor there is **no branch point / polypyrimidine tract** вҖ” two scoring surfaces only: default **IUPAC consensus match-fraction** `FindDonorSites`/`ScoreDonorSite` (plainer than the acceptor's PWM+PPT; GC donors self-penalize via the +1-U mismatch, 8/9 vs 9/9) and opt-in **MaxEntScan score5ss** `ScoreDonorMaxEnt` (Yeo & Burge 2004 9-nt window, single 16,384-entry table with no overlapping sub-windows вҖ” the contrast with score3ss; canonical `cagGTAAGT`вҶ’**10.86**). GC-AG + U12 **AT-AC**/`ATATCC` non-canonical donors; the `MAG|GURAGU` consensus is an [[iupac-degenerate-consensus|IUPAC-degenerate]] / [[consensus-sequence|consensus]] motif (cf. [[known-motif-search]]). Record [[splice-donor-001-evidence]].
- [[breakpoint-detection-split-reads]] вҖ” **germline structural-variant (SV)** family anchor (SV-BREAKPOINT-001): **breakpoint detection from split (soft-clipped) reads** вҖ” localize an SV breakpoint to a single base at the aligned/clipped **junction** of a split read (SAM/BAM CIGAR **soft clip `S` consumes the read but not the reference**, sits only at a read end вҶ’ **leading `S` = left / trailing `S` = right breakpoint**; a no-`S` read carries no signal), then **cluster** per-read junctions into a supported call under **positional tolerance** (ClipCrop 5 b), **minimum support** (SoftSearch вүҘ x clipped reads, default 5 / configurable 2), and **same clip-side + same chromosome**, with a **min clip length** filter (вүӨ 5 clipped bases dropped) and a `RefineBreakpoint` region-consensus method. `SplitRead` record stores the junction directly (`PrimaryPosition`/`SupplementaryPosition`/`ClipLength`). One ASSUMPTION (cluster coordinate = rounded mean of member junctions, sub-tolerance only). The germline-SV anchor orthogonal to the oncology read-evidence [[gene-fusion-detection-read-evidence]] / [[chromothripsis-inference]] and distinct from the gene-order [[genome-rearrangement-breakpoint-distance]]; research-grade, not for clinical use. Record [[sv-breakpoint-001-evidence]].
- [[read-depth-cnv-segmentation]] вҖ” **germline structural-variant (SV)** family, **read-depth** member (SV-CNV-001): **read-depth CNV detection** вҖ” call copy-number deletions/duplications from **read depth of coverage** (distinct method from the split-read anchor [[breakpoint-detection-split-reads]]; aggregate depth, not per-read junctions). **read depth вҲқ copy number** (Yoon 2009) вҶ’ **windowed counting** (non-overlapping fixed-size windows, one read per start, per-window mean RD) вҶ’ optional **GC correction** `r_i'=r_iВ·m/m_GC` вҶ’ **log2 ratio** `log2(observed/reference depth)` (reference = overall median of window means, default self-reference) вҶ’ **integer CN = round(2В·2^log2)** (CNVkit "round", diploid ploidy 2) вҶ’ del/dup call + segment merge (`DetectCNV`/`SegmentCopyNumber`). Anchors (verbatim CNVkit): log2(1/2)=вҲ’1вҶ’CN 1 (loss), log2(2/2)=0вҶ’CN 2 (Neutral), log2(3/2)=+0.585вҶ’CN 3 (gain), log2(2.0)=+1вҶ’CN 4 (amp); CN strictly increasing in log2, clamped **вүҘ 0**. Corner cases: **zero-depth window вҶ’ no-call** (log2(0) undefined), **NaN вҶ’ Neutral**. Two ASSUMPTIONs (reference = overall median of non-zero window means; diploid ploidy 2), both source-supported. Consumes **windowed depth** (cf. exact per-base [[coverage-depth-calculation]]), not raw BAM. The oncology [[copy-number-alteration-classification]] is the discrete-state classification layer built on this same log2 ratio; [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]] adds BAF/purity вҖ” this germline unit is total-CN-from-depth only. Sources Yoon 2009 + CNVkit `call.py`/docs; research-grade, not for clinical use. Record [[sv-cnv-001-evidence]].
- [[discordant-pair-sv-detection]] вҖ” **germline structural-variant (SV)** family, **discordant-read-pair / paired-end-mapping (PEM)** member (SV-DETECT-001): **SV detection from PEM signatures** вҖ” read how a mate pair's mapped **span + orientation** deviate from the concordant **FR** proper pair (SAM FLAG 0x02; RF everted/discordant) and classify the SV type. A third read-evidence channel, orthogonal to the split-read anchor [[breakpoint-detection-split-reads]] (within-read clip junction вҶ’ single-base breakpoint) and the depth-based [[read-depth-cnv-segmentation]] (aggregate dosage); integrated callers (DELLY) combine PEM + split reads. Signatures (same chr unless noted): span `> Ој+cВ·Пғ` FR вҶ’ **Deletion**, span `< ОјвҲ’cВ·Пғ` вҶ’ **Insertion**, **FF/RR** вҶ’ **Inversion**, everted **RF** вҶ’ **tandem Duplication**, different chromosome вҶ’ **Translocation**. Span cutoff `c` s.d. of the empirical insert-size distribution (BreakDancer `-c`, default 3); **signature-then-cluster** with **min support** вүҘ `-r` (default 2). One ASSUMPTION вҖ” inter-chromosomal (translocation) precedence over orientation. Corner cases: insertion > insert size invisible + sequence unrecoverable by span (split-read's job), below-support clusters dropped, exact cutoff bounds. Sources Medvedev 2009 + BreakDancer (Chen 2009 / Fan 2014) + SAM/BWA proper-pair + DELLY/SVXplorer; research-grade, not for clinical use. Record [[sv-detect-001-evidence]].
