- [[differential-expression]] вҖ” anchor for the **Transcriptome / RNA-seq** family (first ingested unit, TRANS-DIFF-001): **two-group differential expression** `TranscriptomeAnalyzer.CalculateFoldChange` / `FindDifferentiallyExpressed`. **log2 fold change** `log2((mean(treatment)+c)/(mean(control)+c))` (pseudocount c=1, positive = up in treatment/condition 2) + **Welch unequal-variance two-sample t-test** raw p (unbiased (NвҲ’1) variances, Welch-Satterthwaite df, exact Student-t tail `p=I_{ОҪ/(ОҪ+tВІ)}(ОҪ/2,ВҪ)` via regularized incomplete beta) + **Benjamini-Hochberg FDR** reproducing R `p.adjust(method="BH")`. DE вҮ” **two-criterion gate** `|log2FC| вүҘ threshold (default 1.0) AND adjusted p < alpha (default 0.05)`; fail either вҮ’ not significant. Edge cases: <2 replicates вҶ’ p=1, se=0 вҶ’ p=1/0, zero mean вҶ’ pseudocount; adjusted p вҲҲ [raw p, 1]. A **simple two-group** estimator, **not** the DESeq2 negative-binomial GLM. Sources DESeq2 (Love 2014, log2FC/BH) + Science Park lesson + Welch 1947 + Student-t CDF + BH 1995. `alternative_to` the non-parametric rank-sum [[significant-taxa-detection]] (which applies no built-in FDR); structurally akin to the Fisher's-exact [[differentially-methylated-regions]] gate; distinct from the single-sample z-score [[expression-outlier-zscore-signature-score]]; DE gene lists feed [[pathway-enrichment-ora]]. Research-grade, not for clinical use. Record [[trans-diff-001-evidence]].
- [[expression-quantification]] вҖ” **Transcriptome / RNA-seq** family, **quantification / normalization** unit (TRANS-EXPR-001): convert raw RNA-seq **counts вҶ’ comparable expression** with `TranscriptomeAnalyzer.CalculateTPM` / `CalculateFPKM` / `QuantileNormalize`. **TPM** `(X_i/l_i)/ОЈ(X_j/l_j)В·10вҒ¶` вҖ” divide by length into RPK **then** rescale so each sample **sums to exactly 10вҒ¶** (the sum-to-a-million invariant RPKM lacks; average TPM = 10вҒ¶/#transcripts = const; Wagner 2012, Zhao/Ye/Stanton 2020). **FPKM/RPKM** `X_iВ·10вҒ№/(l_iВ·N)` вҖ” per-kilobase + per-million-mapped-reads; RPKM (single-end) вүЎ FPKM (paired) formula; `TPM = FPKM/ОЈ FPKMВ·10вҒ¶` so FPKM does **not** sum to a constant. **Quantile normalization** (Bolstad 2003) вҖ” match all samples to one shared distribution with no reference: sort each column, set each rank to the cross-column rank mean, re-place; **ties get the mean of the rank means they span**. Oracles: TPM A(10,2000)/B(20,4000)/C(30,1000) вҶ’ (125000,125000,750000)/ОЈ=10вҒ¶; FPKM X=1000,l=2000,N=10вҒ¶ вҶ’ 500; quantile C2 tied `4`s вҶ’ 5.166вҖҰ. Edge cases: all-zero counts вҶ’ TPM 0/0 вҶ’ emit 0; non-positive length/N вҶ’ FPKM 0; empty вҶ’ empty. Two source-backed ASSUMPTIONs (all-zero TPM вҶ’ 0; effective length = annotated length). The within-sample (TPM/FPKM) + cross-sample (quantile) normalization **upstream** of the family anchor [[differential-expression]]; TPM/RPKM are within-sample relative measures, misused across samples (Zhao 2020). Classic count-normalization, not kallisto/salmon effective-length or edgeR/DESeq2 size factors. Research-grade, not for clinical use. Record [[trans-expr-001-evidence]].
- [[alternative-splicing-psi]] вҖ” **Transcriptome / RNA-seq** family, **alternative / differential splicing** unit (TRANS-SPLICE-001): quantify how a gene's exons are spliced from RNA-seq reads with `TranscriptomeAnalyzer.CalculatePSI` / `DetectAlternativeSplicing`. **Percent-Spliced-In** `ОЁ = I/(I+S)` (inclusion vs exclusion read support; Wang 2008, PMC3330053, SUPPA2) with opt-in **rMATS length-normalized** `ПҲМӮ = (I/lбөў)/(I/lбөў + S/lвӮӣ)` (Shen 2014); **О”PSI** = splicing-level differential readout. Classifies an event between **two isoforms of one gene** into the **five canonical AS classes** (Wang 2008 = rMATS SE/RI/A5SS/A3SS/MXE): SkippedExon, RetainedIntron, AlternativeFivePrimeSS (alternative **donor**), AlternativeThreePrimeSS (alternative **acceptor**), MutuallyExclusiveExons. Oracles: (80,20)вҶ’0.80, (80,20,200,100)вҶ’0.6666вҖҰ. Edge cases: 0/0вҶ’NaN, S=0вҶ’1, I=0вҶ’0, `0вүӨPSIвүӨ1`, <2 isoforms вҶ’ no event. The **splicing-level counterpart** to the gene-level anchor [[differential-expression]] (a gene can be differentially spliced without changing total expression); self-normalizing ratio, so unlike [[expression-quantification]] it needs no TPM/library correction. **Distinct from** the genomic splice-site *motif* predictors [[splice-donor-site-prediction]] / [[splice-acceptor-site-prediction]] / [[gene-structure-prediction-intron-exon]] (which score `GT`/`AG` sequence signals) вҖ” cross-linked only to disambiguate. Two source-backed ASSUMPTIONs (length normalization opt-in; forward strand). Read-count ratio, **not** the full rMATS/SUPPA2 replicate statistics. Research-grade, not for clinical use. Record [[trans-splice-001-evidence]].
- [[gene-structure-prediction-intron-exon]] вҖ” **splicing** family **composite / umbrella** (SPLICE-PREDICT-001): **gene structure prediction (intron/exon)** вҖ” the integrative unit that **consumes** [[splice-donor-site-prediction]] + [[splice-acceptor-site-prediction]] and adds what neither boundary unit produces: **pairs** each `GT/GU` donor with an `AG` acceptor into an **intron** under the GT-AG rule (bounded by `minIntronLength` default 60 / `maxIntronLength`, **greedy non-overlapping** selection), then builds the whole model вҖ” **exons** = the gaps, each **typed** Initial/Internal/Terminal/Single and carrying a reading-frame **phase** = `(ОЈ preceding exon lengths) mod 3`, the **spliced (mature) sequence** (introns removed), and an **overall score** = mean of per-intron `(donor.Score+acceptor.Score)/2` in [0,1]. U2 (GT-AG) / GC-AG / U12 (AT-AC) intron types; single-exon (intronless) genes вҶ’ 1 Single exon; empty вҶ’ empty structure. Sources Breathnach & Chambon 1981 + Shapiro & Senapathy 1987 + Burge 1999 + Wikipedia Intron/Exon/Gene-structure; all 4 assumptions RESOLVED (default branch-point 0.3 constant removed). Record [[splice-predict-001-evidence]].
- [[variant-effect-annotation-vep]] вҖ” the **interpretation / annotation** member of the variant-analysis family (VARIANT-ANNOT-001): **VEP-style variant effect annotation** вҖ” map an already-**called** variant to its **functional consequence** + **Sequence-Ontology term/accession** + **IMPACT** (HIGH/MODERATE/LOW/MODIFIER) via the Ensembl **OverlapConsequence predicate system**. **IMPACT is a stored property of the term, not computed**; **most-severe selection returns the lowest-rank term**. The coding engine **`depends_on`** [[genetic-code-translation]] вҖ” **translates the ref/alt codons** (NCBI Standard code table 1) and compares peptides: `synonymous` / `missense` / `stop_gained` / `stop_lost` from `ref_pep` vs `alt_pep`, **`frameshift` purely length-based `|altвҲ’ref| mod 3 вү  0`**, inframe ins/del = Г—3 indel; precedence stop_gained>missense, start_lost(rank 7)>coding-substitution. Downstream of variant calling [[somatic-variant-calling-tumor-normal]], orthogonal to pathogenicity/tier classification. Sources McLaren 2016 (VEP) + Ensembl Constants.pm/VariationEffect.pm + NCBI gc.prt + Sequence Ontology. Two assumptions (Standard code table 1 only; single-codon SNV comparison, no NMD). Research-grade, not for clinical use. Record [[variant-annot-001-evidence]].
- [[germline-variant-calling-snp-indel]] вҖ” the **calling / detection** member of the variant-analysis family (VARIANT-CALL-001): **variant calling** вҖ” detect **SNP / insertion / deletion** (Danecek 2011: a variant is a difference from reference) by aligning a query to a reference (`CallVariantsFromAlignment` вҶ’ `SequenceAligner.GlobalAlign`) and reading out differing columns, then classify each SNP **Transition** (AвҶ”G, CвҶ”T) vs **Transversion** (AвҶ”C/AвҶ”T/GвҶ”C/GвҶ”T) and report **Ti/Tv** (undefined `#Tv=0`вҶ’0). In-memory `Variant` uses a `"-"` gap sentinel + 0-based position; VCF **padding base + 1-based POS** apply only to serialized `ToVcfLines`. **Upstream of** annotation [[variant-effect-annotation-vep]] (calling produces what VEP interprets); **`alternative_to`** the oncology tumor-vs-normal caller [[somatic-variant-calling-tumor-normal]] (same goal, different evidence). Assumptions: indels **not** left-aligned/parsimony-normalized (Tan 2015 вҖ” position-only implementation-dependence in repeats), gap-sentinel internal rep, Ti/Tv zeroвҶ’0. Alignment-based single-query comparison, **not** a read-pileup genotype caller. Sources VCFv4.3 + Danecek 2011 + Tan 2015 + Collins & Jukes 1994 + Acharya 2017 (Hamming). Research-grade, not for clinical use. Records [[variant-call-001-evidence]] + [[variant-snp-001-evidence]] (SNP facet: `FindSnps`/`FindSnpsDirect`, Hamming-mismatch enumeration, equal-length/common-prefix precondition) + [[variant-indel-001-evidence]] (indel facet: `FindInsertions`/`FindDeletions`, directional length invariant, Tan 2015 normalization theory).

## Gotchas

- [[research-grade-limitations]] вҖ” beta, not for clinical use; simplified-subset implementations; internal-only validation.
